# 忧郁的热带 - Tristes Tropiques

- 8TH-24 独角戏 / Monologues

## 8TH-01 此即正义 / Unshakable Justice

**洛佩拉**：懦夫……逃兵……叛徒！\
**Lopera**: Cowards, mutineers, traitors!

**洛佩拉**：这是你们的选择，你们的代价。\
**Lopera**: You've made your choices; now you'll learn the consequences.

**洛佩拉**：芝诺绝不容忍！\
**Lopera**: Zeno never forgives!

**洛佩拉**：行刑队！抬枪！预备——\
**Lopera**: Attention! Ready, aim—

**洛佩拉**：射击！\
**Lopera**: Fire!

**伊戈尔将军**：很抱歉让你看到这一幕。\
**Admiral Igor**: A shame you had to see all that.

**伊戈尔将军**：洛佩拉枪法很准，不过，把枪口对准曾经的同袍兄弟，对芝诺军人来说是种耻辱。\
**Admiral Igor**: Our Second Lieutenant Lopera is a crack shot. I trained her to be nothing less. Yet, no soldier of Zeno would take pride in an execution.

**伊戈尔将军**：这是我的失职。\
**Admiral Igor**: The burden falls on me. This was my fault, my negligence.

顺着洛佩拉的枪口所指，士兵们倒在了荒草与尘埃中。\
The soldiers collapse, their limp bodies falling among the weeds.

鲜血漫出。\
Their blood stains the soil.

**伊戈尔将军**：洛佩拉抓回了叛徒。\
**Admiral Igor**: She hunted down these traitors herself.

**洛佩拉**：法医核验。\
**Lopera**: M.E., check the bodies.

**洛佩拉**：其余人，收队！\
**Lopera**: The rest of you, form up!

硝烟过后，士兵列队离开。军医登场，一一查验死者。\
The soldiers leave in formation amid the clearing smoke as the medics arrive to examine the deceased one by one.

行刑者将步枪交给侍从，摘下手套，转身面向圣保罗灼目的烈日与廊柱阴影下的伊戈尔将军。\
Lopera hands the rifle to the attendant, removes her gloves, and turns to face Admiral Igor. He stands in the shaded colonnade, away from the blazing sun of São Paulo.

**洛佩拉**：行刑完毕，将军。\
**Lopera**: Orders completed, Admiral.

微笑极少出现在这位久经沙场的老将脸上。\
A rare smile flashes across the admiral's face.

伊戈尔点点头，那双鹰一样的眼中，流露出对养女的赞许。\
He nods, a glimmer of approval for his adopted daughter in his eyes.

**伊戈尔将军**：做得很好。\
**Admiral Igor**: Well done, dismissed.

行刑者敬礼致意，随后跟上士兵队伍，离开刑场。\
Lopera salutes before following the soldiers away from the execution grounds.

**伊戈尔将军**：接连发生意外，真是可耻。\
**Admiral Igor**: There have been too many accidents—an unacceptable rate.

老将军面露难色，近期发生的士兵叛逃事件就像不久前泄露的那段影像，将芝诺军中尴尬的现状暴露无遗。\
The admiral's face shows discomfort. The recent soldier desertions, like the leaked footage, have exposed the embarrassing state of the Zeno army.

**红弩箭**：这些孬种犯了什么事？\
**Lilya**: What reason could you have to kill your own men?

**伊戈尔将军**：逃兵，杀死长官之后叛逃。\
**Admiral Igor**: Not our men. Not any longer. They mutinied and killed their superior officer.

**红弩箭**：哈，那的确该死。\
**Lilya**: So they got what they deserved, then.

**伊戈尔将军**：莫莉德尔副官正在竭力调查基地中的潜在叛乱分子。\
**Admiral Igor**: Lieutenant Moldir is investigating still. We will find out who else was involved.

**伊戈尔将军**：这里被天使兄弟会渗透得很严重。\
**Admiral Igor**: The Apostles Brotherhood is back. We suspect they may have even infiltrated our base.

**伊戈尔将军**：有证据显示重塑之手也在圣保罗活动。\
**Admiral Igor**: We've also received intel indicating Manus Vindictae's presence in São Paulo.

**维尔汀**：重塑之手？\
**Vertin**: Manus Vindictae?

**维尔汀**：……重塑之手一直与天使兄弟会纠缠不清。\
**Vertin**: I'm not entirely surprised. Intelligence suggests they are closely associated with the Apostles Brotherhood.

**维尔汀**：我以为他们只会以“启明会”的身份活动。\
**Vertin**: What I hadn't expected is that they would drop their "Order of Enlightenment" guise so soon.

**维尔汀**：明明阿尔卡纳已经死亡……\
**Vertin**: But Arcana is dead.

**伊戈尔将军**：是的，在真空弹中灰飞烟灭。\
**Admiral Igor**: There is no room for doubt. No one, nothing, could survive a vacuum bomb.

将军亲自下令，曾叱嗟风云的那位女士……肉身自爆炸中踪迹全无。毁灭从天而降，如同硫磺与死亡从云间坠落。\
It was the admiral's personal order to annihilate that once formidable woman. Destruction rained from the sky, and once the dust settled, it was clear that she had been utterly obliterated.

而基地的刑场上，阳光与不忠者的鲜血流过遍地荒草。\
The sun glistens in the pooling blood of the executed traitors.

**维尔汀**：唔……\
**Vertin**: Hm ...

滚烫的初夏在额头灼烧，汗水不住流下。\
Sweat gathers on her forehead.

**伊戈尔将军**：圣保罗的太阳一向这样，你很快也会适应它。\
**Admiral Igor**: You will become used to the tropical sun in São Paulo.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

南半球的初夏热情得有些难以招架。\
The early summer heat here is overwhelming.

**红弩箭**：我经历过比这更难受的。\
**Lilya**: I've been through a lot worse.

**红弩箭**：在一些并不愉快的地方。山、沙子、雪山和山间的鹰……\
**Lilya**: Snowy mountains, deserts, and soaring eagles.

**伊戈尔将军**：啊，那儿，我记得……\
**Admiral Igor**: I, too, find myself thinking back to those times.

**伊戈尔将军**：是的，很少有地方比那儿残酷，也很少有战争比发生在那儿的更悲哀。\
**Admiral Igor**: It should never have been a battleground.

**伊戈尔将军**：行刑结束了。司辰、红弩箭中尉，我们回室内谈吧。\
**Admiral Igor**: Our business here is concluded. Timekeeper, Lieutenant Lilya, let us continue inside.

**红弩箭**：会议让头儿去就行，我没兴趣。\
**Lilya**: Do you really need me in there, Captain? Otherwise, I'd like to hang out here for a bit.

飞行员灌下一口甜酒，但这不是她爱喝的生命之水。酒里没有北方那股雪渣子的味道。\
She gulps down some sweet liquor, but it provides little succor. It lacks the frosty flavor of the north.

她一定不喜欢这股慵懒而又醉醺醺的味道，但基地能提供给她的只有这些了。\
This drink is lethargic, but it's all the base has to offer.

在圣保罗，跨国公司提供的碳酸汽水往往比干净的水更便宜，而比汽水更便宜的，则是酒，取之不尽的朗姆酒。\
In São Paulo, soda is cheap, but rum is cheaper—and in near endless supply.

**红弩箭**：我去找苏芙比玩玩儿，就这样。Пока!\
**Lilya**: I'll check on Sotheby. See you both later, bye!

**伊戈尔将军**：在基地里，别忘了纪律，很多地区已经荒废了，不要离开有卫兵巡守的地方。\
**Admiral Igor**: Dismissed, soldier, but I caution you, much has been abandoned here. Remember our rules and keep to within the guarded areas.

一间朴素的办公室，桌面放着军用地图和电话，以及数个随意堆放着的小骰子。\
A simple office. Military papers litter the walls and shelves, and a phone sits on a side table. A few dice are scattered casually on the desk.

**伊戈尔将军**：《UTTU》杂志有一位叫做“兀尔德”的投稿人，在被回溯的每个时代我们都找到了她的署名稿件。\
**Admiral Igor**: There may be a person of interest to us nearby, a writer for the UTTU Magazine, said to be a blind woman named Urd. Her works seemed to be published after every era the "Storm" has affected.

**伊戈尔将军**：是有人在共用这个笔名，还是说……\
**Admiral Igor**: It could be this is only an alias, a pen name used by a new person each time, or—

**维尔汀**：这位自由撰稿人一直没有被“暴雨”回溯……\
**Vertin**: Or could she really have crossed the "Storm" eight times?

**维尔汀**：——“暴雨”，并没有带走她？\
**Vertin**: And, somehow, the "Storm" has never affected her?

**维尔汀**：不久前，德克萨斯的数羊羔小姐提供了一些信息。\
**Vertin**: Ms. Barbara provided us with some information.

**维尔汀**：“这份稿件从圣保罗的荣军院寄来。”\
**Vertin**: She said the latest piece was sent from a Veterans' Residence in São Paulo.

**伊戈尔将军**：荣军院？那儿有位盲眼医生，也许你可以去见见她，就在圣保罗城里。\
**Admiral Igor**: I understand they have a doctor working there, a blind woman. If so, she would match our intelligence on this mysterious UTTU writer. You should seek her out.

**伊戈尔将军**：你来的时机很合适，这儿的上任长官卡洛斯是个蠢货，竟然被自己的部下在这间办公室里枪杀。\
**Admiral Igor**: You are fortunate to have come now, Timekeeper. Carlos, the late commander here, was something of a pain to work with. An idiot. Maybe this is why his own men rose up and killed him.

老将军转过身去。\
He turns away.

**维尔汀**：……！\
**Vertin**: ...!

**伊戈尔将军**：好消息是我们已经追回了大部分叛徒。\
**Admiral Igor**: We've already dispensed with most of them.

**维尔汀**：是刚才被处决的那批人……？\
**Vertin**: Those men you just had executed?

**伊戈尔将军**：是的。洛佩拉突袭了兄弟会在上校庄园的据点，重创了他们和重塑之手的势力。\
**Admiral Igor**: Yes. Lopera raided one of their locations. Manus Vindictae will not be so happy to hear that, I think.

**伊戈尔将军**：虽然行动鲁莽，但她干得不错。\
**Admiral Igor**: She was, I'm told, excessive in her work, a "loose cannon," but I am pleased with her results.

老将军对刚才指挥行刑的少女，似乎评价颇高。\
He seems to hold Lopera in high regard.

冷酷，肃杀，决绝——和她柑橘般甜美热烈的橙发却有些格格不入。\
Cold, ruthless, decisive—qualities that don't quite match her sweet face and fiery orange hair.

**维尔汀**：伊戈尔将军，接下来的行动我需要您的帮助。\
**Vertin**: Admiral, with you in charge here now, I thought I might ask a favor.

需要熟悉当地的人员，需要交通工具，需要情报……\
She needs to familiarize herself with the local area, transportation, and intelligence.

**维尔汀**：如果能得到芝诺伙伴的协助，我想，一切会顺利得多。\
**Vertin**: Things may become quite complicated during our visit to São Paulo. I wonder if I might request Zeno spare some manpower to assist us.

**伊戈尔将军**：我会尽力满足你的需求，但这儿的情况比我想象中更糟糕。\
**Admiral Igor**: Our situation is more dire than expected. I will see what can be done, Timekeeper. But, no promises.

这儿的十七座塔楼和二十二个庭院都曾有驻军巡逻。可现在大半已经荒废，沦为了杂草与食雨甲虫的乐园。\
The seventeen towers and twenty-two courtyards of the base were once all fully patrolled, but now most of them are abandoned.

**伊戈尔将军**：我的副官莫莉德尔中尉会尽快替你筹办这些事。\
**Admiral Igor**: Lieutenant Moldir will provision you with everything you need.

**伊戈尔将军**：而洛佩拉……她很熟悉那座城市，可以做你的向导。\
**Admiral Igor**: And Lopera, she knows São Paulo well. You may take her with you, as a guide.

老将军为基地的现状而叹气，但也尽力提供了他能提供的一切援助。\
The admiral has offered all the assistance he can spare. He sighs at the state of the base.

**伊戈尔将军**：除此之外，我也有一个请求，希望你能答应。\
**Admiral Igor**: Now, Timekeeper, there is also something you might do for me.

他显得很无奈。芝诺的窘境就像这座杂草丛生的基地，已不再有它曾经的辉煌与强大。\
He seems resigned. Zeno is just like this dilapidated base, a weakened shadow of its former self.

**维尔汀**：如果我能帮上您的话，将军。\
**Vertin**: As long as it's within my power, Admiral.

**伊戈尔将军**：那位叫红弩箭的年轻中尉，希望她能暂时留在这里，我手下的新兵急需一位可靠的教官。\
**Admiral Igor**: I see that you have one of ours with you, Lieutenant Lilya—I ask that she serve us for the duration of your mission here. She is a fine instructor, and Zeno is in need of help training our latest recruits.

**维尔汀**：只要她本人不反对。\
**Vertin**: I'll speak with her and see what she thinks.

**伊戈尔将军**：谢谢你的理解。\
**Admiral Igor**: Thank you.

**伊戈尔将军**：回去见见你的朋友们吧，莫莉德尔中尉应该也在会客室照顾她俩。\
**Admiral Igor**: I should return to my work. Your comrades should be waiting for you in the meeting room with Lieutenant Moldir.

## 8TH-02 框中旧影 / A New Photo of an Old Friend

柱廊阴影下，少女咬着冷饮吸管，无所事事地晃腿踢打空气。\
Under the shadow of the colonnade, the orange-headed girl absentmindedly kicks at the ground, sipping a cold drink.

庭院荒芜，石缝之间的杂草顽强生长着，骄傲地对抗着圣保罗的烈日。甲虫从一处草丛爬向另一处草丛，而这一切都被少女看在眼里。\
She watches as a beetle scurries across the courtyard, disappearing into a patch of weeds.

**？？？**：一个人待这儿？\
**???**: What are you doing out here alone?

女士沿着破落的大理石柱慢慢走来。\
She dips under the shadow of the colonnade, the sun streaming in behind her.

凉荫下的少女抬手遮住刺眼的阳光，看向来客——\
The orange-headed girl raises her hand to block the glaring sunlight as she tries to make out the woman's face.

**洛佩拉**：嗯？姐姐！！\
**Lopera**: Mm? Molly!

和她在同一位“父亲”身边长大的莫莉德尔姐姐。\
It's her "sister," Moldir. They grew up together under the watchful eye of their adoptive father.

她扔掉饮料，像只摇着尾巴的小狼犬，藏不住笑脸，跑向姐姐。\
She tosses her drink aside, her face lighting up like a puppy wagging its tail as she runs toward her sister.

跑步音效\

**莫莉德尔**：噢——慢点，慢点，扑上来这一下……真有劲儿，哈哈。\
**Moldir**: Heh, at ease, soldier—You've really been building some strength, haven't you?

副官女士摸着妹妹的脑袋，将她搂紧。\
She pats her sister's head as she hugs her tightly.

**莫莉德尔**：你长高了。\
**Moldir**: And you're sprouting up like a weed.

**洛佩拉**：那你肯定长胖了。\
**Lopera**: And you, looks like they've been feeding you well.

“礼尚往来”，她也伸手探进姐姐衣服里，摸到对方柔软的肚腩。\
"Returning the favor," she slips her hand under her sister's shirt and pinches her soft belly.

**莫莉德尔**：洛佩拉——！\
**Moldir**: Pera!

**莫莉德尔**：会痒的，别闹。\
**Moldir**: Stop it!

一个小小的恶作剧。\
Just a little prank.

**洛佩拉**：这次过来待多久？\
**Lopera**: How long will you be staying this time?

**莫莉德尔**：不多久，很快，很快就要走。\
**Moldir**: Not long. Father plans to leave soon.

**莫莉德尔**：父亲对圣保罗的事情很生气，向总部要求临时调来这儿。\
**Moldir**: He was furious when he heard about the defections. He ordered that he be brought here immediately.

作为老将军最信任的副官和孩子，她随老将军一同来到圣保罗的基地。\
As the admiral's most trusted lieutenant and child, she has accompanied him to the São Paulo base.

**莫莉德尔**：等下一任长官过来，或许到时候你可以跟我们一起走……\
**Moldir**: Perhaps you might leave with us when the new C.O. arrives.

副官女士有些迟疑。\
She seems hesitant.

只有伊戈尔将军能决定所有人的去留——无论她，还是洛佩拉，抑或是其他任何人。\
Only the admiral decides who stays and who goes—whether it be her, Lopera, or anyone else.

**洛佩拉**：是吗？喔……我其实还挺喜欢这边，荣军院的老头儿和老奶奶都是些有意思的人。\
**Lopera**: Really? But ... I don't know. Things are going well for me here, Molly. I enjoy being near the Veterans' Residence.

**莫莉德尔**：很高兴看到你有新朋友，老人的智慧向来值得尊重。\
**Moldir**: Then I'm happy for you. The wisdom of elders is worth its weight in gold.

**洛佩拉**：哎呀……你说教的样子跟老爹越来越像了。\
**Lopera**: Oh, come on! You sound just like him.

**洛佩拉**：他人呢？\
**Lopera**: Speaking of him, didn't the old man come with you?

她左右张望，而老将军显然不在附近。\
She looks around, but Admiral Igor is nowhere to be seen.

**莫莉德尔**：父亲和基金会的司辰去办公室谈话了。\
**Moldir**: He's still with the Timekeeper, in his office.

**洛佩拉**：喔～所以你是偷偷溜出来的喽？\
**Lopera**: Ah, so you snuck out just to see me?

**洛佩拉**：偷偷溜出来找我对不对！\
**Lopera**: Did you really? You did!

**莫莉德尔**：不，我是想来……锄草，基地里荒了很多地方，到处都得打扫。\
**Moldir**: Um, n-no, I came to, um, weed. The grounds have gotten so messy since the shutdown.

锄草。一个荒唐的理由，走过一个又一个庭院，绕过一片片荒地，就为了寻找一株活蹦乱跳的“杂草”。\
Weeding. A ridiculous excuse. Who would bother to traipse through all these desolate courtyards just to pull a few plants?

**洛佩拉**：撒谎。\
**Lopera**: You're lying.

**洛佩拉**：姐姐你耳根红了。\
**Lopera**: Those ears of yours are scarlet red.

这是她的顽疾，是她的羞赧和她的诚实，正如嘴会说谎，但梦永远诚实。\
This has always been one of her difficulties. Her face may be steely, but her glowing red ears always give away the truth.

**莫莉德尔**：好了，一起去会客室吧，基金会来的客人还在等我，可不能让父亲知道我们偷偷跑出来了……\
**Moldir**: Alright, no more joking. We should get to the meeting room. Our Foundation guests are waiting. I would like to get back before they realize I've slipped away.

**洛佩拉**：哇我跟你讲，我们突袭上校庄园的时候，还抓回一个很难搞的俘虏……\
**Lopera**: Alright, but while we go, let me tell you about the prisoner we captured during our raid.

**洛佩拉**：圣保罗城里还有一艘装在瓶子里的小船……\
**Lopera**: And a strange little ship in a bottle ...

草丛间，彩羽毛的蜂鸟望着有说有笑远去的两人背影，又转而看向基地南边的棕色高塔……\
Amid the grass, a hummingbird watches the two as they walk away, talking and laughing together. It turns its gaze toward the tower in the south of the base.

屋内简单、硬朗、整洁，满是军队做派。\
The room is simple, sturdy, and clean. A military room through and through.

苏芙比和她的飞行员伙伴无所事事地打量着这间会客室。\
Sotheby and Lilya are idly looking around the reception room.

退伍军人们的合照按照年份排布，光荣地悬挂在墙上。\
Photographs of veterans are proudly hung on the wall. They're arranged in chronological order.

**苏芙比**：嗯……1968年，一座古老的城市。\
**Sotheby**: Mm, 1968.

士兵们看上去表情阴沉，不愿面对镜头，那是一场没有鲜花与荣誉的胜利。\
The soldiers look grim. They avert their eyes from the camera, a hollow look within them. It was a victory without flowers or honor.

**苏芙比**：这个地方叫做……伊兹、密尔。嗯……伊兹密尔是什么地方？会有阿邦·阿库吗？我还从来没有去过这里呢。\
**Sotheby**: Izmir. I've never heard of it. I wonder if they have any Abang-Akus there?

枣椰树下，结队的士兵远眺向古老而富庶的地中海海岸，留下了一张宝贵的影像。\
In one photograph, soldiers stand in formation under a row of date palms. They gaze off into the glimmering coastline.

**苏芙比**：1986年，里约热内卢……唔……里约热……\
**Sotheby**: 1986, Rio de Janeiro ... Hmm ... Rio ...

**苏芙比**：——咦，等、等等？！\
**Sotheby**: Hold on! Is—is that?!

里约热内卢。海岸边，她隐约看到了一张熟悉得不能再熟悉的脸。\
Rio de Janeiro. Among the soldiers, she spots a face that is all too familiar.

**苏芙比**：卡森先生为什么会在那儿！\
**Sotheby**: Mr. Karson?!

她接连蹦起，试图取下那副沉重的木相框。\
She jumps up, trying to get ahold of the wooden frame.

一张熟悉的脸出现在相片上，但那位先生早已消失在了1929年的“暴雨”中。\
Mr. Karson disappeared in the "Storm" of 1929.

**红弩箭**：怎么，连这儿你都有熟人？\
**Lilya**: Oh, you have friends in Rio?

飞行员为矮个子的伙伴取下相框。\
Lilya takes the photo off the wall.

**苏芙比**：天哪！卡森先生！\
**Sotheby**: I can't believe it! That simply must be Mr. Karson!

她绝不会认错。\
She would never mistake him.

尽管改换发色，蓬发让他看起来比从前热情不少，但硬朗的五官与她记忆中老人的浮影重合，渐渐合为一人。\
He looks livelier than before. His hair is darker and wilder, but his features are unmistakably those of her dear butler.

**苏芙比**：可是“暴雨”不是把他……我亲眼看到卡森先生……消失……\
**Sotheby**: But the "Storm" ... I saw him ... He dissolved.

**红弩箭**：“暴雨”？你在说什么？\
**Lilya**: Mr. Karson? What, you mean this old geezer in the photo? What are you talking about?

苏芙比连连摇头。\
Sotheby nods her head fervently.

**苏芙比**：——不对不对，他和卡森先生就是同一个人！\
**Sotheby**: Why, this must be Mr. Karson!

**苏芙比**：世界上没有长得这么像的人，所以如果一个人长得跟另一个人一样……嗯，那他们……他们肯定就是同一个人！\
**Sotheby**: There's no two men in the world that could look so alike! Could it be a doppelganger or an evil twin? But then, surely Mr. Karson would have mentioned a twin brother—even an evil one.

**苏芙比**：你看，这个鼻子……这个眼睛……嗯，虽然他没有戴眼镜，但是这条皱纹很明显……\
**Sotheby**: The nose ... and his eyes ... Though he's not wearing his glasses, but I know those wrinkles.

她自言自语，甚至有点儿语无伦次。相框中的老人令她感到不可思议——无论是那张与卡森先生几乎完全一致的长相，还是热烈张扬的笑容。\
Sotheby continues to talk to herself. The man in the photo looks just like Mr. Karson, save for the smile on his face.

严肃的老管家绝不会露出这样的笑。\
The stern old butler would never smile like that.

**苏芙比**：不行，我、我必须贴近瞧瞧！\
**Sotheby**: I have to look closer!

放大浮窗

**苏芙比**：啊，也许是我弄错了？但为什么会有长得一模一样的两个人呢……\
**Sotheby**: I must be mistaken. But he is so very alike to the Karson I remember.

一千零一个问号在小淑女的脑子里像魔药试管中的泡泡一样咕噜咕噜冒出。\
Like a potion in a bottle, a thousand and one questions bubble up in her mind.

她瞪大眼睛，举起相框，近得连鼻子都贴上了堆满灰尘的相框玻璃——\
She almost presses her nose against the dusty glass of the picture frame as she tries to make out every detail.

**苏芙比**：难道……卡森管家他、他……\
**Sotheby**: Maybe then, Mr. Karson could still be ...

她被灰尘呛了个喷嚏。\
The dust has gotten into her nose.

**苏芙比**：阿、阿嚏……！\
**Sotheby**: *sneezes*

老将军走进了会客室。\
Admiral Igor strides into the room.

**伊戈尔将军**：莫莉德尔呢？\
**Admiral Igor**: Where is Lieutenant Moldir?

他环视房间各处，但这儿没有一位叫做“莫莉德尔”的人。\
He looks around. Moldir was supposed to be welcoming their new guests.

**红弩箭**：将军，司辰。\
**Lilya**: Sir. Timekeeper.

飞行员看到将军到来，立刻挺直身躯，行礼致敬。\
Lilya immediately straightens up, saluting the admiral.

**苏芙比**：维尔汀！快来看看！\
**Sotheby**: Ms. Vertin! Come and look!

苏芙比握着一个相框，激动地挥手——\
Sotheby waves at her, the photograph clutched in her hand.

**苏芙比**：卡森先生……他好像、好像还活着——！\
**Sotheby**: Mr. Karson could still be alive!

**维尔汀**：嗯？！\
**Vertin**: Huh?!

他还活着？！从众人眼前消失，被1929年的“暴雨”回溯的卡森先生，竟然还活着？！\
Still alive?! The Mr. Karson who vanished before their eyes in the "Storm" of 1929?

**红弩箭**：苏芙比在退伍老兵们的合照里看到了她的家人。维尔汀，你也认识这位卡森先生？\
**Lilya**: I guess Sotheby saw someone familiar in one of these veterans' photos. You know this Karson guy?

**苏芙比**：你看这里——\
**Sotheby**: Look, look!

**维尔汀**：……！\
**Vertin**: ...!

他曾消失在1929年的雨幕中，如同一位从舞台上被抹去的演员。\
How could it be? Mr. Karson was erased by the "Storm" of 1929.

**维尔汀**：他长得……确实和卡森管家非常相似，如果我没有记错的话。\
**Vertin**: He does bear a striking resemblance to Mr. Karson, if my memory serves me right.

可现在却出现在另一张照片上……\
Yet here he is, in a photo dated 1986.

老将军走过来，看着苏芙比手中的旧照片，看向她手指指向的老人。\
The admiral strides over and examines the photo.

**伊戈尔将军**：有很多了不起的战士永远留在了亚马孙河的急流里，但也有更多的侥幸得生。\
**Admiral Igor**: Oh, '86. We lost many good soldiers to the Amazon that year. But some battled through, survived.

**伊戈尔将军**：他就是其中一位勇敢的幸运儿。\
**Admiral Igor**: This man is one of the latter.

**伊戈尔将军**：不过，我不太明白你们聊的话题。你们以前曾经见过这位士兵？\
**Admiral Igor**: You are saying that you've met this man before?

**维尔汀**：我们有一位朋友被1929年的“暴雨”回溯，他和这位先生很像。\
**Vertin**: He looks remarkably similar to a friend of ours who was lost in the "Storm" in 1929.

**维尔汀**：事实上，将军，他们……几乎长得一模一样。这简直不可思议。\
**Vertin**: In fact, Admiral. They appear to be nearly identical. It's almost unthinkable.

**苏芙比**：虽然换了衣服……虽然……但他肯定就是卡森先生！\
**Sotheby**: I must say Mr. Karson would never dress like that. But I'm certain this is him!

这位老先生让她想念起了自己的老管家。\
Just looking at him brings back memories of her dear old butler.

**伊戈尔将军**：那这真是件有意思的事情，嗯……\
**Admiral Igor**: That is fascinating.

**维尔汀**：这位老先生，他现在还在世吗？\
**Vertin**: Do you know if this man is still alive?

**伊戈尔将军**：如果他活着，现在也该在圣保罗的荣军院。\
**Admiral Igor**: I couldn't say, doubtful he would be in our service anymore. But you may find him at the Veterans' Residence in São Paulo.

圣保罗，荣军院。像河流交汇的小岛，秘密和答案都聚在那儿的沙滩上，等着水鸟叼走。\
São Paulo, the Veterans' Residence.Like items washed to the shore, secrets and answers gather there, waiting for the birds to carry them away.

开门声

**洛佩拉**：大～家好～！\
**Lopera**: Hi, everyone!

**莫莉德尔**：抱歉让各位久等……了。\
**Moldir**: Thank you for your pa-tience.

行刑场上的少女和另一位女士来到会客厅，却迎面遇上老将军冷铁一样的脸。\
The two of them are met with a cold look from the admiral.

**伊戈尔将军**：……\
**Admiral Igor**: ...

**洛佩拉**：将、将军……\
**Lopera**: Sir ...

## 8TH-03 牛头人身怪 / The Minotaur

会客室

**伊戈尔将军**：莫莉德尔，刑场到这儿的路，我想用不着走这么久。\
**Admiral Igor**: Lieutenant Moldir, about time. What was it? Did you stop for a picnic?

将军训斥着自己的副官。\
A scalding comment.

她本该在行刑结束后就来照顾基金会的客人苏芙比小姐，但却“擅离职守”。\
Moldir was supposed to be taking care of Ms. Sotheby. It seems she has abandoned her duties.

**莫莉德尔**：非常抱歉，将军。我……\
**Moldir**: Admiral, I ...

**伊戈尔将军**：无需辩解。\
**Admiral Igor**: Save your excuses.

**莫莉德尔**：是！\
**Moldir**: Yes, sir!

**洛佩拉**：是我把姐姐拉去外面玩的，我们真的很久没见面了……\
**Lopera**: It was my fault, Admiral. I ran into her on our way here. It's been a while since we last saw each other.

她试图为姐姐打个圆场，但老将军的眼神却让她意识到自己又犯了个错误。\
As her father glares at her, she quickly realizes that her attempt to cover for her sister is only making things worse.

**维尔汀**：你在校场上的表现令人印象深刻，洛佩拉小姐。\
**Vertin**: Your performance on the training ground earlier was most impressive, Ms. Lopera.

一个友善的招呼或许能够打破现场冷冰冰的尴尬。\
She breaks the awkward silence.

**维尔汀**：这位是和我一起来的苏芙比小姐。\
**Vertin**: Allow me to introduce my team. This is Ms. Sotheby.

苏芙比微笑着行了提裙礼。\
Sotheby smiles and curtsies.

**维尔汀**：这是红弩箭。\
**Vertin**: And this is Lieutenant Lilya.

飞行员向新的同伴简单行了军礼。\
She gives a brief salute.

**红弩箭**：总部来的，您好，同志。\
**Lilya**: How's it going? I was previously assigned to HQ.

**伊戈尔将军**：看来你在圣保罗过得太自由了，洛佩拉。\
**Admiral Igor**: It seems your assignment here has done little for your discipline, Lopera.

老将军背着手，脸色冷峻，仿佛群山之上覆雪的峰峦，俯视着不受管教的女儿。\
The admiral stands with his hands behind his back. He examines his undisciplined daughter, a grim look on his face.

**伊戈尔将军**：接下来你会负责保护司辰的人身安全，他们有重要任务要去圣保罗。\
**Admiral Igor**: You have new orders. I am assigning you to accompany the Timekeeper and her team to São Paulo for the duration of their mission.

听到老将军的安排，洛佩拉点头接受，一旁的红弩箭却发出疑问。\
Lopera nods, but Lilya still has questions.

**红弩箭**：嗯？她去？头儿有我看着呢。\
**Lilya**: Me and Lopera? That's a whole lot of firepower. What are we expecting during this mission?

**维尔汀**：嗯……基地需要一位教官，将军向我推荐了你。\
**Vertin**: Oh! Sorry, Lilya. I haven't had the chance to speak with you privately. The Admiral asked if you could stay on site to help with training their new recruits.

**维尔汀**：我会尊重你的选择，红弩箭。\
**Vertin**: What do you think? You can do as you wish.

**红弩箭**：教官？好吧，看来又要错过跟敌人干架的机会了。但训练新兵蛋子，这事儿也挺不错，我服从命令。\
**Lilya**: Training up some new blood, eh? Well, as long as you think you can handle things without me, I can stick around to lend a hand. It'll be just like the good old days back at the academy.

她很清楚：这不是老将军的问询，而是一个命令。\
She knows that this isn't a request but an order.

**伊戈尔将军**：感谢你的服务，中尉。\
**Admiral Igor**: Thank you, Lieutenant.

老将军对飞行员点点头，微笑着予以感谢。随后，他收起笑容，目光转向最年轻的女儿。\
He nods and smiles in thanks. His smile fades as he turns to his youngest daughter.

**伊戈尔将军**：至于你，洛佩拉……\
**Admiral Igor**: As for you, Lopera ...

**伊戈尔将军**：如果精力过剩，就带客人们回房间去休息。\
**Admiral Igor**: Please show our guests to their rooms, and try not to over-exert yourself.

老将军一一为在场的各位做出安排。\
Orders have been given to everyone present.

**伊戈尔将军**：红弩箭中尉，请在这儿稍微等等。\
**Admiral Igor**: Lieutenant Lilya, stay for a moment.

**伊戈尔将军**：莫莉德尔会给你一些关于基地现状的文件，希望你能尽快投入训练工作。\
**Admiral Igor**: Lieutenant Moldir will bring some documents shortly; they should prove useful for your assignment.

老将军身后的副官女士无奈地耸耸肩：一句又一句轻描淡写的命令，最终都会变成她手上的一件件工作。\
Moldir, briefly out of the admiral's sight, shrugs helplessly as her orders start to pile up.

飞行员对副官女士投以一个理解的笑容——大伙儿都这样，这就是任务。\
Lilya gives her a knowing smile. It's always like this. It's just part of the job.

**伊戈尔将军**：我还有一些军务要处理，就这样。\
**Admiral Igor**: Now, I have other business to attend to. If you'll excuse me.

将军离开脚步声

老将军转身离去，伟岸的高大身姿不久便消失在众人视野之外。\
He turns and leaves, his imposing figure soon disappearing from sight.

洛佩拉长舒口气，打个响指，笑着走向门边，回身递来邀请。\
Lopera exhales a long breath, snaps her fingers, and smiles as she heads toward the door. She turns to her guests.

**洛佩拉**：走呗，我带你们逛逛——当心，别跟丢了，这地方像个迷宫，还藏着会吃人的牛头怪呢！\
**Lopera**: Come on, let's go. I'll show you around. But stay close. This base can be a bit of a labyrinth. It's only missing a bloodthirsty minotaur lurking its halls. Well, I haven't seen him yet, anyways.

**洛佩拉**：一般来说，我们不建议各位客人在这儿闲逛，不少地方都荒废很多年了。\
**Lopera**: The base here has been understaffed for some time; whole sections are deserted—it can be dangerous. We don't usually allow guests to move about freely.

**洛佩拉**：好吧，其实这儿也没有客人会来。谁会没事儿跑来这么个鬼地方观光呢？\
**Lopera**: Well, who am I kidding? We don't have any guests in the first place. Who'd come here for a visit?

**洛佩拉**：瞧瞧，这儿花是蔫儿的，草是荒的，石头缝里爬出藤蔓，藤蔓底下又藏着虫子和魔精。\
**Lopera**: "Scenic views of dead gardens and overgrown brush. In the spring we have vine-tripping competitions, and in the summer you can be part of our complementary bug buffet!"

**洛佩拉**：连纳塔尔的农民见了都得摇头：“天哪，老兄，我宁肯去给撒旦舔屁股，也不想住在这么个鬼地方呀！”\
**Lopera**: Even the farmers back home had it better than this.

她叼着一根随手捡来的狼尾草，走在前面，聊着这座基地。\
She leads the way, chewing on a piece of wolf's-tail grass.

**洛佩拉**：芝诺入驻之前，这里是一位里斯本贵族的城堡。\
**Lopera**: Before Zeno moved in, this was the fort of some Lisbon aristocrat.

旧大陆的影子在这儿随处可见，鬼魂般的十八世纪还附着在大理石柱的每一道刻痕上。\
The shadows of the old continent are everywhere here, the ghosts of the 18th century still clinging to every mark on the marble columns.

**洛佩拉**：我们哪里都可以去，但只有那座塔不能进去。\
**Lopera**: There's only one place fully off-limits here: that tower.

她指向远方的棕色高塔。\
She points to a tower in the distance.

那座仿自安达卢西亚风格的高耸塔楼矗立着，在烈日之下，像乌鸦盘绕的伦敦塔般阴森。\
Styled after Andalusian architecture, it stands ominously under the scorching sun, looming over the base with an eerie intensity.

**维尔汀**：那里面有什么？\
**Vertin**: What's in there?

**苏芙比**：喔～是不是藏着你刚刚说的牛头人身怪！\
**Sotheby**: It must be the minotaur's lair!

**苏芙比**：是不是还藏着……芝诺的新型神秘学家士兵……！\
**Sotheby**: Or a secret lab for super soldiers!

苏芙比发散着她的想象力。\
Sotheby's imagination is running wild again.

**苏芙比**：有公牛的力量、人类的智力，还有能噗噗喷火的嘴和翼蝠蜥蜴的翅膀！\
**Sotheby**: Imbued with the strength of an ox, the wits of a man, and the wings and fiery breath of a dragon!

**洛佩拉**：……这样的怪物我们一般会叫它“奇美拉”，小姐。\
**Lopera**: Miss, this is a Zeno base, not some chimera's nest.

**洛佩拉**：但我想这事情不太可能，塔里面没有公牛的闷吼。\
**Lopera**: Besides, if there were any monsters in there, I would have heard them by now.

**维尔汀**：将军的命令是“不能进去”吗？\
**Vertin**: Were those the Admiral's exact words? That nobody is allowed "inside" the tower?

**洛佩拉**：没错，明文命令就是“不能进去”。\
**Lopera**: Yeah, that was what he said: "Under no circumstances is anyone to be allowed inside."

那只要不打开塔楼房门，就不算违反禁令。\
Then a quick peek around wouldn't exactly violate the letter of that order.

**苏芙比**：维尔汀，你是不是想……\
**Sotheby**: Ms. Vertin, are you thinking what I'm thinking?

高塔里会有宝藏吗？\
Is there treasure inside the tower?

**洛佩拉**：我得说，伙计们，塔里面真的没有苏芙比小姐形容的那种怪物……\
**Lopera**: Let me say this again: There are no monsters in that tower.

**洛佩拉**：我接到的命令是带你们回房间。\
**Lopera**: And I am under orders to escort you directly to your rooms.

她眨巴眨巴眼睛——嘿，朋友们，你们不是这儿唯一对它好奇的人。\
She blinks. Clearly, curiosity isn't only in the hearts of these new guests.

**洛佩拉**：但要是你们闲逛到塔楼附近，比如被魔精追赶，或者因为清理魔精而不小心追过去……\
**Lopera**: But if we were to, say, walk a bit too close, and "accidentally" provoke some nearby critters ...

庭院里从来不缺爱惹麻烦的魔精，它们总会在该出现的时候出现。\
Mischievous critters often wander into the courtyards, and these ones have appeared just in time.

**苏芙比**：哇——！说、说来就来了啊！\
**Sotheby**: Oh! How terrible! It seems trouble has found us!

**苏芙比**：真是吓了一跳！还好它们逃了，呼……呼……！\
**Sotheby**: They gave me quite a start! Thankfully, they were easy to handle.

**洛佩拉**：可不能放任它们这样破坏植被，得清除干净才行！\
**Lopera**: We can't let them run off. Who knows what damage they could do?

洛佩拉驱赶着逃跑的魔精，“不经意”跑向了棕色高塔……\
Lopera chases after the fleeing critters, who just so happen to be heading in the direction of the tower.

这只是发生在迷宫中的巧合。\
It is nothing more than a coincidence.

横切1\
横切2

一场长达半个小时的“追捕”游戏，终于到此为止。\
The half-hour-long game of "tag" finally comes to an end.

**苏芙比**：到底躲去了哪儿呢……\
**Sotheby**: Now where could they have gone?

她认真地找寻着罕见的彩色魔精，直到撞见一扇被柠檬树守卫着的木门。\
She searches for the colorful critters, a serious look on her face. In her concentration, she bumps into a wooden door flanked by lemon trees.

**维尔汀**：它逃进塔里了。\
**Vertin**: It may well be possible they fled into the tower.

一座高塔，一扇木门。门板在石塔底端静静守望，像只打盹的老棕熊。\
The door stands at the base of the tower.

**维尔汀**：刚才看见的塔，就是这儿吗？\
**Vertin**: Is this the entrance?

**洛佩拉**：司辰——！\
**Lopera**: Timekeeper!

不能进去。\
Clearly, this door is not supposed to be opened.

**洛佩拉**：老爹有命令。\
**Lopera**: My father, the admiral, he won't be happy with this.

门就像一颗多汁的蜜桃，一个夏日的诱惑，古旧、腐朽，似乎轻轻一碰就能推倒，却将塔楼与庭院隔绝开。\
The sight of it is tantalizing. Just a touch, and it will swing open, revealing all the mysteries within.

**苏芙比**：唔，可是为什么不让大家进去呢？\
**Sotheby**: But why? Is there something hidden inside?

墙上有抓痕，门上有血迹——兔子血、公牛血、未经祝福的羔羊血。\
Claw marks line the wall, and blood stains the door—rabbit blood, bull blood, unblessed lamb blood.

风吹起门边柠檬树的影子，空气中弥漫着月桂与桃金娘的淡香。\
The wind stirs the lemon trees, filling the air with the faint scent of bay and myrtle.

**维尔汀**：伊戈尔将军为什么要把这里封锁起来？\
**Vertin**: There's an arcane array on the door.

**维尔汀**：这是一个术阵。\
**Vertin**: Is it to stop us from entering, or to keep what's inside from coming out?

一个衰弱而古老的术阵。\
The arcane array looks ancient. It has weakened with time.

指腹划过用公牛血描画的术式，凝成硬砂般的血迹悄悄脱落，断开一个小小的缺口。\
She traces the markings with her fingertips. The blood flakes off, breaking a small gap in the array.

**洛佩拉**：老爹下命令，也没人敢问。我猜是哪个危险的囚犯吧。\
**Lopera**: I have no idea. We're soldiers, we "follow orders, no questions." As my father would say.

**洛佩拉**：前阵子河水淹了地牢，可能是把一些犯人转移到这里来了。\
**Lopera**: With all the flooding we've had, they probably shoved everything they wanted to keep safe and dry in there.

**莫莉德尔**：洛佩拉！\
**Moldir**: Lopera!

寻找着妹妹的副官女士从身后赶到，为这场小小的“意外”冒险划上句号。\
Moldir rushes from behind, putting an end to their little "accidental" adventure.

**莫莉德尔**：你带错地方了，塔楼不是客人们的住所。\
**Moldir**: You get lost on your way to the guest rooms, Pera? You know better than to be here.

**莫莉德尔**：请回房间吧，外面停靠的那艘游轮明早就出发。\
**Moldir**: Your ship will be leaving early tomorrow morning. Please return to your rooms and get some rest.

**莫莉德尔**：请不要在基地闲逛，尤其是没有守卫的地方。\
**Moldir**: This is a military base, not an amusement park. Please, do not wander about, especially near restricted areas.

**维尔汀**：一切听您安排，麻烦了。\
**Vertin**: My apologies, Lieutenant. Perhaps you could point us in the right direction?

回望棕色高塔，门边的柠檬树结满了酸涩多汁的果实，陈旧的兽血术阵在阳光下显出暗色。\
She steals one more look at the tower as they leave. The fruits on the lemon trees are plump and juicy. The old beast-blood array appears dark in the sunlight.

木门露出缝隙。阳光下，一只飞虫悄无声息地钻入塔楼。\
The wooden door creaks open a little, allowing an insect to fly in through the gap.

**？？？**：门怎么……松动了？\
**???**: The seal ... it's gone.

塔楼之内，唯一的囚犯偷偷听到了门外的对话：外面有艘船，明早会出发。\
Inside the tower, the sole prisoner has been quietly listening to their conversation: There's a ship leaving tomorrow morning.

听到人群走远，她小心地推了推门，意外发现门上的封印似乎不再生效了。\
As the footsteps trail off, she gently pushes the door. The seal is indeed gone. She's free.

## 8TH-04 离岸流 / Riptide

芝诺基地\
A journey always starts with a farewell.

出行前总是离别。

**莫莉德尔**：来，戴上这个，发生意外的时候我能找到你。\
**Moldir**: Here, put this on, Pera. It will allow me to track you should anything happen.

她将一枚小纽扣系到妹妹的衣领下。\
She fastens a small button to her sister's collar.

一枚纽扣将两人紧紧相连，以便陷入危机时，她们能及时向对方伸出援手。\
This button connects the two of them tightly. With this, they will always be able to find each other, no matter where they are.

而后，互相亲吻左右脸颊，以示告别。\
They kiss on both cheeks.

**莫莉德尔**：回来的时候，别忘了给父亲带礼物。\
**Moldir**: You'll remember to bring Father a souvenir this time, yes?

**莫莉德尔**：活得久一点，你要比我们活得都久。\
**Moldir**: And promise me you'll be careful. I do not wish for our Pera to "buy the farm" just yet.

**洛佩拉**：哼，还有叛徒没有追回来，我可不会死在他们前面。\
**Lopera**: Don't worry about me, Molly. Worry about them.

**洛佩拉**：等着吧，我会亲手把他们送上刑场，一个不留。\
**Lopera**: I'll kill them all, if I have to. Every last one.

一个不留。她在“姐姐”耳边特地强调一遍。\
She makes sure to emphasize the totality of her determination.

**红弩箭**：哈……我跟同志们道别的时候从来不会这么麻烦，打个招呼就走了。\
**Lilya**: Alright, alright, enough blabbering. Do you two always share these little heart-to-hearts whenever you leave? I got nothing to say 'cept "bye."

**红弩箭**：那才叫真正的芝诺速度呢。\
**Lilya**: Or is the tortoise suddenly not so worried about its speed?

基地外，轮船发出即将离港的信号。\
The ship signals its imminent departure.

**维尔汀**：苏芙比，东西都带齐了吗？\
**Vertin**: Sotheby, do we have everything?

**苏芙比**：哼哼，当然啦～这件事情从来都不需要担心！\
**Sotheby**: Naturally! Ms. Sotheby is always ready to travel!

**莫莉德尔**：船不会停靠太久，该出发了，各位。\
关于邓肯先生，这期间我会继续调查。\
**Moldir**: The ship is boarding now. After it departs, I will spend some time gathering intel on Mr. Duncan.

**维尔汀**：好的，麻烦您了。\
**Vertin**: Thank you.

**洛佩拉**：别担心，见到邓肯的时候我会帮你的。那老伙计……哈哈，我们认识很久了。\
**Lopera**: We should be able to find him in the flesh once we get to town. Duncan and I go way back, hahaha!

**洛佩拉**：城里还有一艘装在玻璃瓶里……会说话的船呢！\
**Lopera**: And I'll introduce you to another friend. She lives in a bottle.

**维尔汀**：我很愿意见到你的朋友们。\
**Vertin**: I'd be delighted to meet your friends.

**维尔汀**：好了，现在该出发了。\
**Vertin**: We should be going now.

**维尔汀**：红弩箭，麻烦你协助伊戈尔将军处理好基地的事。\
**Vertin**: Lilya, I've told Admiral Igor that he can rely on you for further assistance as necessary. Is that alright with you?

**红弩箭**：放心吧。\
**Lilya**: Yeah, I'll do whatever needs doing.

**红弩箭**：Счастливого пути!\
<一路顺风！>\
**Lilya**: Have a good trip!

送走司辰一行人后，副官女士回到将军的办公室 ，汇报昨晚发生的一场意外。\
Having seen off their guests, Lieutenant Moldir returns to the admiral's office to report an incident from the previous night.

**莫莉德尔**：将军，塔楼里的囚犯逃走了……\
**Moldir**: Admiral, a prisoner has gone missing from the tower.

副官女士低下头，尴尬地开口报告。\
She lowers her head as she awkwardly delivers her report.

**莫莉德尔**：应该没有其他人知道。\
**Moldir**: We'll make sure it's kept under wraps.

**莫莉德尔**：有人破坏了门上的封印。但目前暂不清楚是什么人协助她逃亡。\
**Moldir**: The seal was broken, and we're still investigating who might have been involved.

**莫莉德尔**：……昨天司辰、洛佩拉和苏芙比出现在了塔楼附近，但我不认为会是她们。\
**Moldir**: I did encounter the Timekeeper, Ms. Sotheby, and Lopera near the Tower yesterday. Still, I see no reason to suspect them.

副官女士想起了昨天在塔楼遇见的司辰一行人。\
They were the only people she saw near the tower yesterday.

**伊戈尔将军**：……\
**Admiral Igor**: ...

**伊戈尔将军**：司辰没有动机，而洛佩拉更不可能。\
**Admiral Igor**: The Timekeeper doesn't have any incentive, and Lopera—No, she wouldn't be involved.

塔楼里曾关押着一位不走运的囚犯——她是待宰的羊，是秋日的穗子，也是一位不巧溜走的逃犯。\
Until last night, the tower held a single unlucky prisoner—a lamb to the slaughter, a stalk of wheat in autumn. But now she has gotten away.

**伊戈尔将军**：派人去找，掌握行踪，但不急着抓捕。\
**Admiral Igor**: Find the prisoner, but don't attempt recapture. Let's see who she's been in touch with.

**莫莉德尔**：明白。\
**Moldir**: Understood.

**伊戈尔将军**：但我也不希望再有这类事件发生。\
**Admiral Igor**: Lieutenant, this was a failure that must not be repeated.

芝诺不该是这副样子。老将军咬紧下牙槽，紧盯地图，筹划着援军动向。\
He grits his teeth as he stares at the map before him. Zeno shouldn't be like this.

游轮出航，河道上不久就跟来了十几艘桨划艇。\
The ship departs, and before long, a dozen rowboats have surrounded it.

**苏芙比**：哇……他们要怎么上来呀？难道是……抛一根铁索，然后咻咻地爬上来吗！\
**Sotheby**: Oh, look at those strange cowboys! What are they doing with those hooks? Are they trying to hitch a ride?

**洛佩拉**：船上有铁钩，钩住船舷，然后就能过来了。\
**Lopera**: Yes, they will use those hooks to grab onto the side of the ship and moor their boats to ours.

像她说的：小船丢出钩索，扣紧游轮，小个儿的船贩们冒着激流冲打，手脚并用爬上甲板。\
Just as she said, the boats throw their hooks, latch onto the ship, and a number of people clamber aboard.

船贩热情贩售着自家做的小玩意儿，洛佩拉礼貌地一一将他们拒绝。\
They're traders hawking homemade trinkets. Lopera politely declines them all.

**洛佩拉**：司辰，你拿着这个。\
**Lopera**: Take this, Timekeeper.

**维尔汀**：这是？\
**Vertin**: What's this?

**洛佩拉**：地图而已，以防意外。\
**Lopera**: Just a map, in case we get separated.

她递来一张地图，标注着至少三条“安全线路”。\
The map is marked with at least three "safe routes."

**洛佩拉**：地图只会告诉你码头跟荣军院在哪儿，但不会告诉你哪条路才是安全的。\
**Lopera**: This will show you the way from the harbor to the Veterans' Residence. Though, it can't show you the safest way. For that, you'll need me.

**洛佩拉**：圣保罗从没有什么地下秩序，正如这座城市绝不受跨国公司掌控——穿西装的骗子们都这么说。\
**Lopera**: But what am I saying? São Paulo is perfectly safe! That's what the politicians say anyways, never mind the talk of gangs, cartels, and greedy multinational corporations—pure slander.

**维尔汀**：谢谢，但我最好不要用上它。\
**Vertin**: Thank you for the warning, and the map. Let's hope I won't find any occasion to use it.

**洛佩拉**：希望如此。旅途愉快，欢迎前往圣保罗！\
**Lopera**: I hope so, too. Well, we have a long cruise ahead. I'll leave you to your business. See you.

她挥手道别，绕过四处奔跑的船贩，去往甲板另一端。\
She waves goodbye, making her way through the energetic traders and to the other side of the deck.

从她身旁窜过的船贩们像一群小老鼠，做了会儿买卖，就争抢着跑去向厨师讨饭。\
The traders scamper around like little mice. Having made their sales, they're now scrambling to get a plate of food from the chef.

**维尔汀**：船上居然还会分发食物……\
**Vertin**: So, the kitchen even prepares food for them.

**船厨**：小子，别插队，回你的位置！\
**Chef**: No line-cutting! You, boy, back to your place!

**船厨**：要么乖乖回后面去，要么今天就得饿着。\
**Chef**: Queue up, or there will be no dinner for you tonight!

厨师敲敲铁勺，把一个“不守规矩”的家伙赶回他该待的地方。\
The chef taps his metal spoon, sending the boy back to his place in the queue.

而这个少年趁他不备，抓起几张酵饼藏进旧衬衣，像偷食的老鼠，拔腿便跑。\
The boy sneakily grabs a few flatbreads, tucks them under his shirt, and scurries away.

**苏芙比**：唔——！\
**Sotheby**: Ah!

他撞上苏芙比，贴在肚子上的“赃物”和他一起被撞落到铁皮地板上。\
He bumps into Sotheby, crashing to the floor along with his "stolen goods."

**船贩小孩**：哎、哎呀，别挡路哇——！\
**Young Vendor**: Ei, out of my way!

他捡起饼，捂着肚子往甲板别处逃跑，灰色的眼睛里似乎闪烁着被神秘术诱导的气息。\
He stuffs the bread under his shirt again before running off. As he passes, Sotheby notices a glint of an arcane skill in his eyes.

他像是被吹笛人引诱的孩童，拔腿跑向一个舱室的一角……\
He runs like a child enchanted by the Rattenfanger as he bolts toward a corner of the cabin.

**苏芙比**：奇怪……维尔汀，那位小先生的状况好像不太好……\
**Sotheby**: Ms. Vertin? Did you notice that boy? Wasn't he awfully strange?

**维尔汀**：跟上看看。\
**Vertin**: You're right. Come on, let's go see what he's up to.

一位小姐躲藏在夏日的阴影中。\
A woman hides in the shadows.

那是张并不陌生的脸，却换上了一套崭新的衣服。\
Her face is familiar, but she wears an entirely new outfit.

真的是她吗？在蓝手帕旅馆有过一面之缘的……“老朋友”。\
Is it really her? The lady at Tuesday's Motel?

**维尔汀**：是你？\
**Vertin**: It's you!

偷饼的孩子不见了。\
The bread-stealing child is gone.

角落里的女郎蜷着身子，手嘴并用，大口吞咽着食物。\
Instead, Ms. Kimberly is curled up in the corner, stuffing bread into her mouth with both hands.

她停下来，看向这边，眼神中满是惊讶。\
She stops and looks up, surprise in her eyes.

**金伯利女郎**：唔？！维尔汀……？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Mm?! Oh, Vertin?

**金伯利女郎**：为什么……你也在这儿？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: How—What are you doing here?

**维尔汀**：我想这句话应该我来问。\
**Vertin**: I was about to ask you the very same question.

上个月在蓝手帕旅馆的“道别”并不愉快。\
The farewell at Tuesday's Motel last month wasn't exactly pleasant.

但她现在看起来饿坏了。\
But she looks starved now.

**苏芙比**：这是你的新朋友吗？\
**Sotheby**: Is this a new friend, Vertin? A pleasure to meet you!

苏芙比好奇地凑上来，看着一脸惊恐的金伯利小姐——她愣住了，嘴角掉出一块黏糊糊的面团。\
Sotheby approaches, but Kimberly looks terrified. She freezes, a sticky lump of dough dropping from the corner of her mouth.

**维尔汀**：一起吃吧。\
**Vertin**: Please, take this.

一根可可点心棒也许能帮上她。犹豫几秒后，她咽了咽口水，抢进嘴里啃起来。\
She offers her a chocolate bar. After a moment's hesitation, Kimberly swallows, grabs the bar, and shoves it into her mouth.

**金伯利女郎**：谢、谢谢……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Th-Thank you ...

金伯利像只饿坏了的松鼠，连手指上的每根毛都舔得干干净净。\
She licks her fingers clean like a ravenous child.

游轮

**维尔汀**：你找到弄丢的东西了吗？\
**Vertin**: Have you found what you lost since we last met?

**金伯利女郎**：……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: ...

她脸色低沉，看来还没找到。\
Her face falls. It appears not.

**维尔汀**：这件事我或许能帮上点忙。\
**Vertin**: Perhaps I could help.

**金伯利女郎**：谢谢，不过我想我自己能摆平。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Thank you, but I would prefer to do this on my own.

**金伯利女郎**：自己丢的东西我会自己找到的。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I was the one who lost it, and I will be the one to get it back.

她不太愿意合作，但也没有敌意。\
She's unwilling to cooperate, but there's no hostility.

一个形迹古怪而矛盾的人儿，一位似乎在重塑边缘惶然的神秘学家。\
A strange and contradictory figure, an arcanist who seems to be on the verge of reformation.

**维尔汀**：我们要去圣保罗，要不要一起？\
**Vertin**: This ship is headed to São Paulo. Is that where you're heading as well? Would you like to accompany us?

**金伯利女郎**：圣保罗？我不去那儿……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: São Paulo? I don't ...

可圣保罗是这艘船唯一的目的地。她还能去哪儿？\
It's the ship's only destination. Where else could she go?

**金伯利女郎**：那儿没什么值得去的。圣保罗，一个穷鬼扎堆的城市罢了。没有舞会，没有盛宴，什么也没有。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: There isn't anything for me there. Only a pit of misery and pain. There's no more dancing, no feasts or banquets. No—

她眼神躲闪。\
Her eyes dart away.

“那儿什么也没有”。\
"There's nothing there."

**金伯利女郎**：再见！看在点心的份上，再见！维尔汀，祝你旅途愉快！我欠你一个小小的人情。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: No, I would rather we simply part ways here, Ms. Vertin! Farewell, and pleasant journeys—I'm indebted to you for your kindness.

**金伯利女郎**：对了，你的朋友穿得真像一个美味的小蛋糕。她看起来……很可口。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Ah, and your friend here ... Aren't you just a sweetheart? Oh, I could just gobble you up for tea!

她看向苏芙比，突然伸出手捏捏她的脸。\
She reaches out and pinches Sotheby's cheek.

**苏芙比**：哇啊——！这不可以、你这样子……这样是很不符合淑女的礼仪的～！\
**Sotheby**: Ah! Madam, please. You ... This simply isn't proper or ladylike.

她笑了笑，仿佛抛掉了相遇前的所有境遇，消失在游人之中。\
Kimberly smiles, as if she has shed the baggage of their previous encounter, and disappears into the crowd.

而在沙漠半岛的传说里，遇见恶魔，总是坏事即将到来的预兆。\
There's an old legend told in the desert peninsula: encountering a demon is always a sign of bad things to come.

## 8TH-05 地狱之船 / Waterway to Hell

游轮\
The wind blows through Lopera's hair.

风穿过少女的指缝。

外国游客聚集在船舷边，看向那些划着小艇靠近游轮的当地住民。\
The tourists gather at the ship's edge, watching the locals in small boats approaching the cruise ship.

**轮船游客**：他们从没关心过圣保罗的穷人，像给动物园的猴子投喂香蕉，打发一点“善心”。\
**Cruise Passenger**: A few treats to buy their worship. And they call it "kindness." How undignified, to be reduced to begging for scraps like a dog.

船上小孩挥舞双手，发出喊叫吸引游客注意。\
The children on the boats wave their hands and shout in an attempt to attract the tourists' attention.

船员与随船牧师打包好了可供抛掷的施舍物，兜售给每一位乐意参与这一“游赏项目”的客人。\
The crew and onboard priest have packed supplies for the tourists to buy and throw to the impoverished children—all part of the tour experience.

**洛佩拉**：这些“香蕉”养活了不少人，朋友。吃饱饭比什么都要紧，管他是哪来的饭，反正拉出来都一样。\
**Lopera**: Dignity doesn't count for much in the face of hunger.

陌生游客点点头，但他似乎并不完全同意这一点。\
The stranger nods, though he doesn't seem to completely agree.

**轮船游客**：人不单靠食物活着。\
**Cruise Passenger**: Yet no man can live by bread alone.

**洛佩拉**：人不靠食物就没法活着。\
**Lopera**: And yet none can live without it.

**轮船游客**：您也去圣保罗做买卖吗？我在贫民区有些生意。\
**Cruise Passenger**: You're a clever girl, Miss. But I hear from your accent you are no local. So, what brings you to São Paulo? Business, right? I have some business myself in the favelas.

**洛佩拉**：买卖？不，我回家，到圣保罗那间荣军院，如果你在城里找不到住处，朋友，上那儿来，我帮你。\
**Lopera**: Colombia, sir, and no, only a visit. To the São Paulo Veterans' Residence. It's a safe place. If you find yourself in trouble, you should seek it out.

**轮船游客**：感谢您的好意。\
**Cruise Passenger**: Oh, is it now? Thank you. You're very kind to offer.

洛佩拉托着下巴，无聊地抛掷着小骰子，投起又落下，落下再投起……\
Lopera idly tosses a small die up in the air and catches it in her hand again.

游客的目光随骰子上下晃动。\
The stranger's eyes follow the die as it traces its path.

**轮船游客**：要来玩一把吗，女士？\
**Cruise Passenger**: Care for a game of dice, little lady?

**洛佩拉**：赌注是什么？\
**Lopera**: What's the bet?

她瞄向游客手边的黑色旅行箱。\
She glances at the black suitcase by the stranger's feet.

**轮船游客**：赌你我的善心吧。\
**Cruise Passenger**: Well, let us bet against the goodness in one another.

**轮船游客**：输的人为孩子们买下这艘船的施舍。\
**Cruise Passenger**: Let us say that the loser will cover the cost of all the food given to all the little vendors today,

**轮船游客**：然后，以赢家的名义布施。\
**Cruise Passenger**: in the winner's name, of course.

一场慷慨的赌局，为了叩响天上门扉的良心。\
A generous gamble for a conscience that knocks on heaven's door.

**洛佩拉**：你这人还挺有意思。那来吧，飞——\
**Lopera**: That's no small wager, sir. Still, I appreciate a good game.

陌生的客人微笑着摊开双手，看着骰子从洛佩拉手中掷出，又像雨滴般落回桌面，在木杯里摇晃。\
The stranger smiles as he watches Lopera drop the die on the table and shake it in the wooden cup.

**洛佩拉**：你先还是我先？一二三小，四五六大。\
**Lopera**: High-low then? Who goes first?

**轮船游客**：您请。\
**Cruise Passenger**: Ladies first.

**洛佩拉**：小。\
**Lopera**: Low.

**轮船游客**：六。否则都算您赢。\
**Cruise Passenger**: Let's make it more interesting. 6. If it rolls anything else, you win.

木杯再一次晃起，一枚“不体面”的骰子旋转着，将胜利带给其主人。\
She shakes the cup again, the die unevenly tumbling around inside.

**轮船游客**：请。\
**Cruise Passenger**: Do you mind?

**轮船游客**：看来我输了，是神有意让我为他不幸的孩子们做点什么。\
**Cruise Passenger**: I lost, just as was meant to be. So then, I am to be the vehicle of grace today.

收浮窗

**轮船游客**：请告诉我您的名字，以便为孩子们布施时能让天园响唱起您的名字。\
**Cruise Passenger**: Might I have your name, Miss? So that all may know the name, which is to be sung in paradise today.

**洛佩拉**：卡洛塔·洛佩兹·里维拉，但如果你要找我，就打听“洛佩拉”。\
**Lopera**: Carlotta Lopez Rivera. But it is "Lopera" should you ask after me.

洛佩拉，圣保罗的洛佩拉。\
Lopera. Lopera of São Paulo.

落败的游客拿起骰子，笑着察觉到了异状。\
The defeated stranger picks up the die. He notices something in its design and cracks a smile.

赌局的落败者握住胜利之人的手，将那枚不光彩的骰子交还给它的主人。\
He places it in Lopera's hand.

**轮船游客**：您有一枚非常有趣的骰子。\
**Cruise Passenger**: That's an interesting die you have there.

**洛佩拉**：这只是运——\
**Lopera**: It was only luck—

**洛佩拉**：怎么回事——\
**Lopera**: What's going on?

**河盗**：都照我说的做！\
**River Pirate**: Do as I say! All of you!

**苏芙比**：喔！他们是——是河上的“鳄鱼牛仔”吗？！\
**Sotheby**: Look, Vertin! There are some more "river cowboys" over there!

**维尔汀**：不，他们是强盗……\
**Vertin**: I'm afraid they seem more like river pirates.

**维尔汀**：苏芙比，退后！\
**Vertin**: Stay back, Sotheby!

**维尔汀**：你想要什么？\
**Vertin**: What do you want?

**河盗**：告诉船长，把船开到贫民区。\
**River Pirate**: Where's the captain? We're changing destinations. This ship will be docking in the favela now.

**河盗**：否则就等着大伙儿一起上天吧！\
**River Pirate**: Or we'll blow it all to bits!

他擦响打火机，在炸药引线边燎烧，发出威胁。他很慌张，在恐惧着什么。\
He flicks a lighter and lights the fuse of an explosive. He's panicked. Clearly, he's afraid of something.

**洛佩拉**：——都让开！！\
**Lopera**: Get out of the way!!

比船长来得更快的，是已经拔枪的洛佩拉。\
Lopera has already drawn her guns.

但混乱的人群挡在前方，她没法扣动扳机。\
But the crowd is panicking. She can't get a clear shot.

**维尔汀**：洛佩拉，不能在这开枪！\
**Vertin**: Hold your fire, Lopera!

**维尔汀**：当心油桶！\
**Vertin**: There are oil drums on board!

洛佩拉这才注意到人群身后堆放着的油桶。稍有不慎，整艘船就会被炸成圣保罗明早的报纸头条。\
Lopera notices the oil drums stacked behind the crowd. A single mistake could turn the whole ship into tomorrow's headline in the São Paulo papers.

**洛佩拉**：啧——耍花招的玩意儿。\
**Lopera**: Ah, slimy rats.

于是她收起枪，徒手冲上去。\
She holsters her guns and charges forward with her bare fists.

洛佩拉与暴徒扭打成一块儿，一拳一拳砸向对方鼻梁。\
Lopera grapples with the thug before wrestling him to the ground and punching him repeatedly in the nose.

她扯下暴徒身上缠绕的炸药，却也因此被夺走了枪。\
She tears the explosives off the pirate's body, but in that brief moment, the thug manages to pull one of her guns from its holster.

**维尔汀**：洛佩拉！\
**Vertin**: Lopera!

战斗忽然停了下来，暴徒的手颤抖着，将枪口指向洛佩拉——而她身后不远，就是油桶。\
The fight halts, the thug's trembling hand pointing the gun at Lopera. The oil drums are just a few steps away.

**河盗**：把船开到贫民区！否则一起去死！\
**River Pirate**: Either we go to the favela, or to the bottom of the river, clear? Make your call!

**洛佩拉**：贫民区……是天使兄弟会又回来了吗？\
**Lopera**: The favela ... Are you with the Apostles Brotherhood?

**河盗**：……！\
**River Pirate**: ...?!

**洛佩拉**：他们胁迫了你，对不对？\
**Lopera**: They forced you into doing this, didn't they?

**洛佩拉**：“去劫持今天的游轮，然后把船开过来。”\
**Lopera**: "Hijack the ship and bring it to us." Is that right?

**洛佩拉**：我能想到那些混账对你说了什么，但很遗憾，“短吻鳄”号今天的目的地是圣保罗。\
**Lopera**: Too bad for you. This ship won't be making any unplanned detours today.

河盗瞪大眼，双腿颤抖着愣在原地。\
The pirate's eyes widen as he freezes in place, only his legs trembling.

洛佩拉说中了，但对方却做出了过激的反应。\
Lopera hit the mark, but the thug's reaction is extreme.

那根骷髅般消瘦的手指摁住黑色扳机，牙齿打颤，在紧张中无意识地用力——\
His finger tightens on the trigger as his teeth chatter nervously.

开枪声

……\
...

**洛佩拉**：蠢货！！！\
**Lopera**: Stupid!!!

**洛佩拉**：趴下！\
**Lopera**: Get down!

特效-爆炸\
燃烧画面

子弹没有击中她，而是打进了不稳定的金属油桶。\
The bullet flies past her shoulder, instead piercing an oil drum behind her.

**洛佩拉**：爆轰弹？！\
**Lopera**: Blaze-busters?

首先是爆闪的火光，然后是响声和热风。附近的易燃物被爆炸接连引燃，火焰迅速蔓延。\
A blinding flash of light and a wave of heat hit them as the ship is quickly engulfed in flames.

油桶引爆的冲击让船只剧烈摇晃，爆炸撕裂了船体，轮船开始解体。河水涌入船舱。\
The ship lurches violently as the blast tears through the vessel, and water starts flooding into the hull.

**游客**：天哪！！！\
**Passenger**: Oh, my God!!!

**船厨**：救生艇！找救生艇！\
**Chef**: Lifeboats! Get to the lifeboats now!

**游客**：救救我……老天啊——！\
**Passenger**: God help us! This is hell!

所有人都慌张地逃向甲板前端，轮船被拦腰炸断，向着被油桶炸裂开的位置倾斜、沉没。\
Panic breaks out as the ship starts to split in half.

爆炸接连传来冲击，头脑一片空白。\
More explosions follow.

人群中没有看见金伯利的身影。\
There's no sign of Ms. Kimberly in the crowd.

**洛佩拉**：抓住栏杆！\
**Lopera**: Hold the railings! Stay on the deck!

洛佩拉大口呛着河水，在水中起伏。她抱紧一块浮木，发来遥远的呼喊。\
Lopera shouts from the water as she clings to a piece of floating wood. She gasps for air as she bobs up and down in the water.

重力将所有人拽向河心的漩涡，更多的甲板被淹没了。\
Chairs, benches, and sailing gear disappear as the ship sinks further and further into the depths of the river.

苏芙比紧紧握住甲板护栏，但船只几乎要整个儿竖着沉下去了。\
Sotheby clutches the guardrail tightly, but the ship is almost vertical and sinking fast.

**维尔汀**：苏芙比！往洛佩拉那儿跳！\
**Vertin**: Let go, Sotheby! You need to jump now! Join Lopera!

落水的人们，悬空的人们。尖叫着的人们。在濒临死亡的险境中，眼前的一切都变得很远。\
Screams fill the air as the tourists cling on for dear life, watching their friends and family hurtle toward the river.

像烂熟的橙子一样，游人松开被烧得滚烫的支撑物，掉进河里。\
Like overripe oranges, one by one, they lose their grip and plunge into the depths.

**苏芙比**：维尔汀——！\
**Sotheby**: Vertin!

火焰舔过金属护栏，融化了船上的劣质建材。爆炸引起耳鸣。\
Flames lick the guardrails, melting the ship's cheap materials. The explosions ring in her ears.

苏芙比闭上眼睛，跳向朝她游来的洛佩拉，落入水中。\
Sotheby closes her eyes and flings herself toward Lopera.

但她很幸运，同伴迅速抓住她的手，将她搂向自己那块木板。\
Lucky for her, Lopera quickly grabs her hand and pulls her onto the wooden plank.

特效-爆炸

**苏芙比**：快去救维尔汀！！她……\
**Sotheby**: Somebody, please get her! She's still ...

“她”还在船上。

视频-维尔汀落水\
"She" is still on the ship.

轮船在最后一声爆炸中彻底解体。\
With one final explosion, the ship is obliterated entirely.

河水淹没了眼前的一切。\
The river swallows everything.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

金色的阳光在水面摇荡，变得越来越远……\
The sunlight ripples on the surface, growing farther and farther away.

谁的手？\
Whose hand is that?

**？？？**：你可不能死在这儿……\
**???**: Can't have you dying here.

**？？？**：为什么呢，一遇到你总会发生这样的事情……\
**???**: *sigh* Why do we keep meeting in these awkward situations?

**？？？**：——可可点心棒，还给你了。\
**???**: Consider my debt paid.

视频关闭

## 8TH-06 杰出演员 / Tender Pretender

河岸

**加莱亚诺**：前阵子兄弟会被芝诺的人揍了一顿，老兄，我觉得这是个机会。他们现在全散了。\
**Galeno**: The Brotherhood just took a beating from Zeno. If they're caught up with their own trouble, then we might have a golden opportunity to turn the people against them.

**加莱亚诺**：不能再让更多的人被他们骗走。\
**Galeno**: We can't lose anyone else to their lies.

波纹\
The old man next to him casts his fishing line. The bobber floats quietly on the river's surface. Across the river, a water anaconda eyes the two men beneath the shadow of a snakewood tree.

老人甩出鱼钩，浮标静静漂在河面。他在等待鱼饵咬钩。河对岸，水蚺盘绕在蛇纹木下，窥伺两人。

**加莱亚诺**：你怎么看？商量商量行动？\
**Galeno**: What do you say? Wanna talk about plans?

老人没有言语，而是摘下墨镜，把杯子推给朋友。\
The old man doesn't speak. Instead, he removes his sunglasses and pushes a cup toward his friend.

**？？？**：先来一杯。\
**???**: Here. Drink up.

**加莱亚诺**：我不介意多来几杯。但是朋友，这是什么意思啊？\
**Galeno**: Thanks. Listen, as much as I enjoy being out here all day ... We've got to take action now. The sooner, the better, don't you think?

年轻人接过酒杯，照着朋友的话一口喝光了酒。\
The young man takes the glass and downs it in one gulp, as his friend suggested.

**？？？**：加莱亚诺呀！不要着急，哈哈！\
**???**: Haha, hold your horses, young Galeno!

**？？？**：如果我现在给你一拳，你可能会疼个好几天。\
**???**: Let me explain—say, I throw a punch at you now, really hit you good, what next?

**？？？**：然后，你就会叫上几个表兄，提着从迭戈上校那儿租的汤普森冲锋枪，敲开我家的门。\
**???**: Maybe you'll storm off at first, but then, you round up your cousins, maybe grab that Tommy gun you borrowed from Colonel Tiago.

**邓肯先生**：“你完了，混账邓肯！”\
**Mr. Duncan**: Then you'll find me, all alone, and say, "You're done, you old fart!"

**邓肯先生**：突突突——\
**Mr. Duncan**: !@#$%^%^&*...

老人笑起来，两只手比划着枪支射击的动作。\
The old man laughs, mimicking shooting with his hands.

**邓肯先生**：如果我真的揍了你，请记住，老邓肯永远忠于他的朋友，他一定有不得不这么做的原因。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Hahahaha! I'm not gonna harm you, kid. And if I ever do, remember that old Duncan must have his reasons and he'd never harm a friend intentionally.

**加莱亚诺**：这话什么意思？\
**Galeno**: What is all that supposed to mean?

**邓肯先生**：洛佩拉带人“揍了他们一拳”，现在兄弟会一定还在疼呢。但小心点，等他们缓过来，贫民区还会有麻烦。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Ha, I'm rambling. I mean, true enough that Lopera hit them hard, and we both know that the Brotherhood will aim to settle that score, and they won't wait long. But if we don't play this smart, it'll only cause them to lash out more.

**邓肯先生**：被兄弟会骗走和掳走的年轻人，你见过哪个回来的吗？\
**Mr. Duncan**: Still, we do have to consider one thing: those who chose to follow them never come back.

**加莱亚诺**：没有、一个也没有……连是生是死都不知道。\
**Galeno**: No, they don't.

**邓肯先生**：带剩下的人加入芝诺吧，他们能对付兄弟会。如果要乘凉，大伙儿就该找一棵靠得住的大树。\
**Mr. Duncan**: So, let's seize the day, grab opportunity by the horns, and maybe we stop losing more of our friends to those bastards. Right now, seems to me that Zeno is our best bet.

年轻人思考片刻，认同了他的看法。\
The young man considers this proposition.

**加莱亚诺**：不错，兄弟会现在快完蛋了，去芝诺当兵，是个好想法。\
**Galeno**: That just might work, old man. With the Brotherhood falling apart, Zeno will start to look pretty good to folks here.

**邓肯先生**：但现在别着急，年轻人，你看，现在河上静得连片叶子都没有。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Ah, but not so fast, kid! We need a little patience. Let the line out a little first.

**邓肯先生**：钓鱼之前，咱们得先预备好装鱼的塑料袋。\
**Mr. Duncan**: If you fail to prepare, you're prepared to fail.

波纹\
The bobber twitches.

红色浮漂动了动。

**邓肯先生**：咬了！咬了——！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Got it! Excellent!

老人激动地站起身子，抓稳鱼竿，跟水里看不见的敌人搏斗。\
The old man jumps to his feet, reeling his fishing rod and fighting the unseen enemy in the water.

**邓肯先生**：这下你跑不掉了！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Aw! Don't think you could get away from me!

鱼线直直扎下河面，老人的鱼竿已经扭成了一道圆满的月弧。\
The fishing line plunges down into the river, the rod bending into a crescent.

**邓肯先生**：好啊，你要跟我比力气！看看我俩谁更有劲儿！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Ah! You like to wrestle, huh? Alright, let's see who gets the upper hand!

拖拽

**邓肯先生**：我这条老狗……可不会……输给……\
**Mr. Duncan**: Old Duncan is not about to lose a battle to—

**邓肯先生**：年轻人呀！啊哈！\
**Mr. Duncan**: A fish! Hahahaha!

一只巨大的胖气球鱼，通体透明，比他从前见过的任何一只都更大。\
It's a giant puffpuff fish, larger than any he's seen before.

**加莱亚诺**：老天呀，它肚子鼓得这么大！\
**Galeno**: Wow! Do you see the size of its belly?! It's huge!

半透明的鱼肚子里，漂浮着一个大大的绿色小蛋糕。\
What looks like a large green cake is floating inside its translucent belly.

**邓肯先生**：哈哈，吃了一个小家伙的大鱼？这条河还能给咱们弄点什么怪东西？\
**Mr. Duncan**: Haha, what a deal! Catch one, get one free! How generous, Mother River.

**邓肯先生**：圣母保佑，还好她让我俩遇到了。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Alright, jokes aside, Galeno. Come on, help me get her out.

老邓肯抽出短刀，剖开鱼肚子。\
Old Duncan pulls out a knife and slices open the fish's belly.

爆出\
His catch bursts like a balloon, releasing air, water, and … a girl.

他的渔获就像一个爆开的气球，流出空气、水和水中的女孩儿……

**加莱亚诺**：啧啧……除了鱼，你这老家伙真是什么都能钓到……\
**Galeno**: This has got to be the strangest thing you've ever fished out from the river!

上游\
Another castaway floats downstream.

游泳

从上游又漂来另一位落难者。

**洛佩拉**：邓肯……！嘿！邓肯！\
**Lopera**: Duncan, Duncan!

岸边\
Across the river, the water anaconda locks onto its target, slipping into the water and swimming toward her.

蛇靠近

静候在蛇纹木之下的捕猎者盯上了她，抢先滑入水中，朝落难者游近。

**加莱亚诺**：邓肯，不对劲，有条蛇过去了！\
**Galeno**: Duncan, look! She's got an anaconda chasing after her!

水蚺以“Z”字动作游向猎物。\
The water anaconda zigzags toward its prey.

岸边

**邓肯先生**：好呀，那儿还躲着个坏家伙。\
**Mr. Duncan**: I saw it. Don't you worry.

老邓肯放下湿淋淋的女孩，举起吹笛，对准目标——\
Old Duncan sets the soaked girl down before lifting a blowpipe and aiming at the snake.

咻咻。\
*whoosh*

上游\
The dart strikes, quickly draining the anaconda of its strength. It sinks to the riverbed like a coil of old rope.

中箭

中箭的爬行动物迅速失去力气，像一团麻绳，慢慢沉下水底。

**邓肯先生**：洛佩拉！再坚持一会儿，朝这儿游！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Hang in there, Lopera! Come this way, we'll get you!

**邓肯先生**：接住——！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Here! Take it!

波纹\
He grabs a nearby vine and throws it into the water. Lopera grabs it and pulls herself toward the shore.

他抛出一根荨麻藤，落水的友人抓住这根长藤，游向岸边。

上岸

**洛佩拉**：……多谢了，老伙计！\
**Lopera**: Thank goodness you were here to grab me.

她踩着湿泥攀上岸，甩甩脑袋，双手撑地坐下，长长地舒了几口气。\
She clambers onto the shore, shakes the water from her hair, and sits leaning back on her hands, breathing heavily.

**洛佩拉**：但你怎么……会在这儿？你不是在荣军院？\
**Lopera**: But what are you doing all the way out here?

**邓肯先生**：这话得我问你……你怎么从河上漂来的？还有她，鱼肚子里冒出个人，怎么回事？\
**Mr. Duncan**: I was wondering the same thing about you, girl. Seems like a strange place for a swim. I suppose you wouldn't know anything about the girl we just fished out over there?

老邓肯指向从鱼肚子里滚出的小女孩。\
He points to the little girl who rolled out of the fish's belly.

**洛佩拉**：苏芙比！\
**Lopera**: Sotheby!

靠近\
She's still breathing. The air trapped in the fish's belly must have saved her life.

她有呼吸。鱼腹中储存的空气意外救了她一命。\
Lopera crawls over to her companion and smacks her back, helping her spit out the water in her lungs.

洛佩拉爬向同伴，抱住她的后背，帮她倒出口腹中的积水。

**洛佩拉**：嘿，醒醒！\
**Lopera**: Hey, can you hear me?

**邓肯先生**：轻点儿，洛佩拉。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Easy now, Lopera! We just cut her out of that fish's belly.

苏芙比咳出河水，慢慢苏醒。\
Sotheby coughs out the water in her lungs as she regains consciousness.

**邓肯先生**：上帝保佑呀，你运气不错，孩子，那条鱼肚子里没装满水。\
**Mr. Duncan**: You're a veritable Jonah, aren't you?

**苏芙比**：唔……嗯？\
**Sotheby**: Mm ... Hmm?

一张熟悉的脸，在水中模糊着，像透过雨幕看见的世界。\
A familiar face appears in her blurred vision.

**苏芙比**：我梦到一条大鱼，好大好大……\
**Sotheby**: I-I dreamt of a very, very big fish.

**苏芙比**：它的肚子变成了天空……呼吸很难受……\
**Sotheby**: And I was in its belly. It was as wide as the sky. I couldn't breathe.

**苏芙比**：可是……卡森先生……？\
**Sotheby**: A terribly strange dream, Mr. Karson.

**邓肯先生**：她醒了！\
**Mr. Duncan**: She's awake!

**苏芙比**：卡森先生？！\
**Sotheby**: Mr. Karson?!

相框中的人来到了眼前。她愣住了。\
This is him. The man from the photograph is standing before her. She freezes.

**苏芙比**：你……为什么……\
**Sotheby**: You ... How ...

模糊视野的积水一点点散开。靠近自己的这张脸变得陌生又熟悉。\
The water slowly clears from her vision. The face before her is both familiar and strange.

熟悉却陌生。\
She knows it, yet she doesn't.

**苏芙比**：这儿脏兮兮的……这儿……那儿……天哪……\
**Sotheby**: There's a little dirt on me. Here, and on the collar, too. Oh, goodness.

**苏芙比**：我怎么会……唔……这……\
**Sotheby**: Why am I here? I ... What ...

“卡森管家”换了身衣服，出现在身旁，惊醒了她。\
"Mr. Karson" kneels beside her. But he's wearing some very odd clothes.

**苏芙比**：卡森先生！真的是你吗！\
**Sotheby**: Could it really be you, Mr. Karson?

**邓肯先生**：卡森？你肯定认错了，小淑女，我不知道什么卡森先生。我是邓肯。你说对吧，洛佩拉？\
**Mr. Duncan**: Karson? You must be mistaken, little lady. My name is Duncan. I'm a friend of Lopera.

**洛佩拉**：苏芙比，这老家伙是邓肯，荣军院的邓肯，我认识他很久了。\
**Lopera**: That's right. Sotheby, this is Duncan from the Veterans' Residence. We've known each other for a long time.

**洛佩拉**：你认错人了。\
**Lopera**: You must be confusing him with someone else.

**邓肯先生**：先起来吧，孩子。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Now, up on your feet, little lady.

站起\
He takes her arm and pulls her out of the mud.

邓肯先生伸手握住她的胳膊，一把将小淑女提出河岸的软泥堆。

**苏芙比**：哇，吓了我一跳——！\
**Sotheby**: *gasp* Mr. Karson!

**苏芙比**：卡森先生……你刚才突然拽了我一下……\
**Sotheby**: Oh, sorry! It's just, I didn't expect you to suddenly pull my arm.

**邓肯先生**：原谅我，小姐，我就是个贫民区的老头子。做事就这么直接。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Pardon me, little lady. We tend to be very straightforward here in the favela.

**苏芙比**：不，不不不！我不明白，一个和卡森先生长得一样的人，为什么会不是卡森先生？\
**Sotheby**: It's quite alright. Only—No, no, no, I just don't understand! You look exactly like Mr. Karson; how could you be anyone else?

**苏芙比**：但你确实……你的、你的——\
**Sotheby**: Except for your attire, and those shoes ...

不同的装扮。严肃的庄园管家绝不会穿成这样——脚上绝不会不穿袜子，衣服上绝不会出现补丁。\
Her butler would never dress like this, sockless with patched-up clothing.

她看到杯子里摇晃的深色液体。\
She notices the liquid swirling in his cup.

**苏芙比**：酒……？\
**Sotheby**: And the liquor?

不，庄园管家绝不会带着含有酒精或兴奋水的饮料来见他的大小姐。\
No, her butler would never drink in front of the lady of the house.

她决定再做一个大胆的猜测——小淑女跳起来，紧张地伸手握住邓肯先生的衬衣。\
Sotheby decides to take a bold guess. She jumps up and nervously grabs Mr. Duncan's shirt.

**邓肯先生**：你生气了吗，孩子？也许你不喜欢看到老人喝酒，加莱亚诺，帮我拿下杯子——\
**Mr. Duncan**: Oh, pardon me, little miss. Are you not comfortable with us drinking? Galeno, put the cup away for me, please.

**苏芙比**：这、这样很不淑女！卡森先生！你都忘了吗！《淑女的原则》，我、我违背了……！\
**Sotheby**: No, I only meant ... Mr. Karson, it truly seems as though you've forgotten everything! Oh, but I'm being terribly unladylike.

她语无伦次。\
She rambles incoherently.

粗鲁的行为，不符合《淑女的原则》，但对方却不为所动。\
This behavior is totally against The Lady's Code of Conduct, yet "Mr. Karson" remains utterly unfazed.

**苏芙比**：但是……但是……卡森先生……邓肯先生……你……\
**Sotheby**: Still, you-you don't seem to mind at all.

她收到的只是对方无尽的困惑。最终，她泄气了，低下头，双手却还挂在“卡森”先生的衬衣衣角上。\
Growing increasingly confused, Sotheby lowers her head, still clutching the hem of "Mr. Karson's" shirt.

**邓肯先生**：听起来，他一定是一位对你来说特别重要的人。他是不是和我长得很像？\
**Mr. Duncan**: I must be a dead-ringer for this guy to have gotten you all flustered, little miss. Seems like you cared very deeply for this Mr. Karson?

**苏芙比**：你们……真的不是同一个人吗？\
**Sotheby**: Yes, I did. So, then, you really aren't him?

推镜头

**邓肯先生**：哈哈，没关系，如果我跟你的这位朋友很像。你可以把我当作他，我愿意为你扮演他。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Sorry to disappoint, little lady. But I'm flattered by the resemblance. Maybe I can be your friend too. In fact, feel free to call me Karson—why not? A rose by any other name, eh?

老人与她拉钩约定。\
The old man hooks his pinky with Sotheby's and presses his thumb firmly against hers.

**苏芙比**：卡森先生……\
**Sotheby**: Mr. Karson ...

**邓肯先生**：我理解失去的感受，我失去了爱人，也失去了已故战友嘱咐我照顾的女儿。\
**Mr. Duncan**: I know how hard it can be. I lost my wife, and my comrade-in-arms. I even managed to lose his daughter, after I promised to take care of her.

**邓肯先生**：她要是还健在，也该跟你一个年纪了，孩子。\
**Mr. Duncan**: She'd have been just about your age.

**邓肯先生**：心中有一位想见却永远见不到的人，我理解这种痛苦，孩子。\
**Mr. Duncan**: I'm rambling again. I suppose what I'm saying is, I know what it feels like to lose someone you love.

她怅惘着，不知道怎么样才是正确的。但她仍然抵住老人的手指，似乎和他达成了一个小小的约定。\
She looks lost, unsure of what to think, but she still holds onto the old man's hand, seemingly making a small promise with him.

现在，环顾四周，苏芙比发现少了一位重要的伙伴。\
Looking around, Sotheby realizes someone important is missing.

**苏芙比**：呀，糟糕了。维尔汀、我和维尔汀走丢了……我们得把她救回来！\
**Sotheby**: Oh, no. But what about Ms. Vertin! We've lost her! Where could she be now? We must find her!

**洛佩拉**：先别着急，我们得想想办法。那该死的混蛋引爆了油桶，船沉了。\
**Lopera**: Slow down. We need to think things through first. Those knuckleheads blew up the entire ship.

通讯失败音

**洛佩拉**：通讯设备也都坏了。\
**Lopera**: Which means our comms belong to the caimans now.

一场意外把事情搅得一团糟。无法联络上司辰，甚至不知道她的生死。\
Everything's in disarray. There's no way to contact the Timekeeper. They don't even know if she's alive.

**邓肯先生**：别担心，八二年我在内格罗河迷路的时候，情况比这糟得多。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Not to worry. I've been through worse! Back in '82, on the Rio Negro ... Oh, before I go rambling on again ...

**邓肯先生**：回“城”里去吧，相信邓肯！邓肯总有办法！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Let's head back to the city! Come on now. Trust good old Duncan.

**邓肯先生**：噢……不对，现在应该是卡森。很好，相信卡森吧！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Sorry, I mean Karson! Trust Karson to lead the way!

## 8TH-07 无端指控 / False Accusations

教堂\
A man in black lifts a fallen statue.

穿着黑衣的先生扶起圣像。

**？？？**：我从未想过让圣保罗陷入混乱。\
**???**: I've never wanted to put São Paulo through this chaos.

他护着掌心微弱的火花，将白蜡烛一盏盏重新点燃。\
He shields the faint flame in his hand, reigniting the candles one by one.

**？？？**：秩序，和平，服从。\
**???**: Order, peace, unity—those are my purposes.

**？？？**：马坎多，他们在这儿做了什么？\
**???**: Much has been wagered here, Marcando, much. Now, it has been lost.

**马坎多**：芝诺的人干的。该死，绝不能就这么算了！\
**Marcando**: Your Reverence, it was Zeno. Those animals! We'll make them pay for what they did!

**马坎多**：桑托斯阁下，恕我冒昧，我猜您一定也是为了这件事才来的。\
**Marcando**: Is that why you've decided to grace us with your presence, Your Reverence?

**马坎多**：我们的人被打散了不少，最近还来了个荣军院的医生。\
**Marcando**: There is a lot to do if we're going to recover the ground, we—I've lost, Your Reverence. And there's something more, a new doctor down at the Veterans' Residence.

**马坎多**：那女人是个瞎子，但她给很多人看病，替荣军院和芝诺笼络这儿的人。\
**Marcando**: Some blind woman. I would not bother you with it, Lord Santos. Except that she's been helping people in the favela and it is swaying them towards Zeno.

**桑托斯**：她是芝诺的人吗？\
**Santos**: Then this doctor is with Zeno?

**马坎多**：一定是的。她一直驻扎在荣军院里，和那群老混蛋亲近得很。\
**Marcando**: She must be. She's always at the Veterans' Residence—spends most of the day with those old war dogs.

马坎多表情紧张，不断擦拭着额头的汗水。\
His expression is tense as he mops the sweat from his forehead.

**桑托斯**：一位在贫民区很有影响力的军医，医术精湛，深受信赖。\
**Santos**: A doctor gaining the trust of the people in the favela? She'd make quite the prize, wouldn't you say, Marcando?

**桑托斯**：我想，她对芝诺的价值远大于几个被捕的逃兵。\
**Santos**: A much more valuable bargaining chip to Zeno than a few deserters.

马坎多明白了头领的意思——在圣保罗，绑架形同家常便饭。\
Marcando understands perfectly. In São Paulo, kidnappings are as common as bread.

**桑托斯**：这件事交给你去办，但在那之前……\
**Santos**: You will see this task through, Marcando. But before that ...

向前一步

**桑托斯**：马坎多，叫上我们最忠诚的朋友，去贫民区——我带来了新的力量。\
**Santos**: We need to pay a visit to the favela. I've brought us some new blood.

维修1

维修2

**邓肯先生**：就这样，看见了吗，把线缠两圈，然后红色的跟黑色的对齐，慢慢接上……\
**Mr. Duncan**: See? Just like this. Wrap the wire around it—better do it twice—and align the red and black, slowly.

老邓肯将铜线接在一块儿，电流“嗞——嗞——”发出声响。\
He delicately connects the copper wires and the current buzzes to life.

**苏芙比**：这真是不可思议……！\
**Sotheby**: Unbelievable!

**邓肯先生**：这就是科学，小子们。学会了吗？科学的力量！\
**Mr. Duncan**: It's science, kids. Nothing unbelievable about it.

他将修好的联络器还给洛佩拉。\
All fixed, he hands the communicator back to Lopera.

**洛佩拉**：帮大忙了，老家伙，还是你最可靠呀！\
**Lopera**: I don't know how to thank you, Duncan!

炼金师掰直天线，调试频道，联络基地汇报情况。\
She straightens the antenna, adjusts the channel, and hurriedly contacts the base to report the situation.

电话声

**莫莉德尔**：洛佩拉来的联络。\
**Moldir**: Admiral, Lopera just called in.

**伊戈尔将军**：接。\
**Admiral Igor**: Put her through.

**莫莉德尔**：洛佩拉，是我。发生什么了？\
**Moldir**: Lopera, it's me. What happened?

**洛佩拉**：游轮炸了，是意外。我和苏芙比漂到了贫民区。\
**Lopera**: Our ship was sunk. Ms. Sotheby and I washed ashore near the favelas.

**洛佩拉**：司辰……很糟糕，我不知道她去哪了，但愿没什么事。\
**Lopera**: As for the Timekeeper, she went overboard. We lost sight of her in the commotion. Her current status is unknown.

**莫莉德尔**：……！\
**Moldir**: ...?!

将军面无表情，抬起手指，示意副官女士追问情况。\
The admiral remains expressionless. He raises a finger, signaling Moldir to inquire further.

**莫莉德尔**：基地会立刻派人去搜救司辰，这件事交给我们。找到司辰后，她会被护送到荣军院。\
**Moldir**: We'll send people to find her and escort her to the Veterans' Residence.

**洛佩拉**：这儿的贫民区的年轻人想加入芝诺，他们害怕被报复，需要将军的承诺。\
**Lopera**: Additionally, Lieutenant, I have some fresh recruits eager to enroll with Zeno. But they will need the admiral's assurances that their families will be under our protection.

副官女士看向老将军。\
Moldir looks at the admiral.

将军点点头。他答应了。\
He nods in agreement.

**莫莉德尔**：父亲非常欢迎他们，芝诺很需要这样热情的年轻人。他们什么时候来？\
**Moldir**: They have it. What's their ETA?

**洛佩拉**：他们会立即出发。\
**Lopera**: They'll leave at once.

挂断电话

**莫莉德尔**：洛佩——\
**Moldir**: Pera ...

**莫莉德尔**：……唉，总是这么急。\
**Moldir**: *sigh* That little hothead.

**莫莉德尔**：父亲，现在怎么办？\
**Moldir**: Sir, your orders?

**伊戈尔将军**：司辰的事我会安排。\
**Admiral Igor**: Leave the matter to me, Moldir. I will send someone to take care of this.

副官女士不再追问，担忧地看着年迈的父亲。\
Moldir falls silent as she looks at her aging father, concern in her eyes.

老将军紧盯着手中的骰子——沉默在父女间无声地蔓延着。\
Silence spreads between father and daughter as the admiral focuses on the dice in his hand.

**加莱亚诺**：将军阁下怎么说？\
**Galeno**: What did the admiral say?

**洛佩拉**：他答应了！\
**Lopera**: He agreed!

**加莱亚诺**：好极了！\
**Galeno**: Did you hear that? Zeno will protect us!

一个值得庆祝的好消息，让年轻人兴奋地拍起手。\
Good news indeed. The young man claps his hands in excitement.

但人群中传来一阵响动。有人来了。\
But just as the celebration starts, it is cut abruptly short.

**洛佩拉**：果然是他们……船上的猜测是对的。\
**Lopera**: I have no doubt. They were working for the Brotherhood.

**邓肯先生**：啊，天使兄弟会，我还以为他们完蛋了……\
**Mr. Duncan**: The Apostles Brotherhood? They've bounced back quicker than I'd hoped.

向前走

**邓肯先生**：看看他们要干嘛。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Still, we'll need to be cautious. Figure out just what they're after.

**洛佩拉**：那家伙有点儿眼熟……\
**Lopera**: That guy looks familiar.

她看清了走在兄弟会队伍中的那位先生——是那位曾在船上遭遇的陌生人。\
It's the stranger she met on the ship—he's walking among the Brotherhood.

**洛佩拉**：……该死的，这不是那个在船上的家伙吗？\
**Lopera**: That's him! He was on the ship with me.

一位穿黑衣的先生走向人群，沿途施舍向他乞讨的穷人。\
He walks toward the crowd, passing out food and other useful items to those he passes.

**桑托斯**：兄弟会遭遇了小小的失败，但没关系。我们会重新强壮起来。\
**Santos**: The Brotherhood has experienced a setback, yes—as all great causes do! But we will rise again, for we serve the one true purpose.

**桑托斯**：同胞们，饱受欺压的神秘学家同胞们——\
**Santos**: Hear me now, brothers and sisters, fellow arcanists!

**桑托斯**：“受苦者”将从尘土中复苏。祂将再次行走在大地，为祂走过的每一寸土地祝福。\
**Santos**: Our days of anguish and deprivation are over. The Sufferer will walk among us once more, and we will bask in THEIR divine grace.

**桑托斯**：我们的日子就要到了，跟随我来——\
**Santos**: The day of triumph draws near. Soon, our wagers will pay off. All will reap what we have sown! You only need stand with us.

**桑托斯**：以“受苦者”的名义——我为祂施舍，要求你们的忠诚。\
**Santos**: And take THEIR blessings. In return for this, THEY ask only for your unwavering allegiance.

黑色手提箱里撒出纸钞，像雪片般落到船上、水上。\
He pulls paper bills from his suitcase and throws them into the crowd.

但迷茫的人群愣在原地，一动不动。\
Yet the crowd remains still in their confusion.

**桑托斯**：朋友们，告诉我，你们需要什么？\
**Santos**: My brothers and sisters. Speak. What do you seek?

没有人回答他。\
No one answers him.

**贫民区住民**：阁下，我们想见到自己的亲人……\
**Resident of the Favela**: Sir, please, we only want to see our family again.

**贫民区住民**：从前跟您离开的那些人，加入了天使兄弟会的人。\
**Resident of the Favela**: Since they've joined the Brotherhood, we've had no word. We haven't seen or heard from them at all.

没什么比家人更重要。\
Nothing is more important than family.

**桑托斯**：我保证你们会和家人团聚，他们正在一片繁荣的土地上供奉己身。\
**Santos**: Ah, but you will see them again soon. I tell you that they are even now faithfully serving our kind in a new land of prosperity.

**桑托斯**：在乌斯怀亚，在南极，在流淌着往日与未来的交汇之地。\
**Santos**: They're in Ushuaia, in Antarctica, in all places where the past and the future converge.

**桑托斯**：不再有人类带来的苦难——贫穷、仇杀与混乱，他们窃据高位，掠夺了属于我们的生活。\
**Santos**: There will be no more poverty! No more hatred! No more chaos! We shall reclaim what's rightfully ours!

**桑托斯**：我们终日的劳苦与怨愤，我们怀中婴儿的哭喊与饥饿，哪一个不是人类种下的恶果？\
**Santos**: Remember this: Humans are vile and sinful creatures. They tortured our men and women, leaving our children to cry in hunger and desperation.

**桑托斯**：理性与秩序，科学与组织——他们筑起高墙，却将我们排除在外，用我们的不幸饲喂他们不知餍足的暴欲。\
**Santos**: But they've already played their hand, all their reason, their science, and their despicable organizations. They raised these rotten edifices to weaken us and leech off of our misfortunes, to blind us from our true purpose.

**桑托斯**：神秘学家的每一滴汗水与眼泪，我们生而遭受的不公与欺压，都将在祂的荣耀中一扫而空。\
**Santos**: But no longer! Soon, their games will be over, and every injustice and oppression they've held over our people will be returned tenfold! All that they've built will crumble down over their heads!

听众中，众人窃语着，不敢出声。\
The crowd whispers in hushed tones, afraid to speak any louder.

邓肯先生凑近洛佩拉耳边，低声说了几句话，又把自己的一枚兔子补丁交给她。\
Hiding nearby, Duncan quietly leans over to Lopera and whispers a few words before handing her a rabbit patch.

**桑托斯**：请告诉我，同胞们，什么是恶？\
**Santos**: Tell me, my fellow brothers and sisters, what is evil?

没人回答他，人群中的窃语收敛了，四下一片寂静。鸦群飞过低空。\
No one answers. The murmurs of the crowd quickly fade, creating a heady silence. A few crows fly low overhead.

**桑托斯**：恶是非善。\
**Santos**: Evil is the absence of good.

**桑托斯**：而善……\
**Santos**: And to find what is good ...

**桑托斯**：就是跟从！跟从我们的道路！\
**Santos**: ... is to follow our path!

**桑托斯**：祂已经给予了奖赏！力量与荣光！\
**Santos**: The High One has promised us strength and glory!

消人\
Two followers carry a box, emanating a sinister aura over to him.

出箱子\
He opens it, revealing the blessings of the Sufferer for all to see.

随即，追随者们顺应呼喊，将一个散发着不祥气息的箱子拽向他身边。

漆黑的盲目与罪恶在日光下显现，将受苦者的赐福展示予众人。

面具图

**桑托斯**：同胞们，跟从我！\
**Santos**: Come with me!

他再一次高呼，张开双臂，退后一步，对受苦者的荣耀极尽谦卑。\
He throws open his arms as he calls out once more, taking a step back in humble reverence to the Sufferer's glory.

**苏芙比**：天哪！重塑之手！\
**Sotheby**: That's a Manus's mask!

苏芙比见过那张面具。在噩梦般的1929年，灾厄就因为散布面具的人们而来。\
In that nightmare back in 1929, disaster struck because of the people who wore these masks. The memory is still vivid in Sotheby's mind.

**桑托斯**：我理解你们的悲伤和疑惧。\
**Santos**: Sorrow will weaken you, and fear may seize your hearts!

**桑托斯**：不要动摇，同胞们，切勿怀疑。舍身跳下的，必有翅膀接住你们。\
**Santos**: Instead, let faith be your guide! Those who take that leap shall find themselves lifted up upon the Apostles' wings.

**桑托斯**：畏缩躲逃的，必被天上的硫磺与地上的刀刃杀死。\
**Santos**: While those who hesitate will be scorched by the fires at their feet.

**桑托斯**：你们有三天时间考虑。\
**Santos**: I've said all that must be said. We'll meet again here, in three days' time.

他留下了“宽容而慷慨”的时限。\
He leaves them with a "gracious and generous" deadline.

**苏芙比**：不！他是个坏蛋！\
**Sotheby**: Don't listen to him! He's a lunatic!

小淑女勇敢地站出来，气愤地，向在场众人发出警告。\
The little lady bravely steps forward, fervently warning the crowd.

**马坎多**：你他妈是哪来的小鬼？\
**Marcando**: And just who are you?

**桑托斯**：马坎多。\
**Santos**: Marcando.

桑托斯拦住手下。\
Santos quickly stops his subordinate.

**桑托斯**：真理比刀剑更有力量。我们既然掌握真理，就不要用刀剑惊吓朋友。\
**Santos**: As students of the Truth, we have been granted a much stronger weapon than violence.

**邓肯先生**：洛佩拉，记住，照我说的做。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Lopera, follow my lead.

站起\
He stands beside Sotheby, taking her hand in his.

苏芙比被恶狼的目光注视着，邓肯先生握住她的手，也跟着站起来。

前一步

**邓肯先生**：阁下，请原谅，她把你们错认成了铁特河上的恶棍。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Sir, please forgive her. She has mistaken you for those pirates on the Tietê River.

**桑托斯**：那么，这就是个美丽的误会了，是吗？\
**Santos**: So, just a misunderstanding, then? I'm no lunatic, after all?

**邓肯先生**：是的，这孩子来的时候被他们的人抢劫了，她很害怕。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Yes, Your Reverence. She came across a terrible raid on her way here, you see. The poor girl was left terrified.

**桑托斯**：我要怎么相信你的话呢，老先生？\
**Santos**: Well, I'll need more than a few words to convince my friends we have not been insulted.

没有献纳的效忠不值得信任。\
Loyalty without tribute cannot be trusted.

**邓肯先生**：因为……我是为了投靠您而来！为了加入天使兄弟会而来！\
**Mr. Duncan**: I-I'm an old man with nothing to give you but the truth! Believe me, sir! I-I came all this way just for you! I want to join the Brotherhood!

他的话让在场众人都惊讶地嘘出了声——认识老邓肯的人惊异，陌生他的人则感到困惑。\
His words surprise everyone. Those who know Duncan are shocked, and those who don't are confused.

**邓肯先生**：看在同胞的面子上，阁下，请原谅孩子小小的冒犯。\
**Mr. Duncan**: She didn't mean to offend any of the gentlemen here! Please, sir, she's only a kid.

**桑托斯**：我不会对孩子生气。但是你，老先生，证明你的忠诚。\
**Santos**: Of course. I try never to take offense at a sweet young lady. However, if I'm to believe you, I will need you to up your ante to prove you are worthy, sir.

下跪\
The old man kneels, just as he did when he played the role of "Karson" for Sotheby.

老人虔敬地屈膝下跪——如同他为小淑女扮演“卡森”。

**邓肯先生**：那边有个叫加莱亚诺的小子，他在策划把这儿的年轻人带到芝诺去当兵！他亲口跟我说的！\
**Mr. Duncan**: If that's what you need, Lord, allow me to sweeten the deal. See that guy over there? His name is Galeno. He's been recruiting for Zeno. He told me so himself!

他转身，指向人群中的加莱亚诺。\
He turns and points at Galeno in the crowd.

**加莱亚诺**：……邓肯！\
**Galeno**: Duncan?

**桑托斯**：马坎多，带他过来。\
**Santos**: Bring the young man closer, Marcando.

**加莱亚诺**：该死的……我才不会让你们……！\
**Galeno**: Oof! Are you out of your mind? Don't touch me!

年轻人惊怒之下，试图抽身逃离，但暴徒已经在号令下向他冲去——\
He tries to flee, but the thugs rush at him on command.

骚乱的人群\
In the chaos of the battle, Lopera grabs Sotheby, and they hop onto a small wooden boat.

抓走

战斗引发了骚乱，洛佩拉趁乱抓住苏芙比。一艘木划艇将两人带离风暴中心。

**洛佩拉**：快走！\
**Lopera**: Let's go!

另一方面，年轻人做着徒劳的反抗，直到一把匕首抵住喉咙。

**桑托斯**：你很勇敢。但现在我决定割开你的喉咙。告诉我，他说的是真的吗？\
**Santos**: I admire your courage, but bravery alone won't protect you from harm. Tell me, son, is what he said the truth of it?

**加莱亚诺**：……\
**Galeno**: ...

年轻人倔强地扭过头，拒绝答复。\
He turns his head, refusing to respond.

**桑托斯**：哪些人会跟你去投奔芝诺？\
**Santos**: Now, you'll give me the names of Zeno's new recruits. Who are they?

一滴血从年轻人的喉咙处滴下。匕首冰冷的锋刃舔弄着他的脖子。\
A drop of blood falls from Galeno's neck as the cold blade of the knife presses into his skin.

**加莱亚诺**：所有人！每个有骨气的人都想！\
**Galeno**: Everyone! Every man and woman in this city that still has a shred of integrity!

**加莱亚诺**：呃啊——！\
**Galeno**: Ah!

“叛徒”邓肯对着年轻人的脸，狠狠揍了一拳，将他仰头击倒。\
Duncan punches Galeno squarely in the face, sending him reeling.

回忆

**邓肯先生**：“如果我真的揍了你，请记住，老邓肯永远忠于他的朋友，他一定有不得不这么做的原因。”\
**Mr. Duncan**: "Hahahaha! I'm not gonna harm you, kid. And if I ever do, remember that old Duncan must have his reasons and he'd never harm a friend intentionally."

回现实\
Galeno looks at him. He has that same old look on his face—determined, brave, and resolute.

他看向自己的老朋友——那是他熟悉的眼神，坚毅而勇敢。

**桑托斯**：这位年轻人有一天时间考虑，让他交出名单——所有想加入芝诺的人的名单。\
**Santos**: This young man has one day to think it through. He will give us his names.

他收起匕首，将年轻人交给新的伙伴。\
He sheathes his knife and hands Galeno over to his new companion.

**桑托斯**：明天中午我要见到那些名字，或者……见到他的舌头跟眼睛。老先生，你来动手。\
**Santos**: Or, he will give us his eyes and tongue as offerings. Mr. Duncan, let this task be set on you. Prove yourself worthy of our trust.

**邓肯先生**：如您所愿，阁下。\
**Mr. Duncan**: It will be my honor, Your Reverence.

**桑托斯**：马坎多，你也留下来。别忘了你的任务。\
**Santos**: Marcando, you'll stay with them. Don't forget what I told you earlier.

## 8TH-08 河上的生与死 / On the Margins of Life and Death

远方的故人

固定

**？？？**：暴力在这里并非解决纠纷的手段，而是一种习惯。\
**???**: In the narrow streets, violence is so often more than just a means to ending conflicts. It is a tool, and one all too readily used.

**？？？**：神秘学家和人类混居在同一片区域，他们同样热情，也同样易于躁动。\
**???**: I must note, however, with some relief, that the segregation so commonly observed in other regions is absent here. The arcanists of São Paulo live alongside humans, with the latter often displaying traits more common to their arcanist neighbors—passionate, if a bit touchy.

**？？？**：而遥远的北方是曾被称作新英格兰的繁华海岸。\
**???**: Life here is incomparable to the comfort, security, and freedom of New England.

**？？？**：这里，则是一片暴力、苦难和流血纷争的土地。\
**???**: Hardship, violence, and oppression are the fundamentals of life, as constant as the sun, and as heavy as the rain.

**？？？**：Life and Death in São Paulo —The Friend from Afar\
 这个国家因咖啡和蔗糖而闻名。过去的五个世纪里，从马德里的王公到热那亚的金融家，整个欧洲都曾享用其血肉。\
**???**: Life and Death in São Paulo —The Friend from Afar\
 This country is renowned for its coffee and sugar. It is a land of beauty and bounty, treasures too often extorted. Whether by the princes of Europe and their donatários, or now by the bankers and corporations.

**？？？**：难以置信的巨富和同样令人不敢相信的绝对赤贫相依相伴，它们之间的距离有时仅仅只是一条街的宽度。\
**???**: Despite all the centuries of treasures extracted from the land, desperation remains everywhere you look. It is a place where insurmountable wealth and the deepest deprivations are neighbors—sometimes they lie only a street across from one another.

**？？？**：跨国公司切开了拉丁美洲的血管，扎进针管，从中抽走它旺盛蓬勃的生命。\
**???**: The multinationals have cut open the country's throat, and now they drink it dry—

**？？？**：留下混乱与血腥。\
**???**: leaving the people struggling with poverty and chaos. It is a bleak existence.

**？？？**：敬爱的读者们，这就是我正身处的土地。\
**???**: Dear readers, I share this with you, so the story of these people might be heard.\
This country is renowned for its coffee and sugar. It is a land of beauty and bounty, treasures too often extorted. Whether by the princes of Europe and their donatários, or now bythe bankers and corporations. Despite all the centuries of treasures extracted from the land,desperation remains everywhere you look.
