It is a place where insurmountable wealth and the deepestdeprivations are neighbors—sometimes they lie only a streetacross from one another. The multinationals have cut open the country's throat and now they drink it dry— leaving the people struggling with poverty and chaos. It is a bleak existence. Dear readers, I share this with you so the story of these people might be heard.\
The doctor sits by the riverside, a small group of children gathered around her. They watch in awe as her typewriter hammers the letters onto the page.

维持

This country is renowned for its coffee and sugar. It is a land of beauty and bounty, treasures too often extorted. Whether by the princes of Europe and their donatários, or now bythe bankers and corporations. Despite all the centuries of treasures extracted from the land,desperation remains everywhere you look. It is a place where insurmountable wealth and the deepestdeprivations are neighbors—sometimes they lie only a streetacross from one another. The multinationals have cut open the country's throat and now they drink it dry— leaving the people struggling with poverty and chaos. It is a bleak existence. Dear readers, I share this with you so the story of these people might be heard.\
河岸贫民区

喧哗的河岸边，医生敲打着打字机。孩子们聚在她身旁，围观这个古怪的小机器。

**德洛丝医生**：小船，这儿的人一直都这样生活着吗？\
**Doctor Dores**: Shippy, do you know, has life always been like this here?

**白朗姆**：1681年的拿骚港和1990年的圣保罗，说真的，医生，在我看来就是一回事。\
**White Rum**: If you ask me, Doc, São Paulo in 1990 isn't much different from Nassau, 1681.

**德洛丝医生**：大自然对这儿很慷慨，充足的光照、热量和水，这本该是一片富饶的土地。\
**Doctor Dores**: It's a shame. Between the sunshine and warm sands, there is a good life to be lived here, if only they were free enough to live it.

漫长的夏日，如同这个国家漫长的苦难。\
The summer is long, just like the suffering of these people.

**德洛丝医生**：以前我总是会做一些模糊的梦……去到一些陌生的地方。\
**Doctor Dores**: I used to dream of traveling to all sorts of fascinating places.

**德洛丝医生**：泰晤士河畔的雾都、一个很冷很冷的北国小镇……我还遇到了很多人，只是现在都记不起来了。\
**Doctor Dores**: A foggy city by the Thames, and a little town blanketed in snow and sunflowers. I met so many different people, though I find I can no longer recall their voices, I have only their words left, only my records of them.

**白朗姆**：噢，提到这个，圣萨尔瓦多岛的伊洛潘戈湖里有种水草，当地人把这东西采出来，伴着玉米做成糊糊，吃下去。\
**White Rum**: Have you heard of a weed down at the bottom of Lake Ilopango? The people there turn it into a polenta with cornmeal.

**白朗姆**：然后呢，然后……哈哈，然后你就会想起发生过的所有事！所有的事！\
**White Rum**: Supposedly, if you have it, you'd recall every last thing that's ever happened to you. Every bit of it!

**贫民区小孩**：哇啊……那是什么好宝贝！\
**Kid in the Favela**: Wow! What's the weed called?

孩子们围坐在瓶中船“身”边，好奇地问着。\
The children turn to the ship in the bottle, their eyes filled with curiosity.

**白朗姆**：喔，那东西叫白痴草，哈哈哈哈！\
**White Rum**: They call it "La hierba del tonto," Spanish for "the fool's weed," ahahahaha!

**白朗姆**：一个人要是什么都记得住，那这个倒霉的蠢蛋，离发疯就不远了。\
**White Rum**: You see, lad, only a fool would want to remember everything. Sometimes, a little forgetfulness is a blessing in disguise.

**德洛丝医生**：我倒是宁愿什么都能记得。遗忘很痛苦，小船。\
**Doctor Dores**: I beg to differ, Shippy. To forget the past—its lessons, in pain and joy alike—that isn't a blessing. It's oblivion.

**德洛丝医生**：好了，羊癫草只是一个可爱的传说。小船，它像沙漠半岛里的魅魔传说一样，很多年都没人见过。\
**Doctor Dores**: But let's not argue over some mythical weed. For all the claims, no one has ever seen it, just another myth, like the succubus or the minotaur.

**白朗姆**：噢，魅魔，哈哈，男人们听到这个，都得站起来！\
**White Rum**: Aye, aye, let's talk about succubi instead. That's sure to get the lads pricking up their ears!

提到这个话题，瓶中船又开始胡说八道。\
At the mention of this, the little ship goes off again.

**白朗姆**：88年——当然，我是说1688年，摩根大副在贝卢港捡到了某个魅魔的封印物，然后遇见了那该死的魅魔。\
**White Rum**: Back in '88, I mean 1688, of course, our chief mate, Mr. Morgan, had an encounter with a succubus after he found her seal while carousing in Porto Belo.

**白朗姆**：接下来，他失踪了一个月。好吧……我承认一个月有点夸大，但他确实死在贝卢港。\
**White Rum**: If the rumors tell true, once he got a hold of it, she grabbed a hold on him too. I couldn't say what transpired, but we never saw hide nor hair of him again.

这儿没人能戳穿她的谎言，但也没人真的相信她的胡言乱语。\
No one can debunk her stories, but no one really believes them either.

小孩子们漫不经心地听她讲故事，不时东张西望，意外瞧见水上漂来两条“大鱼”。\
The children's curiosity fades, and their eyes start to wander. One of them spots two "big fish" floating in the water.

**贫民区小孩**：嘿，那边有人落水了！\
**Kid in the Favela**: Look over there! Something's in the water!

两个浮在水上的人影。她们混在塑料瓶堆中间，呛着贫民区的脏水。\
Two figures float among the trash in the river, spluttering and choking.

一个抱着另一个，正在奋力游向岸上。\
One is clinging onto the other as they struggle to swim to shore.

**白朗姆**：怎么回事……？\
**White Rum**: What the devil is all that commotion?

睁眼特效

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

闭眼特效

**金伯利女郎**：喂，快醒醒。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Hey. Wake up.

**金伯利女郎**：喂……喂！你可别淹死了！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Hey, hey! Stay with me!

**金伯利女郎**：喂……喂……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Can you hear me? Hello?

河岸贫民区\
Kimberly pats her fallen companion's face.

金伯利拍拍落水伙伴的脸，试图叫醒她。\
No response.

没有反应。

**金伯利女郎**：明明还在呼吸啊……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: She's still breathing. Why won't she wake up?

**白朗姆**：呼……这是怎么一回事？\
**White Rum**: Oh. What happened to the lass?

紧跟在小船身后赶来的，是盲眼医生和孩子们。\
The little ship makes its way over, followed closely by the children and the doctor.

看到一群陌生人赶来，金伯利略微警惕地耸起了肩膀。\
Seeing the group of strangers approaching, Kimberly tenses up.

**德洛丝医生**：小姐，你还好吗？需要我的帮助吗？\
**Doctor Dores**: Miss, are you alright? Is there anything we can do?

**金伯利女郎**：没什么，只是船爆炸了。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Yes, I'm fine. Our ship went down.

**白朗姆**：老天，我好好的，还没炸呢！\
**White Rum**: Blow me down! These waters are getting rougher by the day.

瓶中船晃荡几下，示意自己的健康“无损”。\
The little ship sways back and forth in its bottle, showing off its excellent condition.

**金伯利女郎**：不，我说的可是一艘游轮！总之，我们都掉到了水里，一路漂向这儿。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: And we drifted down the river until we reached the shore here.

从上游顺着水流漂下，来到这儿——一座贫民区。\
A long way to go, only to end up in the favela.

**金伯利女郎**：她应该还有个一起的朋友，但她不见了，我只能抱着她一起漂流。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I know she's traveling with her friends, but I don't know where they could be now. Everything happened so fast.

**德洛丝医生**：小船，落水的人情况怎么样？\
**Doctor Dores**: Shippy, what's going on? Are there people that need care? What's their condition?

**白朗姆**：还有呼吸，活着呢！不过……啧啧，恐怕也没那么乐观。\
**White Rum**: Just one. A lass. She's still breathing, but she looks like she's been keel-hauled for a bit too long.

**德洛丝医生**：小姐，请把她放到地上，侧卧。\
**Doctor Dores**: Miss, please lay her down on her side.

金伯利一一照做。\
Kimberly does as she is told.

**金伯利女郎**：你要做什么……？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: What are you going to do to her?

跪下\
The doctor kneels down, skillfully clearing the girl's mouth of any residue before starting chest compressions.

医生熟练地跪下，把女孩口中的污秽掏出，确保呼吸通畅后，开始按压胸部。

按压

**德洛丝医生**：救她。\
**Doctor Dores**: Save her, if I can.

按压\
One push. Another.

一下，一下。\
It's a professional instinct. The duty of a doctor.

按压\
An unexplainable impulse drives her to revive the drowning girl.

这是职业本能，也是医者的神圣精神。

一种不可思议的冲动催促着她对溺水的女孩施展救援。

**德洛丝医生**：哈……呼……哈……呼……\
**Doctor Dores**: Huh ... Huh ... Huh ... Huh ...

溺水者开始呛出脏污的河水，医生继续帮她恢复呼吸。\
The girl coughs up some water. The doctor continues.

**德洛丝医生**：很快就会康复了，好孩子。没事的，保持呼吸。\
**Doctor Dores**: Good, good. She'll make it. Please, make sure her airway's clear.

她慢慢咳出更多积水，但四肢乏力，躺在地上没法动弹。\
She coughs out more water, but she still lies there, unable to move.

**白朗姆**：我看事情没那么简单……她发烧了吗？\
**White Rum**: Errh, are you sure about that, Doc? The lass looks paler than a ghost. I think she's burning up.

医生伸手摸向额头——手背滚烫。\
The doctor touches her forehead. It's burning hot.

**德洛丝医生**：她发烧了……带她回去，得去弄点药。\
**Doctor Dores**: You're right. We'll need to take her back with us. I'll fix some medicine for her.

**德洛丝医生**：帮帮忙，请把她抬到我背上。\
**Doctor Dores**: Would you give me a hand, Miss? Help her up on my back.

背上\
Kimberly obediently helps the blind doctor lift the feverish girl onto her back.

金伯利没有多说什么，帮着盲眼医生背起了发烧的女孩。

**德洛丝医生**：……她很轻。\
**Doctor Dores**: Oh! She's almost as light as a child.

孩子们跑在前边，为医生扯开拦路晾晒的衣服。\
The children run ahead, pulling aside the hanging clothes for them to pass.

**德洛丝医生**：这不像是普通的发热，或许感染了河内的热毒菌。\
**Doctor Dores**: I need to run some tests and see if it's just an ordinary fever, or if she has contracted something from the water.

**德洛丝医生**：别担心，我会帮助你的。\
**Doctor Dores**: Don't worry. You're safe with us.

医生自言自语，又或许是在安抚陷入昏迷的病人。\
The doctor speaks to herself, or perhaps in reassurance to the unconscious girl.

**金伯利女郎**：喂，等等我——\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Where are we going? Wait up!

**德洛丝医生**：带她回家。\
**Doctor Dores**: Home.

瓶中船跟在身后，金伯利女郎追上医生——等回过神来，她发现，自己已经跟着走了很远。\
Kimberly catches up to the doctor, only now realizing how far they've walked.

她走进了医生的“家”。\
She steps into the doctor's "home."

## 8TH-09 惊情三百年 / Aged Like Fine Wine

小屋\
A fan whirs loudly, yet the room is just as hot as the outside.

电扇呼呼吹着，小屋里依然炎热，一似户外河岸。\
The doctor gently lays the unconscious girl down, resting her head on her lap.

医生缓缓放下昏迷的病患，让那位小姐平稳躺上自己的大腿。\
She lightly strokes her flushed face.

爱抚图

拉镜头

她轻抚着病患发烧滚烫的脸颊。

**德洛丝医生**：所以……你们只是偶然相遇，然后你救了她。\
**Doctor Dores**: So you weren't even traveling together, and still you brought her all the way here?

**德洛丝医生**：谢谢你的善良，金伯利小姐。\
**Doctor Dores**: You have a good heart, Ms. Kimberly.

**金伯利女郎**：不，别这么说我。河水正好把她冲到我身旁……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: You flatter me, Doctor. It was only that the current pushed her to my side when we all fell into the water.

**金伯利女郎**：我不想看着她就这样沉下去。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: And I just couldn't forgive myself if I were to let her drown.

一个意外——也可以叫它巧合。\
An accident or, perhaps, fate.

**金伯利女郎**：这是我们第二次见面，尽管上一回……上一回在德克萨斯，闹得不太愉快。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: In fact, she and I had met briefly before, in Texas. We didn't part on the best terms.

**德洛丝医生**：朋友之间难免会吵架。\
**Doctor Dores**: Sometimes, we find ourselves in quarrels, even among friends.

**金伯利女郎**：不，我们不是……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: No, we aren't ...

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**德洛丝医生**：不好意思，我想我们的声音有些叨扰到她了。她需要休息。\
**Doctor Dores**: Shh. We should let her get some rest.

金伯利不再出声。\
Kimberly falls silent.

她蹲了下来，就像摇篮边的猫，安静而好奇地望着熟睡的孩子。\
She squats down, watching her the way a cat peers at a sleeping baby.

**金伯利女郎**：我可以摸一摸她吗？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: May I touch her?

**德洛丝医生**：发烧在这儿很要命，但比腹泻和呕吐好。\
**Doctor Dores**: Fever is one of the biggest dangers here, though it's still better than diarrhea and vomiting.

**德洛丝医生**：等情况好一点，我会带她去荣军院进一步治疗。\
**Doctor Dores**: I'll take her to the Veterans' Residence for further treatment once her condition stabilizes.

**金伯利女郎**：她好像只是睡着了。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: It almost looks like she's only sleeping.

**德洛丝医生**：你们真的不是朋友吗？\
**Doctor Dores**: Are you two really not friends? Seems to me that you care for her very much.

**金伯利女郎**：她在船上帮了我。但那该死的船不知道为什么爆炸了！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: She helped me. She was kind to me on the ship. That bloody ship ... I don't know what happened.

**德洛丝医生**：嘘……嘘……\
**Doctor Dores**: Shh. Hush, please.

医生示意她安静，也温柔地对她展露笑容。\
The doctor presses a finger against her lips, a gentle smile on her face.

收氛围图

**金伯利女郎**：对不起，我忘了……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: My apologies.

她像个做错事的孩子。\
She has the face of a guilty child.

**金伯利女郎**：我两次遇到维尔汀，两次都遇到了倒霉的事情。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: *sigh* As I said, it was only twice that we'd met, and somehow, both times turned out quite terrible for me.

医生抚摸着发烧病患的头发，柔顺、漂亮，跟她的发色几乎一样。\
The doctor strokes the feverish patient's hair. It's beautiful—almost the same color as hers.

**德洛丝医生**：她的头发像从天上流下的水。\
**Doctor Dores**: Her hair is so silky. It's smooth and soft, like fine rain in my hands.

医生细长的手指穿过发烧病患的发丝，一点点梳开被水黏住的头发。\
The doctor gently combs the hair with her fingers, slowly untangling the matted strands.

**金伯利女郎**：第一次在蓝手帕旅馆，结果那儿的事情变得乱七八糟，我也没找到弄丢的东西。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: First it was Tuesday's Motel. Things there turned into a right mess, and I didn't find what I'd lost.

**金伯利女郎**：后来在庄园，我只是在那儿吃饭，天哪——冲进来一群人，把我绑走，扔到塔里关着。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Then, in that manor, just as I was about to enjoy a bit of dinner, that wild girl burst in. They caught me, threw me into a tower, and locked me up.

**金伯利女郎**：我像只等着被杀的羊，不知道他们什么时候会把我送去屠宰场。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I was stuck there, waiting like a lamb to be slaughtered.

**德洛丝医生**：但你都挺过来了。你很厉害，孩子。瞧，你现在在这间小屋里，这儿很安全。\
**Doctor Dores**: But you've made it through. You're safe with us.

**德洛丝医生**：没有人会伤害你。\
**Doctor Dores**: No one is going to hurt you here.

**金伯利女郎**：谢谢你，医生。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Thank you, Doctor.

她握起病人垂下的手——一只没有气力的手、略有粗糙的手、微微发烫的手。\
Kimberly gently takes the feverish girl's hand into her own. It's limp and slightly rough to the touch.

像是她模糊不定的姐姐，又像是那些欢呼雀跃的老朋友们皱巴巴而温暖的身影。\
The blurred memory of her sister comes to mind, as well as the wrinkled, warm faces of her old friends cheering her on.

**金伯利女郎**：……再见。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Goodbye.

金伯利从后门退出房间，不再打扰医生。她已经“偿还”了船上得到的善意。她该离开了。\
Satisfied that she has paid her back for her kindness on the ship, Kimberly leaves through the back door.

**金伯利女郎**：？！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: ?!

瓶中船等在门口。\
The little ship in a bottle is waiting for her on the other side.

**白朗姆**：我猜你是不是要走了？你说你不是她的朋友，那你们的这段旅途，我想该到此为止了。\
**White Rum**: Leaving your friend so soon, lass?

**白朗姆**：来吧，亲爱的，我送你一程，路上也好聊聊。\
**White Rum**: Well, come as you are, I'll give you a lift. Perhaps we might have a bit of an old jaw along the way.

**白朗姆**：像你这样的……小姐，在这儿可不多见。\
**White Rum**: After all, it's rare indeed to see one of your kind out and about these days.

**金伯利女郎**：我没想到……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: A-A lift? Uh, pardon me, madam, but, I'm not sure you could bring me anywhere.

**金伯利女郎**：你……真的是艘船……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: You're a little too small, and a little too stuck in that bottle.

一艘盖伦帆船，源于十六世纪的探索之梦。她因之苏醒，又因之长眠，长眠至世上再也没有处女地的千禧年前。\
A galleon, born from the 16th century's dreams of exploration. She awakened and slumbered once again until now, a time in which there are no more uncharted lands to uncover.

**白朗姆**：上来吧，如果你要走，我送你一程。如果你没打算离开，那就当是一个小小的邀请——交个朋友如何？\
**White Rum**: Climb aboard, matey! So, where's our heading? Or shall we go for a ride on the river? Don't be shy. I aim to make a friend of you.

金伯利犹豫着，迟迟没能下定决心踏上小小的甲板。\
Kimberly looks hesitant.

**白朗姆**：孩子们都很喜欢在船上玩，像一群小猴子爬上桅杆，拉扯船帆。\
**White Rum**: Don't be shy. I let the little ones play on my deck all the time, climbing here and there, like a bunch of cheerful little monkeys.

**白朗姆**：医生往返荣军院和这边，都靠我接送。别担心。\
**White Rum**: And not just them. I ferry the good doctor from here to the Veterans' Residence too.

入水

航行

**白朗姆**：如果在海上，你会见到一艘大得多的真家伙。\
**White Rum**: You'll have to wait till we reach the sea to see me at my full size.

**白朗姆**：没办法，这地方就这么窄。小瓶里装不了大船。水有多宽，船就能有多大。\
**White Rum**: Once the water opens up, that's when I'm really free.

帆船慢慢离开医生的小屋，顺流而去。\
The sailboat slowly drifts away from the doctor's hut.

**白朗姆**：你要去哪？总得有个方向，要是不知道自己去哪，吹什么风都没用。\
**White Rum**: Now, I ask again, where are we going, mate? Can't just let the wind decide our course.

**金伯利女郎**：去哪儿都行，只要到一个没人找得到我的地方。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Why not? I should like to go somewhere nobody will ever find me.

迷茫，混沌，逃亡，明天或许也像每一个远去的昨天一样。\
Confusion, chaos, escape—perhaps tomorrow will be just like all those yesterdays.

**白朗姆**：遗憾地说，我认为二十世纪九十年代的地球应该不存在这样的地方了。\
**White Rum**: I'm afraid there's precious few places like that anymore, lass.

**白朗姆**：我看过最新的地球仪，天哪，他们连亚马孙雨林里哪儿有个水坑都知道。\
**White Rum**: I've spied the globes they've got nowadays; seems like every last step is covered to the four corners and back.

**白朗姆**：宝贝儿，哪里能找到一只愿意好心救助陌生人的小魅魔呢？我见过你的同胞，她们恶劣、贪婪又下流，但个个都是十足的尤物。\
**White Rum**: But aren't you a strange sight, lass? You know I've seen your kind before. Beautiful to look at, aye, but there's a darkness in you that lies beneath the surface, isn't there?

**白朗姆**：而一个会冒险救下陌生人的魅魔……那我宁愿相信埃尔多拉多不是一个传说。\
**White Rum**: But you're not like the rest of them, you'd say. Well, I would sooner believe in a Map to El Dorado before I'd swallow the idea of a succubus with a heart of gold.

**白朗姆**：我猜，她是你的主人，对不对？或者……她拿着你的封印物？你不得不听命于她？\
**White Rum**: So, was that girl your master? Did she have your seal?

**白朗姆**：如果她真是你的主人，那你恐怕是我见过的最蠢的小魅魔。\
**White Rum**: If that were true, then heart of gold or coal, wouldn't matter for none. You'd be as thick as old tar.

她被认出来了——一个被通缉、被追捕、被遗忘于世人记忆中的古老种族。\
She's been found out. She's a member of an ancient race once wanted—even hunted—and now forgotten by the world.

水鸟停靠在船沿，加入旅途。\
A few seagulls land on the boat's edge, joining them on their journey.

**金伯利女郎**：……？！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: ...?!

**白朗姆**：魅魔小姐，你应该给自己弄一只更好的手套，这样才能遮住爪子。\
**White Rum**: What, are you wondering what gave you away? Your gloves don't do much to hide those claws. I could feel them pressing on my railings as soon as you hopped on.

金伯利立刻将手藏到身后。\
Kimberly immediately hides her hands behind her back.

她的反应出卖了自己。\
Her reaction betrays her.

**白朗姆**：哈哈，看来是真的！\
**White Rum**: Ahahahaha! No use hiding them now, matey.

帆船大笑着荡起河浪。\
Her hearty laugh sends ripples through the water.

**金伯利女郎**：喔呜——！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: You!

金伯利对着桅杆挠下一道抓痕，但她小小的抗议在帆船看来却无足轻重。\
Kimberly scratches the mast with her claws, but this small protest does nothing to dissuade the ship.

**金伯利女郎**：你也是来抓我的吗？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Are you going to turn me in?

她环顾四周。这儿很安全，只要轻轻一跳，她就能回到最近的地面。\
She looks around. This place looks safe enough. Just one small leap, and she'd be back on solid ground.

**白朗姆**：抓你？天哪，小甜心！我只是一艘船呀，被我那亲爱的船长放进瓶子里，一睡睡了将近三百年的小船。\
**White Rum**: Turn you in? And how do you suppose I do that! I'm only a ruddy ship! Bring me back up on land, and I'll be stuck right back in the bottle.

**白朗姆**：和你一样，她也是位逃犯。\
**White Rum**: No, lass. I've sailed with rougher folks than you. My old captain had a bounty on her head, too.

如同惊弓之鸟般四处躲藏的逃犯。\
She's a fugitive, hiding like a frightened bird.

远方传来雷声，停驻在屋檐上的雀崽儿四散奔逃。\
Thunder rumbles in the distance, scattering the birds perched on the roofs on either side of the river.

**金伯利女郎**：……！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: ...?!

雷声令她紧张，却让身下帆船回想起曾随船长穿行咆哮西风带的旧日过往。\
It makes her quiver, but for the boat, it brings back fond memories of sailing the roaring westerlies with her captain.

加速\
Rain starts to pour. The wind picks up, filling the ship's sails and racing her down the river.

响雷之后，是夏日的骤雨。河风吹鼓了船帆，小船兴奋地提高了速度。

**金伯利女郎**：不会有人付你赏金的！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Well, just so you know, I very much doubt they'll pay you anything for handing me over!

**白朗姆**：喔，原来你真的是逃犯。\
**White Rum**: Maybe so, maybe so. Now, you've got the law in your tailwind? What happened? Did you spring loose from the old gibbet?

**金伯利女郎**：你……！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I ...

**白朗姆**：小姐，想瞒过别人，你应该先学会欺骗自己。\
**White Rum**: Mark me now, young lass. If you're going to try to pull one over on me, you'll have to do a lot better job than that.

故技重施。\
That same old trick.

**金伯利女郎**：我不喜欢被人捉弄的感觉。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Are you mocking me? This is not how one ought to treat a new friend.

**白朗姆**：好吧，我为这个恶作剧道歉。你在逃避谁？你的主人呢？他不会为你摆平麻烦吗？船长如果不能照顾他的船，他就该被丢海里去喂鱼。\
**White Rum**: Quite right, lass. So then, who are your pursuers? And your master? Shouldn't you be under his protection? My old crew would say any captain that can't keep his ship safe is only good for bait.

**金伯利女郎**：我不知道。那家伙是个傻子，还弄丢了我的封印物。该死。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I have no idea where he is, or where my seal is for that matter—he was a no-good fool, though. Or only good for bait, perhaps.

**金伯利女郎**：但愿他早点完蛋，死在旧金山哪个没人知道的下水道里最好。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I hope he's dead, rotting in some sewer back in San Francisco.

加速\
The rain stops. Brief and intense, just like her escape.

一场短促的雨，正如她短促而匆忙的逃亡——雨势渐大，来得快，去得也一样快。

**白朗姆**：别担心，这艘船载过很多人，虽然他们无一例外，最后全都死了——但谁又能一直活着呢？\
**White Rum**: Aye, well, mortal flesh doesn't last long. I've ferried many a passenger in my days, and none yet have escaped when Davy Jones came calling their name.

**白朗姆**：“断腿”威廉被吊死前是个纵火犯，一嘴烂牙，在南安普敦上船前被仇家锯断了右腿。\
**White Rum**: As I recall, the first that went was William Half-Leg. He lost the other half in a fight at the port of Southampton. Hanged on the governor's orders.

**白朗姆**：“红手”爱德华是低地佬，喜欢用钝刀子割人质喉咙，但他却在托尔图加港被一个醉鬼抹了脖子。\
**White Rum**: And Eduard the Red-Hand, a nasty piece of work from the low countries, loved a bit of throat-cutting. Until he got his own throat slit by some fool in a ramshackle pub on Tortuga. Hahahahaha!

她一一回忆自己的伙伴。事情久远，但都像发生在昨天。见多识广的小船记得她的每一位乘客。\
She fondly remembers every one of her crew. Though they all died hundreds of years ago, it still feels like yesterday to her.

**金伯利女郎**：这些人肯定都没有好下场。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Sounds as though they got what they deserved.

**白朗姆**：当然，每个人都死了。吊死的，淹死的，被船上的伙计们丢去荒岛上等死的……\
**White Rum**: That they did, lass. They all got what they deserved. Some hanged, some drowned, some we marooned on a desert isle with naught but a pistol and a flagon of rum.

**白朗姆**：有船长的时候，我跟着船长的号令走，去普利茅斯，去拿骚，去皇家港……甚至装成商船在塞维利亚偷运胡椒和肉桂。\
**White Rum**: I've been to Plymouth, Nassau, Port Royal. I once even slipped into Seville disguised as a merchantman to smuggle pepper and cinnamon. Wherever the captain wanted to go, we sailed.

一段惊险的岁月，惊险而又平平无奇。\
An exciting, dangerous life, yet ordinary in its own way.

回忆\
The countless cannonball scars in her hull alone tell the story.

像十八磅加农炮留在她身上的无数个弹孔一样危险。

**白朗姆**：但现在，他们全都没了。可船永远是这艘船，没有船长，我也照样出航，想去哪儿就去哪儿。\
**White Rum**: But one by one, Davy took them all. Now here I am, a ship without a captain. My own master.

**白朗姆**：我知道这对一个生来要服从契约的魅魔来说很难理解，但你有没有想过……过上另一种生活呢？\
**White Rum**: I suppose that's a lot to take in. You ever thought about living a different life?

**白朗姆**：喝着朗姆酒，嚼着比国王脸皮还厚的硬肉干，出海寻找那些没人见过的小岛。\
**White Rum**: To set sail for some far corner of the sea, living on spiced rum and jerky thick as a buccaneer's hide?

**白朗姆**：我的意思是……好奇，就是好奇，哈哈，我也很好奇你，所以才在这儿打听。\
**White Rum**: How's that sound, lass? Not that I'm saying we set sail today. It's only a bit of old fancy.

**金伯利女郎**：我不知道，小船。那可能不重要，我得先……得先找到我弄丢的重要的东西。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I really can't say, uhm, Shippy. I, I suppose I can't, not yet at least. There is something important I need to retrieve.

**白朗姆**：请叫我“船长”——伟大的白朗姆号！既是船长的船，也是船的船长！\
**White Rum**: Ah-ah, that's "Captain White Rum" to you—the ship of a captain, and captain of the ship!

**金伯利女郎**：我可能得……等等……我有点儿……想吐……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I prefer ... Wait ... Sorry ... I need to ...

贫民区\
As the ship docks, she leaps back ashore, doubles over in an alleyway, and retches.

小船靠岸，她跳回岸上，撑着棚屋干呕。

**白朗姆**：……你没说过你会晕船。\
**White Rum**: Seasick? I hadn't thought your kind capable of it.

**金伯利女郎**：你也没跟我说……河上会……这么晃……啊……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I didn't expect this ... either ...

她脚边滚来一个铝罐，打断了和小船的闲聊。金伯利不耐烦地把这小玩意儿踢走。\
A can rolls over, gently hitting her foot. Annoyed, she kicks it away.

不远处，几个少年用铝罐代替足球，练习着颠球。某个好事的小伙子又一脚将“球”踢向金伯利。\
Not far away, a few boys have been practicing their soccer skills with it. One mischievous boy kicks the can back toward Kimberly.

**金伯利女郎**：该死的，什么东西？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Urgh! What now?

这一次，金伯利捡起铝罐，气冲冲地扔向那小伙子的脑袋。\
This time, she picks up the can and angrily throws it at the boy's head.

**贫民区少年**：你敢朝我扔东西？\
**Teenager in the Favela**: Jeez! I like this girl. She's feisty!

面对“还击”，好勇斗狠的少年挨了痛，却首先环顾自己周围的小伙计——和他一样茫然，一样不知所措。\
He straightens himself up as he slowly makes his way toward her, a cocky grin on his face.

**贫民区少年**：你敢对我们天使兄弟会的人动手！\
**Teenager in the Favela**: We're with the Brotherhood, Miss. You apologize now, and we might just let you go.

**贫民区少年**：桑托斯大人回来了！你完了！\
**Teenager in the Favela**: Or don't you know that Lord Santos is back? We can make this rougher for you, if you like.

**白朗姆**：刀？小家伙们，这可不明智呀，嘿——\
**White Rum**: Careful me lads. I wouldn't pull those knives. Things may go rougher than you'd bargained for.

脚步声\
The boys are no match for her.

她轻松摆平了这些不自量力的小伙子。

**金伯利女郎**：哼，龇牙咧嘴的小鬼，再让我看到你们，我一定揪出你们脑子里的毛病来！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Not so tough now, are you boys? Try this again, and I'll make a mince out of what's left of you!

赶走上来挑事的孩子后，她撒气般将脚边的瓶罐一一踹入河中。\
She angrily kicks the can into the river.

**白朗姆**：我想这是个误会……我认识你们的老爹，要是让他知道你们说自己是兄弟会的人，恐怕你们都得挨顿打。\
**White Rum**: I know your fathers, me boys, and I think they wouldn't be none too happy to hear you claiming to be with the Brotherhood.

**贫民区少年**：……切，走了走了，没意思。她不会踢球，我们不跟她玩。\
**Teenager in the Favela**: Let's go. We're wasting our time here.

自称兄弟会信众的少年被吓得尿了裤子，放下狠话，拉着伙伴匆忙逃离。\
The boys scurry off, muttering under their breaths.

**白朗姆**：我敢保证兄弟会的人根本不认识他们。\
**White Rum**: Bilge rats, the lot of them. Not even fit for the Apostles.

**白朗姆**：那伙人能动刀子解决问题，就绝不会动嘴皮子。\
**White Rum**: The Brotherhood always let their knives do the talking.

**白朗姆**：另外……我现在确信你真是个魅魔了，小姐。你下手真的没有轻重。\
**White Rum**: If there'd been any doubt of what you are, lass, that fight sure cleared it up.

## 8TH-10 白色航船 / Boarding the White Ship

平民区

**马坎多**：听着，咱们不是麦德林的黑帮，咱们是天使兄弟会。\
**Marcando**: Listen up. We're the Apostles Brotherhood, not some worthless favela gang.

**马坎多**：先客气点儿，要是那医生不懂规矩，再动手。\
**Marcando**: So, we start off nice and easy. And if the doc doesn't play along, well, then we make her play along, clear?

担架床上，病人的状态比之前好了不少。医生正蹲在床边，为她擦洗脸庞。\
The feverish girl looks to be doing much better than before. Doctor Dores is crouched beside the bed, gently wiping her face.
A few uninvited guests burst in.

几位不速之客破门而入。

**德洛丝医生**：您好，各位先生。有什么需要我帮忙的吗？\
**Doctor Dores**: Hello. How can I help you, gentlemen?

**马坎多**：盲人？\
**Marcando**: Ay, is she really blind?

**德洛丝医生**：请别在意，我只是眼睛看不见，但一样能给人治病。你们中间，是有人生病了吗？\
**Doctor Dores**: I'm afraid yes. But please don't worry. I'm more than able to treat all my patients. Are you feeling unwell, sir?

马坎多看到担架上的病人，对手下抛了个眼神。\
Marcando glances at the patient on the stretcher and signals to his men.

跟随他的“野狗”们迅速将病人围住。\
His "dogs" quickly surround the patient.

**德洛丝医生**：嗯？\
**Doctor Dores**: Sir?

**马坎多**：我的老板生病了。他听说你是个不错的医生。\
**Marcando**: We heard that you're a good doctor. We got someone who needs your help.

**马坎多**：荣军院的德洛丝，大伙儿都认识你。\
**Marcando**: You're Dr. Dores from the Veterans' Residence, right?

**德洛丝医生**：先生，您在说谎。我能听出这是谎话。很抱歉，我——\
**Doctor Dores**: Yes, and may I know who you are? I won't turn away a patient, but I'll also need some assurance that you can be trusted, sir.

**兄弟会信众**：看来你想拒绝我们啊。\
**Brotherhood Member**: So, is she coming with us or not?

不速之客踢翻医生的药瓶，试管意外引起了一个小小的爆炸。\
He kicks over a cabinet, causing the test tubes within to smash in a small explosion on the floor.

平民区

**白朗姆**：你听到什么动静了吗？\
**White Rum**: Did you hear that?

**金伯利女郎**：好像是爆炸，医生那边传来的。怎么回事？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Sounds like some kind of explosion near the clinic. Should we go back?

**白朗姆**：我想医生虽然看不见东西，但不会笨到摔破自己的试管玩意儿……\
**White Rum**: It could be an accident, but she's got a way with her equipment. Doubtful she's the cause of this.

**白朗姆**：走吧，别出了什么大事。\
**White Rum**: Steady on then. Let's hurry back and see for ourselves.

**白朗姆**：船上最坏的家伙都知道，要尊重医生。\
**White Rum**: Ah-ah, that's not how you treat a doctor, lads!

看着“闯入”小屋的不速之客，暴徒们纷纷抽出匕首——这是一种习惯，一种生活的本能。\
The thugs instinctively draw their knives—a habit developed in their line of "work."

**金伯利女郎**：你们要做什么？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: What are you doing to her?!

**马坎多**：桑托斯阁下有些话想找这位荣军院的医生“聊聊”。\
**Marcando**: Lord Santos would like to have a word with the doctor, that's all.

**金伯利女郎**：她得照顾维尔汀，不能跟你们走。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: You're not taking her anywhere. Don't you see she's taking care of this girl?

她亮出爪子，毫不退让。\
She bares her claws, digging her heels into the ground.

**马坎多**：是吗？但你得知道，我不是来这儿征询医生意见的。\
**Marcando**: Yeah, I'm not asking for permission, sweetheart.

马坎多打了个响指，发出信号。\
Marcando snaps his fingers.

**马坎多**：干掉他们，带走医生。\
**Marcando**: Grab the doctor. Ice the rest of them.

靠近\
Kimberly clasps the head of a thug in her claws, poised to crush it, but she hesitates, glancing back at the doctor.

捏住

金伯利握住一个倒霉蛋的脑袋，想用力捏碎，却突然停住，犹豫着回头看向医生。

**德洛丝医生**：请各位停止争斗！\
**Doctor Dores**: Stop! Enough! I won't have you fighting in my clinic!

松手\
Kimberly releases her grip.

医生的话让金伯利松开了手。

**金伯利女郎**：医生？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Doctor?

**白朗姆**：医生，维尔汀还在他们那边。\
**White Rum**: But they've got the girl, Doctor.

高烧的病人被暴徒挟持着，热痛仍在折磨她失去意识的身体。\
The feverish girl's unconscious body has been thrown over the shoulder of one of the thugs.

**马坎多**：这女孩不是贫民区的人。为什么要保护她？\
**Marcando**: This lady definitely isn't from the favela. So, what's she doing here?

**德洛丝医生**：因为她生病了，病人应该得到照顾。\
**Doctor Dores**: She's ill. She needs my help. That is all I ever ask.

**马坎多**：只要你肯跟我们走，我就保证其他人的安全。\
**Marcando**: Well, all we need is you, Doc. So, how's about we make a deal? You come with us, we let the rest of your friends go, understood?

**德洛丝医生**：好。\
**Doctor Dores**: So be it.

他提出一个建议，而医生毫不犹豫地接受了。\
She doesn't hesitate to accept.

**金伯利女郎**：医生……我可以干掉他们！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Please, Doctor! Stand aside. I'll happily take care of these rats.

**德洛丝医生**：暴力不能解决问题，孩子，我相信那位桑托斯先生不会对我做什么。\
**Doctor Dores**: I have no doubt about that, Miss. However, once violence starts and blood is spilled, there will be no end to it. For now, I would be happy to meet with this Mr. Santos, and seek out a peaceful resolution.

**德洛丝医生**：我答应你们的要求。\
**Doctor Dores**: I'll come with you.

**马坎多**：走吧，女士。\
**Marcando**: See? We can all be friends.

兄弟会的暴徒把病人推向金伯利。\
The thug pushes the feverish girl toward Kimberly.

**金伯利女郎**：维尔汀！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Vertin!

金伯利接住陷入昏迷的同伴，抱紧她。\
Kimberly catches her, holding her tightly in her arms.

**德洛丝医生**：如果这孩子今晚还没醒过来，你们就带她去荣军院。\
**Doctor Dores**: If she doesn't wake up tonight, take her to the Veterans' Residence first thing in the morning.

**马坎多**：把这位女士带去见桑托斯。\
**Marcando**: Alright, get the doctor straight to His Reverence.

唤醒\
...

……\
A long sleep with no dreams.

经历了一场漫长的睡眠，但没有梦。\
No worries. No troubles. No thoughts.

没有烦恼。没有忧虑。没有思考。\
Like being back in a warm, dark, damp room.

像回到了一个湿润、温暖又昏暗的房间。\
She awakes to an unfamiliar place. It's quiet and strange.

睁眼-背景模糊

背景清晰

眼前的世界很陌生，陌生而安静。

闭眼

微微睁开

**维尔汀**：咳……咳……\
**Vertin**: *cough*

**白朗姆**：噢，你醒了，咱们的睡美人。\
**White Rum**: Have a good rest, did you, sleeping beauty?

**金伯利女郎**：维尔汀！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Vertin!

**白朗姆**：发生了很糟糕的事情。\
**White Rum**: You've missed quite a bit. All terrible, I'm afraid.

一艘会说话的船，装在瓶子里。\
A talking ship inside a bottle.

一座漂浮在水上的城寨，还有身边焦急的金伯利女郎。\
A tiny floating fortress on the water, and beside her, a worried Ms. Kimberly.

完全睁开

**维尔汀**：这里是……\
**Vertin**: Where am I?

**白朗姆**：这位小姐救了你，你俩一起漂过来的。\
**White Rum**: You and this lass were drifting down the river after your ship went down.

**白朗姆**：要是早点醒来，你还能见到德洛丝医生。\
**White Rum**: You'd have met Dr. Dores, had you woken up a little sooner.

**维尔汀**：医生？\
**Vertin**: Doctor?

**金伯利女郎**：一位盲眼医生，她治好了你。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Dr. Dores, yes. She's a doctor from the Veterans' Residence. She saved you from the very claws of death.

**维尔汀**：她……\
**Vertin**: She ...

不行。身体还是很沉。\
She can't walk. Her body is still too heavy.

**白朗姆**：你发烧了，还喝了很多脏水。昏过去的时候医生一直在照顾你。\
**White Rum**: Aye, you were burning up, lass. But the good doctor pulled you through. She was right there by your bedside the whole time.

**白朗姆**：好消息是，她应该还很安全。\
**White Rum**: The good news is, we think she's still alive.

**维尔汀**：坏消息呢？\
**Vertin**: Still alive? What's the bad news, then?

**白朗姆**：噢，很聪明。坏消息是为了你，她被天使兄弟会的人绑架了。\
**White Rum**: The bad news is she's been snatched up by the Apostles Brotherhood.

**维尔汀**：什么？\
**Vertin**: What?

**白朗姆**：别紧张，人质不会被伤害……顶多挨点儿打，但要是对女人动手……那帮人就真是烂透了！\
**White Rum**: Rest now, lass. They aren't likely to hurt her, for now. You'll need your strength for later.

**白朗姆**：是一个叫桑托斯的要她去，天使兄弟会的那伙混蛋玩意儿。\
**White Rum**: Some scallywag by the name of Santos wanted to "have a word with her," so they said.

……\
...

一场糟糕的水上灾难，把事情全都搞乱了。\
Everything has gone to hell since that ship sank.

**维尔汀**：洛佩拉……还有苏芙比呢……她们在哪儿？\
**Vertin**: But Lopera and Sotheby ... Where are they?

手臂还在痛，像是血管里扎着刺。\
There's a shooting pain in her arm.

**维尔汀**：大家应该在船上一起被……\
**Vertin**: I remember we all fell into the water.

**金伯利女郎**：我不知道……我没有见到她们。我只是……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I'm sorry. I didn't see them. I only—

**金伯利女郎**：没什么，我们只是一起被冲到岸上来了。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: We washed ashore together.

**维尔汀**：我的地图……去荣军院。或许她们已经到目的地了。\
**Vertin**: My map—have you seen it? I have to get to the Veterans' Residence. They may very well be waiting for me there.

撑起身体，先行动起来。\
Come on. On your feet.

**白朗姆**：听起来，也许你们会需要……搭个船？\
**White Rum**: Well, I may be just the ship to get you there, ladies.

## 8TH-11 圣保罗舞曲 / Sao Paulo Bossa Nova

平民区

将医生交给手下伙计，送往教堂据点后，马坎多回到了“不识相的年轻人”那儿。\
After instructing his men to take Doctor Dores to their chapel hideout, Marcando walks over to Duncan, who is watching over a group of hostages.

**马坎多**：聪明的老家伙，我就喜欢和你这样的人一起做事。\
**Marcando**: You're a clever one, old man. I like working with your type.

暴徒领袖叫了几个伙计，把人质送去庄园，随后回到了看守加莱亚诺的地方。\
The hostages—Galeno among them—are lined up on their knees, their hands tied behind their backs. Marcando has ordered they be taken to the manor.

**邓肯先生**：聪明人才能活到我这个岁数呢。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Haha, much appreciated. I've tried to pick up a thing or two over the years.

**马坎多**：哈哈哈哈，你很会说话。对了，那个小女孩呢？\
**Marcando**: You've had plenty of time to learn, a man of your age. By the way, what about that girl? Where'd she go?

苏芙比不见了。\
Sotheby is missing.

**邓肯先生**：可能是吓跑了，别在意，有钱人的小姐都这样，随便吓唬吓唬就会跑掉。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Dunno. Maybe got scared away. You know how little rich girls are.

**邓肯先生**：她有保镖，没事。\
**Mr. Duncan**: I'm certain she's found her way back to her daddy's bodyguards. She'll be no cause for concern.

**马坎多**：我不关心她的死活，倒是这个年轻人……\
**Marcando**: Fine, fine. No need to worry about this spoiled little girl. Now, this bastard on the other hand.

马坎多一脚踢向被反绑双手的加莱亚诺。\
Marcando kicks Galeno hard in the stomach.

**邓肯先生**：算啦，这家伙活不了多久了。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Leave the boy be. He's not got much time left, if he doesn't give up those names.

他的眼睛像灵活的热带飞鸟一样转了起来——观察四周。\
His eyes dart around, keenly scanning his surroundings.

马坎多带了十几个伙计走，但回来的时候少了三个。\
Marcando had left with about a dozen men, but he's only come back with nine.

**邓肯先生**：我藏了一些美酒，你知道的，大伙们都会喜爱的那种酒，马坎多先生。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Hot enough out here? Luckily, I've got a bit of vino left. You a fan of wine, Mr. Marcando?

**邓肯先生**：我得拿些过来跟你们尝尝，为了我们新的友谊——有好事儿的时候别忘了我！哈哈哈……！\
**Mr. Duncan**: I'll fetch some for us, and all the brothers and sisters here! Let's drink to the Brotherhood, and the opportunities that lie ahead.

**马坎多**：哈，街道上就得多些你这样机灵的家伙！去吧，“老”朋友！\
**Marcando**: Hahaha, you old fox, I see your game! But why not? We could all use a drink.

**邓肯先生**：对了，盯好这家伙，他很狡猾，别让他逃了！\
**Mr. Duncan**: You over there! Keep a watch on this guy. Don't let him get away!

他一脚踹向加莱亚诺厚实的胖屁股，借机离开。\
He gives Galeno a kick in the backside as he leaves.

老邓肯焦急地等待着，不断探头看向上游。\
Old Duncan waits by the water, his eyes anxiously fixed upstream.

河面上终于划来一艘小船。洛佩拉带着几个年轻人，如约而至。\
Eventually, a small boat carrying Lopera and a few men rows into view.

**邓肯先生**：总算来了……\
**Mr. Duncan**: Finally ...

船上的伙计们陆续跳上来，带着加了“猛料”的朗姆酒。\
The boat docks, and they jump ashore one by one, carrying spiked wine in their hands.

**洛佩拉**：你们什么时候开始谋划的？\
**Lopera**: Duncan! You nearly had me there. When did you plan all this?

**邓肯先生**：很早以前就开始了，但最近出了意外——今天也是个意外，不要紧。\
**Mr. Duncan**: I've had it brewing for a while, but things have been changing fast lately. Honestly, I didn't expect to be doing this now.

他数着船上来的伙伴，五六个人，比预想中少，但也足够了。\
He counts the men. Just six of them. Fewer than expected, but enough.

**苏芙比**：嘿嘿，呼噜糖浆能保证他们睡不醒。\
**Sotheby**: There's enough snoring syrup in the wine now to put them all in a dreamy, deep, deep sleep!

**苏芙比**：要是再加上一点嗜睡颠茄的话，会不会效果更好呢……\
**Sotheby**: Oh, but might it have had a stronger effect if I had included a dash of slumber belladonna in the recipe?

**邓肯先生**：足够了，小淑女，只要把这些家伙都灌醉，然后——\
**Mr. Duncan**: This will be more than enough, little lady. We only need to get them to drink the wine, then—

**苏芙比**：你应该喝一点这个，只要一点点就可以！\
**Sotheby**: Oh, then you must drink this! Just a drop!

小淑女提起裙摆，抖落出她的魔药收藏。\
She rummages around in her skirt for the potion.

一瓶深绿色的、粘稠的魔药。\
Eventually, she produces a bottle of thick, pine green liquid.

**苏芙比**：刺醒汤能让你不受酒里的东西影响，但……你可能会流眼泪……它黏在舌头上真的好痛！\
**Sotheby**: It will stay on your tongue and prickle around in your mouth. That way, you won't drift off like the others. I've concocted much tastier potions before, but this one ...

小淑女的亲身经历——光是回想起实验时的“惨状”，她就快落下眼泪。\
Memories of her past experiments come flooding back, almost bringing her to tears.

**邓肯先生**：我没问题。\
**Mr. Duncan**: It'll do just fine. Thank you, little lady.

他笑着握住瓶口，喝下可怕的稠绿液体，随后举起吹笛，暗示接下来的行动。\
He smiles as he takes the bottle and downs its contents. He raises his flute, signaling the next step of the plan.

**邓肯先生**：酒给我，听到笛声，你们就过来，把他们全干掉。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Pass me the wine and wait for my signal. When you hear me playing this flute, you'll know it's time to strike.

黑幕转场\
贫民区

**邓肯先生**：墨西哥的老朋友送来的，来，大家一起！\
**Mr. Duncan**: The wine's here! Courtesy of an old friend from Mexico. Take a glass, everyone!

**马坎多**：祝桑托斯阁下健康！\
**Marcando**: Here's to His Reverence's good health!

**兄弟会信众**：祝桑托斯阁下健康！\
**Brotherhood Member**: To His Reverence's health!

**邓肯先生**：敬马坎多！敬不可战胜的天使兄弟会！\
**Mr. Duncan**: To Marcando! To the Invincible Brotherhood!

**兄弟会信众**：敬马坎多！\
**Brotherhood Member**: To Marcando!

吹捧让醉酒的马坎多渐渐放松警惕。\
The flattery and alcohol have successfully lowered Marcando's guard.

**马坎多**：邓肯，笛子给我！\
**Marcando**: Duncan, that your flute? Give it over.

马坎多抢过老邓肯的笛子，斜眼看着他，又打量起他的吹笛。\
Marcando snatches Duncan's flute and looks it over.

**马坎多**：这东西做得不错……嗝儿……！\
**Marcando**: This is, *hiccup*, a f-fine flute!

**马坎多**：你会《La Llorona》这曲子吗？\
**Marcando**: D-Duncan, did you-you said that you g-got a f-friend in Mexico, huh? You know that old Mexican song "La Llorona"?

不，还不行，好几个家伙还醒着，不能在这时候吹笛——\
Can't blow the flute just yet. A few men are still awake.

**邓肯先生**：会啊！当然会！年轻的时候我有个相好的女人，在图卢姆的仙人掌酒吧，啊，她手把手教我吹了这曲子！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Heheh! That I do! I learned it from the best—in the "Cactus" back in Tulum, from a fine young lady with silky hair and gentle eyes as dark as coffee.

一个临机应变的谎言，但谎言里却不乏真相——至少图卢姆的仙人掌酒吧是真的。\
An improvised lie, but there's truth in it. The Cactus Bar in Tulum is real, at least.

**马坎多**：相好的女人？\
**Marcando**: Sure, so-uh, how fine was this lady?

比起笛子跟曲子，暴徒们显然对话题中的另一个词更感兴趣。\
It seems beautiful ladies are much more interesting than music to him.

**邓肯先生**：这个话题就到这儿吧，就当是别让我这个老人想起伤心事……\
**Mr. Duncan**: Ah, don't let me start spinning that yarn. It'll be no fun for you to watch an old man bursting into tears.

谎言的话语，谎言的眼泪，老邓肯的演技或许骗不过清醒人——但在酒精和魔药的催眠下，就是另一回事了。\
Lies and fake tears. Duncan's acting wouldn't fool the sober, but with his audience under the influence of alcohol and potions, he just might get away with it.

**邓肯先生**：她伤透了我的心，像拿仙人掌的一千根针刺痛了我，唉！来喝酒吧，各位，为昨日已去！为明日灿烂！\
**Mr. Duncan**: I'll only say I was heartbroken by the time I left. Ah, that love of mine! *sigh* Anyway, enough about the old flames of yesterday! Let's raise a glass to a better tomorrow!

**马坎多**：敬可怜的邓肯，哈哈！\
**Marcando**: To poor old Duncan, hahahaha!

**兄弟会信众**：敬可怜的邓肯！\
**Brotherhood Member**: Hahahaha! To poor old Duncan!

老邓肯偷偷收回笛子，继续倒酒。\
Duncan adeptly retrieves his flute before pouring out more drinks.

他假意欢笑，一杯一杯和“新朋友”们说笑，直到对方醉到站立不稳。\
He feigns joy, drinking and laughing with his "new friends," until they're too drunk to stand.
Every one of them is utterly inebriated.

他们喝醉了。

马坎多发出鼾声，他身边的“猎犬”们一一醉倒，不省人事。\
Marcando and his "hounds" pass out, one by one, until they're all fast asleep.

**邓肯先生**：好了，好了，到时候了……\
**Mr. Duncan**: It's time.

他吹响竖笛，召唤久候多时的伙伴。\
He blows the flute, and his companions jump into action.

**兄弟会信众**：吹得……不错……\
**Brotherhood Member**: Good, good music.

**兄弟会信众**：你们是……？什么人？！\
**Brotherhood Member**: Mm? Who-Who are you?!

**邓肯先生**：洛佩拉！加莱亚诺！按住他们！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Lopera! Galeno! Come on, give me a hand!

摁倒

**马坎多**：他妈的叛徒！\
**Marcando**: F**king traitor!

**邓肯先生**：该死的是你们！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Time to cash you out.

老邓肯按住还在挣扎的马坎多。\
He pins the struggling Marcando to the ground.

**马坎多**：桑托斯不会放过你们！\
**Marcando**: You'll be ... be-begging for Lord Santos's mercy!

**邓肯先生**：听着，没有人会再跟着你们走，兄弟会别想再从这儿拐走任何人。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Be reasonable, kid. The Brotherhood is finished. Your time's up.

老邓肯抽出加莱亚诺腰间的匕首，用“圣保罗的方式”干掉了他。\
He pulls the knife from Galeno's waist and finishes Marcando off "the São Paulo way."

**邓肯先生**：一个都别放跑！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Don't let them slip away!

**苏芙比**：卡、卡森……不，不是……\
**Sotheby**: Mr. Ka-Karson ... But ... You ...

话到嘴边，却被咽了下去。是的，一向严厉而体面的管家先生绝不会这样做。\
She swallows her words. No, her butler would never do something like this.

这是来自于地下世界的生猛与热烈的力量。\
This is the raw, fierce power of a man who has lived on the streets of the favela.

洛佩拉追上一个逃跑的暴徒，枪托狠狠击打向他的后脑勺。\
Meanwhile, Lopera catches up to a fleeing thug and cracks him over the head with the butt of her gun.

**加莱亚诺**：让我来。\
**Galeno**: Let me.

他抓起一根铝球棍，来到洛佩拉身边，看着倒地的暴徒。\
He picks up a metal bat and stands over the fallen thug in front of Lopera.

**洛佩拉**：下得了手吗？\
**Lopera**: Think you can handle this?

**加莱亚诺**：没问题……！\
**Galeno**: Yeah, I've got it!

这位年轻人咽了咽口水，对准刚才被枪托击打过的地方……\
He swallows hard and aims at the spot where the gun butt had struck.

**加莱亚诺**：为了贫民区。\
**Galeno**: For the favela.

**加莱亚诺**：——兄弟会必须死！\
**Galeno**: The Brotherhood must go!

战斗结束了。\
The battle is over.

**邓肯先生**：让你受苦了，伙计。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Sorry to put you through all that, kid.

**加莱亚诺**：能干掉这些混蛋，不算什么。接下来怎么办？\
**Galeno**: Don't mention it. If this means we can get rid of them for good, it'll all be worth it. So, what's next?

**邓肯先生**：芝诺的人会来接你们，但我们得去荣军院跟基地接洽。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Next, Zeno will come around to pick you up. But first, we've got to get back to the Veterans' Residence.

贫民区的年轻人们有些不安，互相看着对方，不知所措。\
Unease spreads among the group. They exchange a few glances.

**加莱亚诺**：必须留个人，老朋友，要让大伙儿知道他们没有被放弃。\
**Galeno**: No, sir. One of you has to stay. The people need to see you, or they'll worry that you've deserted us.

**洛佩拉**：我可以一个人回荣军院。邓肯，你留下来吧。\
**Lopera**: I can make it there on my own. Stay with them, Duncan.

**苏芙比**：你们是不是忘了我～！\
**Sotheby**: And me!

一个意料之外的人选自己站了出来。\
An unexpected volunteer steps forward.

**苏芙比**：这里还有很多生病的小朋友～\
**Sotheby**: I've seen there are many sick children here in the favela.

**苏芙比**：我比大伙儿都更懂怎么治病呢！\
**Sotheby**: I'm certain that I could do something to help them!

**洛佩拉**：苏芙比！不，这太危险了……\
**Lopera**: Uhm, I'm not sure it's a good idea, Sotheby. The favelas can be dangerous if you don't know them.

**邓肯先生**：勇敢的小淑女可以留在这里，我会陪着她。\
**Mr. Duncan**: The brave young lady can stay with me if she likes. I'll keep her safe.

加莱亚诺和其他伙计们连连点头，站到小淑女身旁。\
Galeno and the others nod.

**邓肯先生**：你敢不敢和我一起在这里冒险呀，小淑女？\
**Mr. Duncan**: What do you say to that, little lady?

**苏芙比**：交给苏芙比吧！\
**Sotheby**: Ms. Sotheby is never afraid!

**邓肯先生**：那就这样。洛佩拉，去荣军院，把消息带给大家，联系伊戈尔将军。\
**Mr. Duncan**: It's decided then. Lopera, head for the Veterans' Residence. Tell them what happened and contact Admiral Igor from there.

听到养父的名字，洛佩拉不再犹疑。\
All hesitation leaves Lopera's body once she hears her father's name.

**邓肯先生**：加莱亚诺！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Galeno!

**邓肯先生**：如果年轻人想成为骑士，那他们的册封仪式上就会有一位身份尊贵的女士。\
**Mr. Duncan**: You've done us proud, kid. If I were king, I'd have made you a knight. Who knows, maybe the little lady could do that for us.

**邓肯先生**：保护好我们的女士，不要让荣誉蒙羞！\
**Mr. Duncan**: But first, young Galeno, we'll seek another deed worthy of knighthood. It's time we fight for our people!

## 8TH-12 “平安夜” / "Silent Night, Holy Night"

白朗姆很熟悉这段航程——从贫民区到荣军院，过去她很多次载着医生往来。\
The route from the favela to the Veterans' Residence is quite familiar to White Rum. She has ferried the doctor back and forth countless times.

**白朗姆**：在洛佩拉之后，你是第一个来这儿的年轻人。医生只能算半个——因为她不怎么年轻了，哈哈。\
**White Rum**: You ever been to a Veterans' Residence? Not many young faces there, besides Lopera. As far as the doc goes, doubtful anyone knows her real age, and even the saltiest sailor knows better than to ask a lady her age!

……\
...

荣军院-夜

**白朗姆**：……这个笑话好像不太合适？\
**White Rum**: Oh. I see that joke missed the bow, so to speak.

**维尔汀**：不，这很好笑。\
**Vertin**: No, no, it wasn't a bad joke at all, really.

听到笑话的人应该做出反应。\
A joke would usually warrant some kind of response.

**白朗姆**：维尔汀，不用这样，一个没人笑的笑话本身就是最好笑的笑话。\
**White Rum**: Aye, thanks for the kind words, lass, but best to leave old flotsam where it lies.

荣军院的玛丽安娜奶奶送来点心。\
Mamãe Mariana from the Veterans' Residence brings out some snacks.

糖在这儿，就像泼洒在里约热内卢海岸的阳光一样取之不尽。\
There's plenty of sugar to go round in this neck of the woods.

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：你又在吹牛讲胡话了，小船。\
**Mamãe Mariana**: Have you been filling this sweet young lady's head with your tall tales, Shippy?

瓶中船曾和医生同住在荣军院，但今天回来的却只有她——以及她的两位新乘客。医生不在其中。\
The little ship used to live with the doctor in the Veterans' Residence, but today she returns alone, and neither one of her two passengers is her old roommate.

**维尔汀**：很抱歉打扰您。\
**Vertin**: Sorry to show up without proper notice.

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：你们是洛佩拉的朋友。\
**Mamãe Mariana**: Don't worry about it! Any friend of Lopera is a friend of ours.

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：如果你们早来几天，还能遇见老邓肯和德洛丝医生。\
**Mamãe Mariana**: Oh. If you'd come a couple of days earlier, we would've introduced you to Mr. Duncan and Dr. Dores.

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：他俩去了贫民区，已经好几天没回来了。\
**Mamãe Mariana**: But they've not been around in a while.

**维尔汀**：看上去我们错过了和两位见面的机会。\
**Vertin**: That's a shame. I was looking forward to meeting them. Hopefully we'll see them soon.

庭院里，金伯利似乎很熟悉这儿的环境，却好像不断警惕着周围。\
Kimberly wanders the courtyard. She's still on guard, but she seems to be oddly familiar with this place.

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：六几年的时候，也有个和她很像的孩子，在这儿做护工。\
**Mamãe Mariana**: You know, I knew a girl who looked just like her. A caregiver here way back in the '60s.

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：这地方当时还叫热情之家。\
**Mamãe Mariana**: Back when this place was called Heartfelt Home.

老人挠着怀中小猫的下巴。\
She scratches the chin of the kitten in her arms.

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：但我想不起她长什么样，年纪大了，就是这样。有些事记得，又好像都忘了。\
**Mamãe Mariana**: But it can't be her now, can it? Besides, I'm old now, and my memory is a bit fuzzier than it used to be.

**维尔汀**：我可以去看看德洛丝医生的房间吗？\
**Vertin**: May I see Dr. Dores's room?

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：当然可以，但别乱碰医生的东西。\
**Mamãe Mariana**: She wouldn't mind, but please be careful not to move anything.

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：那间屋子没有锁，不过平时也没人进去。喔，就是那儿——\
**Mamãe Mariana**: It's that one over there, dear. She never locks the door.

切镜

它看上去和庭院里的其他房间没有区别。\
The place looks no different from the other rooms in the courtyard, but the door is slightly ajar.

一扇没有锁的门。绿藤植物从屋顶垂下，斑驳的墙壁上刻写着一道道远去岁月的痕迹。\
Green vines hang from the roof, and the weathered walls bear the passage of time. It's a simple little home.

一间平平无奇的小屋。屋子门口，金伯利正抱起一只野猫，靠在屋外挠着猫肚子。\
Kimberly stands by the door, a stray cat in her arms. She scratches its belly.

**金伯利女郎**：呀啊——！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Aah!

**维尔汀**：嗯？\
**Vertin**: Hmm?

**金伯利女郎**：好呀，你这个坏东西，敢咬我的耳朵～！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: How dare you scratch me!

猫跳上金伯利肩膀，踩着她，灵活地抓住绿藤，逃向荣军院的矮墙外。\
The cat leaps out of Kimberly's arms, grabs hold of one of the vines, and clambers over the wall of the Veterans' Residence.

**金伯利女郎**：啊……给我、等等……！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Get back here, you fluffy rapscallion! I'll have your tail, you hear me?!

破门

她没有自己想象中的那么灵活。或者说，当真正的小猫出现时，她便变得柔软起来。\
She's not as agile as she looks, or perhaps the kitten has made her soft.

以至于她抓不住那样的小生灵，反而扑倒在蒙尘的木门上，沾得一身灰。\
She fails to catch it, instead stumbling into the door, throwing it wide open, and hitting the floor with a thud.

**维尔汀**：门倒塌了。\
**Vertin**: Do be careful, Ms. Kimberly.

**金伯利女郎**：唔，好疼……怎么会这样……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Ugh, how did that happen?

**金伯利女郎**：该死，你是什么时候过来的？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: And how long have you been standing there?

**维尔汀**：我一直站在这里。\
**Vertin**: Just a little while.

**维尔汀**：很新颖的方式。\
**Vertin**: Funny, I've never thought to open a door like that before.

**维尔汀**：进去看看。\
**Vertin**: Come along. Let's take a peek inside.

医生房间

……\
...

一处平平无奇的客房。\
It's a rather ordinary guest room.

屋里摆着一张白色的大理石椅子，扶手处放有红色按钮。\
Except there's a peculiar white marble chair sitting by the window. It has a red button on the armrest.

**维尔汀**：……嗯？\
**Vertin**: Hmm?

这个大理石的材质，有些熟悉。但却完全回忆不起来。\
The marble feels familiar, but no memories come to mind.

正如金伯利对这座荣军院所怀着的某种似曾相识的感觉。\
Odd how they both have some kind of familiarity with this place.

**金伯利女郎**：一颗……红色按钮？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Hmm, what's this red button on the chair?

一个醒目而突兀的按钮，像在引诱人按下它。\
The button seems totally out of place, as if daring someone to press it.

金伯利坐上那张椅子，好奇地摁下按钮。\
Kimberly takes a seat and curiously presses the button.

——咔嗒。咔嗒，咔咔咔嗒。\
*click—click* *click-click-click*

金伯利像个傲慢的女公爵，反复摁下按钮，但什么也没发生。她恼火地把翘起的腿甩到另一边去。\
Despite her fervent pressing, nothing happens. Frustrated, she swings her legs over the other side of the chair.

**金伯利女郎**：哈……！好吧，原来只是个没用的东西！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Heh. Good for nothing!

没品位的装饰，也没人知道这张椅子为什么会在医生的房间里。\
A tasteless decoration. No one knows why this chair is in the doctor's room.

但的确，按下按钮，没有爆炸也没有烟雾，它只是一个……安全的小装置，没有作用的小玩意儿。

而在房间的另一侧，医生的书桌上陈列着一摞稿纸。\
But pressing the button didn't trigger an explosion or anything of the like. It's simply a functionless, harmless little contraption.

替换浮窗\
On the other side of the room, the doctor's desk holds a stack of manuscripts.

**维尔汀**：没有送出的稿件。\
**Vertin**: These must be articles that she hasn't sent out yet.

圣保罗的街区走访记录，贫民区的神秘学家生活状况，巴西东北部的种植园经济调查……\
Notes on the districts of São Paulo, records of arcanists in the favelas, investigations into plantation economies in northeastern Brazil …

**金伯利女郎**：……她是个好人。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: She's a good woman.

**金伯利女郎**：我想，我遇到的好人不多。所以，她是个好人……我一下就能嗅得出来。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: And her room smells like a good woman's room. You don't find many of those around these days.

**维尔汀**：她做了什么吗？\
**Vertin**: What makes you say so?

**金伯利女郎**：她救了你。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Well, firstly, she did save your life.

**金伯利女郎**：更重要的是——好人的味道是香香的。这一点从来就没有错。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: And secondly, it's hard to explain. Good people have a smell, a pleasant one. My nose has never been wrong.

**金伯利女郎**：维尔汀……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Vertin ...

**维尔汀**：我们会救她。\
**Vertin**: We'll bring her home safely.

翻页声

**金伯利女郎**：……医生好像用那台打字机写了不少东西。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: This typewriter seems like it's seen a lot of use.

**维尔汀**：她有投稿的记录吗？\
**Vertin**: Do you see any drafts? Any samples?

**金伯利女郎**：不知道……我看不懂医生写的东西。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I can't say. I'm not very familiar with these things.

**金伯利女郎**：噢，你看这里～！这儿有个署名……不过，医生是叫这个名字吗？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Take a look! She's signed something here. Hmm, but I thought her name was Dores.

稿纸上，出现了一个简短的单词。\
There's a single word written at the bottom of the manuscript.

书本特效

兀尔德。\
Urd.

**维尔汀**：……！\
**Vertin**: ...?!

敲门声

**？？？**：玛丽安娜——！\
**???**: Mariana!!

院墙之外，传来了熟悉的呼喊声。\
A familiar voice echoes from outside.

## 8TH-13 粉红河豚 / Boto Cor-de-Rosa

荣军院·夜

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：喔，今天还有客人？\
**Mamãe Mariana**: Oh, more visitors?

**维尔汀**：……！\
**Vertin**: ...?!

是洛佩拉。她平安无事。\
It's Lopera. She's safe.

但苏芙比在哪儿？\
But where's Sotheby?

**维尔汀**：大家都躲过了河上的灾难，苏芙比呢？\
**Vertin**: Thank goodness. You survived, too. What about Sotheby?

**洛佩拉**：贫民区发生了一些事……她留在那边了，别担心，邓肯跟她在一起，会保护她的安全。\
**Lopera**: Oh, something happened in the favela earlier, so she decided to stay there. Don't worry. Duncan's with her.

**维尔汀**：有个坏消息，德洛丝医生被兄弟会绑架了。\
**Vertin**: We've got bad news. Dr. Dores has been abducted by the Brotherhood.

**洛佩拉**：什么？那群白痴，他们只能做出这样孬种的事情吗？\
**Lopera**: What? Idiots! What's wrong with them?!

**洛佩拉**：……算了算了，先联系基地，老爹会想办法的。\
**Lopera**: Ugh, guess I'll call the base. My father will figure something out.

**白朗姆**：我还以为你沉了！洛佩拉！\
**White Rum**: Sink me! Lopera! I thought you'd been sent to Davy Jones's locker!

瓶中船不知从哪里冒出来，一股脑地撞到洛佩拉怀中。\
White Rum soars through the air and lands squarely in Lopera's arms.

坚硬，勇猛，差点儿能让一位成年男性心肌梗死。\
The ferocity of the embrace is enough to knock a grown man to the ground.

**洛佩拉**：我的命比这些老家伙的胡渣子还硬，哈哈哈哈，没那么容易死。\
**Lopera**: Hahaha! Why did you think that? I'm tougher than the stubble on the chins of the old geezers here!

**洛佩拉**：在你沉了之前，我都会好好活着的。\
**Lopera**: I'm like you, a ship that'll never sink!

声响

**洛佩拉**：司辰，那边那位是……\
**Lopera**: Umm, Timekeeper, who's that over there?

金伯利躲在医生的房间里，探出半个脑袋，但洛佩拉还是发现了她。\
Kimberly is peeking out through the doorway, only a sliver of her face showing through the gap.

**洛佩拉**：金伯利？你被释放了？\
**Lopera**: Kimberly? Did my father let you go?

释放？\
She's been released?

**洛佩拉**：追捕逃兵的时候，金伯利在重塑之手的人堆里。我们抓回了她，但老爹并没有把她丢进牢里。\
**Lopera**: Oh, Timekeeper, let me explain. When we were routing out the deserters, we found Kimberly hanging out with the Manus thugs.

**洛佩拉**：我不知道她去哪儿了，反正老爹肯定有自己的打算。\
**Lopera**: Pa took her off somewhere, and he always has a plan, so I didn't bother asking where she ended up.

**洛佩拉**：嘿，过来打个招呼如何？他什么时候放你走的？\
**Lopera**: Hey, come over here and say hi. When did Pa let you go?

**洛佩拉**：还是说……你是逃出来的？\
**Lopera**: Or did you sneak out somehow?

金伯利的眼神闪躲，爪子却紧绷着，似乎下一秒钟就会做出激烈的反应。\
Kimberly's eyes shift, her claws tensed, as if ready to spring into action at any moment.

**维尔汀**：我想……她应该救了我，把我从河滩旁拖了出来。\
**Vertin**: I think ... Ms. Kimberly, didn't you pull me out of the water?

**金伯利女郎**：……！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: ...?!

**金伯利女郎**：你怎么知……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: How did you know?

**维尔汀**：在我高烧退去后的几个小时里，我大概想起了昏迷前的事情。\
**Vertin**: Shortly after my fever subsided, I started to remember what happened just before I lost consciousness.

**维尔汀**：当时金伯利小姐惊慌失措地呼唤我，“维尔汀……你不能死，你还不能放弃生命……”\
**Vertin**: There was a voice ringing in my head. It was you calling out to me, "Vertin, I can't have you dying here! You mustn't give up!"

**金伯利女郎**：什么！我才没有！我把你交到医生那儿我就走了！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: What?! I did not say that! I just took you to the doctor and left!

一声抗议的尖叫从另一侧传来。\
Her protestation is almost a scream.

**白朗姆**：哎呀，没错，这位小姐不肯承认自己做了好事，明明她有很多机会可以捏碎维尔汀的脖子，但她选择了救她。\
**White Rum**: Aye, 'tis true what Vertin says. Though Kimberly denies it, she chose to save her—even when she had plenty of chances to blow the lass down.

**白朗姆**：我想她不是你的敌人，洛佩拉。\
**White Rum**: She's a good lass at heart. Not an enemy, Lopera.

**洛佩拉**：……\
**Lopera**: ...

**金伯利女郎**：……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: ...

洛佩拉放下戒心，向金伯利放出善意，朝她挥手。\
Lopera lowers her guard, offering a friendly wave to Kimberly.

阴影中的少女小心翼翼地走出来，仍然与洛佩拉保持着谨慎的距离。\
Kimberly cautiously steps out of the doorway but maintains some distance between the two of them.

洛佩拉看着这位有些害怕的“新朋友”——比起在庄园被逮捕时，金伯利换了身新衣服，险些让她认不出来。\
Lopera looks at her new "friend." Her attire has given her a totally different appearance.

片刻后，她对紧张的金伯利露出微笑。\
After a brief pause, Lopera smiles at her.

**洛佩拉**：你当时和重塑之手的人在一起，很难不让人产生怀疑。\
**Lopera**: You have to understand, it's pretty hard not to suspect someone who hangs around with the Manus.

**洛佩拉**：以前或许是个误会，我为我曾经的鲁莽道歉，当时情况紧急，我来不及……抱歉，金伯利。\
**Lopera**: Anyway, I guess there must've been some kind of misunderstanding. Back then, I didn't have time to ... In any case, I'm sorry, Kimberly.

她向金伯利伸出手，示意友好，但金伯利缩着爪子，有点儿迟疑。\
Lopera extends a hand in a gesture of peace, but Kimberly hesitates, her claws tensing once again.

**金伯利女郎**：好吧。但我不会那么快地原谅你——\
**Ms. Kimberly**: It's fine. But don't think I'll forgive you so easily.

**金伯利女郎**：不过，重塑之手、天使兄弟会什么的……我一直搞不清那群复杂的家伙……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Speaking of the Manus and the Brotherhood, I never quite understood what they were trying to do.

**洛佩拉**：你搞不明白……也很正常。我不会怪你的。\
**Lopera**: I don't blame you. I still don't really get it, either.

**洛佩拉**：——那你和他们究竟是不是一条船上的呢？\
**Lopera**: So you're really not in the same boat as them?

一个突如其来，又顺理成章的发问。\
A sudden yet perfectly reasonable question.

**金伯利女郎**：不，当然不是了！我没有船……我不和任何人在一条船上。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Of course not! I don't have a boat, no, I mean, I'm not in any boat with anyone!

**金伯利女郎**：一旦我能找到……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: If only I'd found my ...

她仿佛想起了什么似的，下意识地向四周张望。一无所获。\
She looks around as if she's forgotten something but finds nothing.

**金伯利女郎**：我不是你们想要找的那种人。我也没法给你们更多的信息了……如果你想要我离开，我会找个地方待着的。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Listen, I don't know who it is you're looking for, but it's not me. I've already told you everything I know. If I'm not welcome here, I'll get out of your way.

**金伯利女郎**：只要别再抓我回去……我不想再看到……你们那个东西。\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Just please don't take me back to that place. I don't want to see that thing ever again.

她不愿意看向洛佩拉腰间。那是一种压抑着的排斥、恐惧……或是某种深藏于心的东西。\
She refuses to look at the weapons around Lopera's waist. Perhaps in a restrained sense of rejection or fear, or something hidden deep within her heart.

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：好了，孩子们。如果你们想聊事情，至少该找个能坐下的地方。\
**Mamãe Mariana**: Alright, girls. If you want to have a chat, at least take a seat first.

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：一大群人站在院子门口，这太不像话了。\
**Mamãe Mariana**: It simply won't do to have you all standing around the entrance like this.

进来\
Mamãe Mariana takes Kimberly with one hand and Lopera with the other and leads them back to the courtyard. When they arrive, she lays out some paçoca for them to snack on.

玛丽安娜奶奶一手牵起金伯利，一手挽住洛佩拉，把大伙儿“请”回庭院，摆上多糖的帕索卡招待。

**洛佩拉**：甜食吃太多会伤牙的。\
**Lopera**: Eating candy's bad for your teeth, Grandma.

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：小孩子才担心这些，到我们这把年纪，想吃点什么，就随心吃。万一明天就走了呢？哈哈！\
**Mamãe Mariana**: Oh, I'm much too old to worry about that. When you reach my age, and just waking up each day is a blessing, you'll eat whatever you want, too.

**维尔汀**：玛丽安娜女士，我有一些关于邓肯先生的问题，可以去聊聊吗？\
**Vertin**: Mamãe Mariana, could I have a word with you, please? I have some questions about Mr. Duncan.

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：老邓肯又闹出什么麻烦啦？好，走吧，好孩子，把这儿留给她俩。\
**Mamãe Mariana**: Oh, Duncan, what kind of trouble has he stirred up now? Alright then. Why don't we head inside and give those two some space?

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：洛佩拉，如果你欺负了人家，记得要好好道歉。\
**Mamãe Mariana**: And Lopera, apologize to that poor girl properly, you hear?

每一位远去的朋友都值得怀念。\
Every lost friend is worth remembering.

**洛佩拉**：我相信老爹，如果他放了你，那你一定是无罪的。\
**Lopera**: My father released you, which means you can be trusted.

**洛佩拉**：你还救了维尔汀，我不会把你当做敌人。\
**Lopera**: And you saved Vertin's life, too. I guess I shouldn't have been so hostile toward you.

**金伯利女郎**：我……\
**Ms. Kimberly**: I ...

**洛佩拉**：来，金伯利，这杯送给你。一个小小的赔礼。\
**Lopera**: Here, have a drink, as a token of my apology.

一杯浓黑的饮料，飘出诱人的香气。\
She hands her a warm cup of something dark. It has a rich smell.

**洛佩拉**：萨尔瓦多产的咖啡，一杯能让你一宿都睡不着。\
**Lopera**: It's Salvadoran coffee. Great if you need to pull an all-nighter!

金伯利接住，伸出舌头好奇地舔了舔。\
Kimberly raises the cup to her mouth with both hands and curiously sticks her tongue into the liquid.

**金伯利女郎**：呜——！好苦！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Bleh! It's so bitter!

**洛佩拉**：就像过去的日子一样苦。\
**Lopera**: Yep. Bitter like the old days.

她沉默了一会儿。\
Lopera falls silent for a while.

金伯利望向她腰间那把枪的眼神，她很熟悉。\
Kimberly glances at the gun around Lopera's waist.

**洛佩拉**：我父亲出卖了种植园的工人。\
**Lopera**: You know, back in Colombia, my father did horrible things to his plantation workers.

**洛佩拉**：不是伊戈尔，而是血缘意义上的父亲。\
**Lopera**: Well, my biological father. Not Igor.

她望着天，无奈地笑起来，像在讲一个陌生人的故事。\
Lopera looks off into the sky and laughs resignedly. It's as if she just spoke of a stranger rather than her flesh and blood.

**洛佩拉**：“那不是枪声，而是胜利的鞭炮声”。\
**Lopera**: He said, "No, that's not the sound of gunfire outside. The workers are setting off fireworks. They're celebrating."

**洛佩拉**：但后来我才知道，他出卖了同胞，那是屠杀的声音。\
**Lopera**: But they weren't fireworks. He betrayed his workers—his compatriots. It wasn't a celebration; it was a massacre.

**金伯利女郎**：……！\
**Ms. Kimberly**: ...?!

**洛佩拉**：后来我离开了家，被老爹和姐姐捡到，在此之后，我才加入芝诺，就这么回事。\
**Lopera**: After that, I ran away from home. One day, the admiral and Molly found me. That's how I joined Zeno.

**洛佩拉**：在这儿，背叛是很常见的事情。被伙伴、被朋友、被家人……一颗脑袋比等重的黄金便宜得多。\
**Lopera**: Betrayal's as common as dirt here. Comrades, friends, family, anyone could sell you out, and for cheap, too.

**洛佩拉**：祝你顺利，早点登上那艘属于你的船。\
**Lopera**: I hope you can find your boat soon. You know, a place where people have your back.

**金伯利女郎**：我可不可以不喝这个？\
**Ms. Kimberly**: Umm, can I not drink this?

**洛佩拉**：哈哈哈……如果你不喜欢的话，我不会介意。我有时候做事就是很莽撞……\
**Lopera**: Hahahaha, of course. Don't force yourself. I know the taste isn't for everyone.

她同新朋友碰杯。\
She clinks cups with her new friend.

**洛佩拉**：卡洛塔·洛佩兹·里维拉。\
**Lopera**: Carlotta Lopez Rivera.

**洛佩拉**：是不是听起来很拗口？\
**Lopera**: That's my full name. Bit of a mouthful, huh?

洛佩拉朝着三十万公里外的发光天体伸出左手，抓握着夏夜粘稠的空气。她握不住月亮。\
Lopera stretches out her arm, closes one eye, and lines up the moon between her fingers. She closes her fist but catches nothing but the air.

推近

**洛佩拉**：我不想见到这个名字，但老爹不让。\
**Lopera**: I wanted to erase it from my profile, from everywhere, to be honest, but my father disapproved.

她凝望着这枚捉不住的天体，抓弄手指。\
She fiddles with her fingers, her eyes lingering on that unattainable celestial body.

**洛佩拉**：姐姐跟我说：不要忘掉过去，洛佩拉。\
**Lopera**: Molly agreed with him. She said, "You mustn't forget your past, Pera."

**洛佩拉**：所以我就接受了，但“洛佩拉”是一个更好听的名字，我喜欢人们这么叫我。\
**Lopera**: So I let it go. But "Lopera" sounds so much nicer, so I prefer to go by that.

**洛佩拉**：你呢，金伯利？\
**Lopera**: And you, Kimberly? What's your real name?

金伯利有些犹豫，而后，她缓缓张口。\
Kimberly hesitates.

**天使娜娜**：娜娜，娜娜·哈丽。热情之家的……天使娜娜。\
**Anjo Nala**: Nala. Nala Hari. The residents of Heartfelt Home called me Anjo Nala.

场景

**维尔汀**：您还记得邓肯先生是哪一年住进荣军院的吗？\
**Vertin**: How long ago did Mr. Duncan move here? Do you remember?

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：大概是五六年前，我记不清了。\
**Mamãe Mariana**: It must have been ... five, maybe six years ago? I'm not entirely sure.

五六年前。并不是遥远的二十年代或三十年代。怎么回事？\
Five or six years ago. Nowhere near the '20s. What's going on?

**维尔汀**：这儿有他的照片可以看看吗？\
**Vertin**: Do you have any photos of him?

热心肠的老人点点头，走向储物间，取出一副蒙灰的相框。\
Mariana nods and pulls a photograph from the storage room.

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：啊，好几年没人看过这东西了。来，这位就是他——\
**Mamãe Mariana**: We do have one, but it's been gathering dust for years. Let me see. Ah. Here. This is him.

消人\
She points to the man who looks like Mr. Karson.

老人指向那位长相酷似卡森管家的人。

**维尔汀**：我们见过一位长相和他极为相似的老先生……的照片。\
**Vertin**: I knew a gentleman who looked just like him.

**维尔汀**：那位先生叫卡森。邓肯先生用过这个名字或者这个化名吗？\
**Vertin**: His name was Karson. Did Mr. Duncan ever go by that name?

老人捧起相框，吹去上面的积尘。\
The old woman blows the dust off the frame.

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：没有，至少我们这儿谁都没听说过这件事。我还在军队里做医生的时候，就知道他了。\
**Mamãe Mariana**: No, not that any of us are aware of anyway. And I've known him since I was a medic in the army.

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：大胆的邓肯，无所不能的邓肯，但从没听说过“卡森”。\
**Mamãe Mariana**: Back then, people called him "Duncan the Dauntless" or "The All-Powerful Duncan." I never once heard "Karson" or anything of the like.

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：很抱歉，在这件事上我帮不了你，孩子。\
**Mamãe Mariana**: Sorry I couldn't be of more help, my dear.

退出房间\
It seems an in-person meeting with Mr. Duncan is in order.

看来必须亲眼见到邓肯先生。\
As they head outside, black flashes across their vision as a crow swoops down from above.

乌鸦忽然飞来，从天上落下黑色的消息。\
It releases the letter clutched in its claws.

一卷信笺随着羽毛飘落。

**维尔汀**：乌鸦……？\
**Vertin**: A crow?

乌鸦栽落到庭院中。信笺随风飘落，来到手边。\
The crow perches nearby as the letter flutters down and lands at their feet.

揭开印章，展开信笺。\
The old woman picks it up and breaks the seal.

**玛丽安娜奶奶**：这看起来可不像好消息……\
**Mamãe Mariana**: Oh, dear. This looks like bad news.

勒索信

**维尔汀**：桑托斯。\
**Vertin**: Santos.

一封笔迹干净的勒索信，署名为“桑托斯”。\
It's a cleanly written ransom note, signed "Santos."

**维尔汀**：德洛丝医生在上校庄园。\
**Vertin**: Dr. Dores is being held captive in the colonel's manor.

**维尔汀**：他给我们三天时间。\
**Vertin**: He's given us three days.

**维尔汀**：桑托斯要求芝诺方面交还被逮捕的逃兵，否则将处决医生。\
**Vertin**: He says that if Zeno doesn't return the deserters they detained, he'll execute the doctor.

……\
...

收浮窗

**维尔汀**：联络伊戈尔将军，我们需要芝诺的援助。\
**Vertin**: Mamãe Mariana, please contact Admiral Igor. We need Zeno's help.

## 8TH-14 无眠之人 / The Sleepless Man

伊戈尔办公室\
Admiral Igor rarely makes calls to Zeno headquarters, but the situation has become desperate.

老将军很少拨通芝诺总部的红色电话。

**？？？**：啊，伊戈尔！圣保罗情况怎么样？\
**???**: Ah, Igor! How are things in São Paulo?

**伊戈尔将军**：比预想中更糟糕。\
**Admiral Igor**: Worse than expected.

**伊戈尔将军**：我带了一些人，但不够用。\
**Admiral Igor**: I have a small number of troops with me, but not enough to deal with the situation.

**伊戈尔将军**：天使兄弟会跟重塑之手勾结，他们至少有一个头目已经向重塑之手效忠。\
**Admiral Igor**: Things have gotten out of hand. At least one of the Apostles Brotherhood leaders has pledged allegiance to the Manus.

**？？？**：兄弟会？这种帮派在南美洲要多少有多少，就像栽在种植园里的甘蔗，一茬没了还会冒出下一茬。\
**???**: Tsk, Brotherhood? These new gangs just keep popping up, don't they? It's like cutting down sugarcane. Before you know it, another one's grown in its place.

**伊戈尔将军**：索姆同志，逃兵杀了自己的长官。\
卡洛斯在基地里被他们杀了，而兄弟会收容了这些逃兵。\
**Admiral Igor**: Carlos has been murdered by his own subordinates. Even now, some of the deserters are with the Brotherhood.

**索姆将军**：……\
**Admiral Somme**: ...

电话那端传来了沉默。\
This news is met with a prolonged silence.

**索姆将军**：人都抓回来了吗？\
**Admiral Somme**: Did you catch them?

**伊戈尔将军**：处决了一部分，剩下的等着移送总部审讯。\
**Admiral Igor**: Some have already been executed. The rest will be transferred to headquarters for interrogation.

**索姆将军**：很好。你需要什么，同志？\
**Admiral Somme**: Good. What assistance do you require, comrade?

**伊戈尔将军**：军队，可靠的军队。\
**Admiral Igor**: An army. A reliable one.

**索姆将军**：军队？但现在哪里都需要人，恐怕……\
**Admiral Somme**: An army? I'm afraid that's not possible. We simply don't have the men to spare.

**伊戈尔将军**：不用太多。\
**Admiral Igor**: It doesn't need to be large.

**伊戈尔将军**：把我的近卫团都调来圣保罗。\
**Admiral Igor**: Just dispatch my Sentinel Unit from Buenos Aires to São Paulo.

一支忠诚的军队，由他亲自抚养长大的孩子们带领，由这些生而加入芝诺的战争遗孤组成。\
A loyal army led by the children he raised himself, composed of orphans of war born into Zeno's cause.

**伊戈尔将军**：至少让托勒密从布宜诺斯艾利斯调过来。\
**Admiral Igor**: Or at the very least, send Ptolemy.

**索姆将军**：托勒密？噢，你的“孩子”……嗯，不错的方案……\
**Admiral Somme**: Ptolemy? Ah, one of your orphan "children." Hmm. That seems like a feasible solution.

**伊戈尔将军**：没什么人比这些芝诺战友的遗孤更忠诚。\
**Admiral Igor**: Yes, his parents died fighting for Zeno. All my children are loyal to a fault.

**伊戈尔将军**：卡洛斯将军就在这间办公室里被自己人打穿了脑袋。我必须有可信任的士兵。\
**Admiral Igor**: Officer Carlos was shot in the head by one of his own men in this very office. I need soldiers I can trust.

**索姆将军**：喔，伟大的伊戈尔也会怕死吗？\
**Admiral Somme**: Ah, so the fearless Igor is afraid of death, after all?

**伊戈尔将军**：长官被自己的士兵在自己的驻地里杀死，伤害的是芝诺的荣誉。\
**Admiral Igor**: An officer was killed by his own soldiers at his own base. This is an immense stain on Zeno's honor.

仅剩的这点儿荣誉，像是冬日的白桦树叶。\
How little honor they have left. Igor clings to it like a leaf to a tree in winter.

**索姆将军**：如果响应及时，很快你就会见到他们。\
**Admiral Somme**: Indeed. If everything goes according to plan, you'll see your unit shortly.

扣上座机

**伊戈尔将军**：接下来，只是时间问题……\
**Admiral Igor**: Now, it's just a matter of time.

老将军握着骰子，不断抛起、接住，再抛起，再接住。\
The admiral tosses the dice in his hand. Up and down, up and down.

他得到同一句神谕，同一个答案，如同贝希斯敦铭文上的刻写，永恒不灭。\
He receives the same oracle—the same answer—like the inscription on the Behistun monument. It is eternal. Unchanging.

“他的心是只悬挂的琴，悬挂的琴……轻轻一拨……”\
"His heart is a hanging lyre, a hanging lyre ... gently plucked ... "

古老的诗歌在老将军的回忆中泛起。\
An ancient verse rises in the old admiral's memory.

漆黑的信息，不详的预言，从他口中低声吟唱……\
Dark omens. Ill prophecies. It is all whispered from his lips.

视频开始\
I have seen the hawk chase the dove and the sun god pull his golden bowstring taut.

开始\
I watched as the wooden horse was welcomed into our territories, and the sacred fountain flowed with the blood of the fledgling birds.

我看见，鹞鹰追赶鸽子，那远射的太阳神的金弦勒紧，蓄势待出。\
Ah, but a man of steely mind and lofty pride knows ...

阴谋的木马被迎入城墙，敬神的水池遍流鸽子血。\
That his city will endure. Its walls will stand strong. It will be as steadfast as the earth's core.

啊，可他的心，和他那高山般骄傲的灵魂也深深地知晓……\
What wickedness ...

他的城邦永存，他的高墙牢固，好像大地坚实的心灵。\
Now, the die is cast ...

罪恶呵……\
The pale shroud will devour him, and he will be enveloped by the grim night.

骰子已经掷出……

苍白的大氅，死夜的阴翳把他笼罩。

**伊戈尔将军**：为了明天。\
**Admiral Igor**: All for a better future.

**伊戈尔将军**：所有人的明天……\
**Admiral Igor**: A better future for everyone ...

雨夜中唯一的答案。\
On this rain-soaked night, this is the only answer.

敲门

**莫莉德尔**：将军——\
**Moldir**: Admiral.

**伊戈尔将军**：进来吧。\
**Admiral Igor**: Come in.

开门后关门

**莫莉德尔**：昨天司辰来了联络，报告德洛丝医生被天使兄弟会绑架，现在她正和洛佩拉商讨救援事宜。\
**Moldir**: Yesterday, we received word from the Timekeeper that Dr. Dores has been abducted by the Apostles Brotherhood. She should be coordinating with Lopera to set up a rescue operation as we speak.

副官女士松了口气，尽管医生被绑架，但至少得到了司辰生命安全的消息。\
She breathes a sigh of relief. The doctor may have been abducted, but at least the Timekeeper is safe.

**莫莉德尔**：出逃的金伯利女郎也在司辰身边，她自称是被释放的。\
**Moldir**: Also, that girl who escaped, Kimberly, is with the Timekeeper. She claims that she was released.

**伊戈尔将军**：嗯，承认她的谎言吧，洛佩拉没必要知道真相。\
**Admiral Igor**: Just play along with her lie. There's no need to tell Lopera the truth.

**莫莉德尔**：请原谅，当时时间紧迫，我私自答应了她……对方要求我们拿洛佩拉抓回的俘虏换回医生，如果再不做决定，他们恐怕就会……\
**Moldir**: The Brotherhood has demanded that we exchange the detained deserters for the doctor. Forgive me for issuing instructions without your consent, but if we refuse or ignore them, I'm afraid they'll—

**伊戈尔将军**：就会处决医生。\
**Admiral Igor**: They'll execute the doctor.

老将军很清楚那些暴徒的做派。\
He knows full well the ways of these thugs.

**伊戈尔将军**：你怎么安排的？\
**Admiral Igor**: What arrangements did you make?

副官女士很紧张——她越过将军，私自做出了安排。\
Moldir tenses up a little, unsure of how her father will react to her decision.

**莫莉德尔**：我告诉她，芝诺的援军会到荣军院找她。\
**Moldir**: I told the Timekeeper that Zeno reinforcements would meet her at the Veterans' Residence.

**莫莉德尔**：让洛佩拉去侦察交接地点，她熟悉那儿。\
**Moldir**: Since Lopera is familiar with the place, I also asked her to scout out the rendezvous location.

**莫莉德尔**：包括对金伯利的安排……和您说的一样。父亲，我……我认为您也会这样做。\
**Moldir**: And, yes. I played along with Kimberly's lie. I-I assumed you would've done the same, Father.

**伊戈尔将军**：非常好。\
**Admiral Igor**: Very good.

副官女士做出了模仿父亲的安排——在昨晚，在老将军拒绝接见任何人时。\
While the admiral refused to talk to anyone last night, his daughter had been modeling her actions after him.

**伊戈尔将军**：很快你会有一支部队，带他们去接应洛佩拉，救回医生。\
**Admiral Igor**: Your squad will soon arrive. Take them to Lopera at the rendezvous point and bring the doctor back.

**莫莉德尔**：部队……？\
**Moldir**: A squad?

老将军望向窗外。\
The admiral gazes out the window.

阳光之下，萧条荒芜，时间溶解在石头里，绿藤攀绕柱廊，这座仿自安达卢西亚风貌建造的废旧城堡，就是如今芝诺分部的基地所在。\
He scans the barren fort, the weathered stone, and the vines slowly wearing away at the walls. How did this come to be?

**伊戈尔将军**：我跟总部通了电话，顺利的话，托勒密他们很快就会到。\
**Admiral Igor**: I've spoken with headquarters. All going well, Ptolemy and the unit will arrive soon.

副官女士长舒一口气，为即将和家人重聚而露出笑容。\
Moldir's body relaxes a little, and a smile grows on her face.

**莫莉德尔**：原来如此……很久没聚在一起了。\
**Moldir**: I see. I can hardly remember the last time we were all together.

她的笑容开始变得有些苦涩。\
Her smile turns bittersweet.

**伊戈尔将军**：你父亲死在阿巴丹，他本来不需要参加那场战役。\
**Admiral Igor**: Your father died in Abadan, in a war he had no obligation to fight in.

**莫莉德尔**：那是我们的荣幸，死在冲锋途中要远比死在病床上光荣。\
**Moldir**: It's far more glorious to die in the throes of battle than to wither away on a sickbed. He made an honorable sacrifice.

**伊戈尔将军**：之后的事，会让他的荣誉蒙上污点。\
**Admiral Igor**: How shameful that we would tarnish his honor.

荣誉蒙上污点，犹如锈迹斑斑的勋章。\
Honor is a thing easily stained.

**伊戈尔将军**：先谈谈那个叫红弩箭的年轻人。关于她，说说你的看法。\
**Admiral Igor**: Let's begin with that young pilot, Lilya. Tell me, what do you think of her?

**莫莉德尔**：训练有素，经验丰富，脾气很直，和洛佩拉在某些方面很像。\
**Moldir**: She's well-trained, experienced, a straight shooter—similar to Lopera in many ways.

**伊戈尔将军**：她一身都是斯拉夫人的臭脾气，我太了解我的同胞了。\
**Admiral Igor**: She's a true Slav. Just like my brothers and sisters back home.

顽固，忠诚，勇敢，又像封冻的西伯利亚大地般不可动摇。\
Stubborn, loyal, brave, and as unshakable as the frozen Siberian earth.

**伊戈尔将军**：她比洛佩拉幸运，不用生来就背负叛徒的骂名。\
**Admiral Igor**: I suppose she's luckier than Lopera. Not destined to become a traitor like her.

**莫莉德尔**：洛佩拉只是个孩子。\
**Moldir**: Lopera's still a child, really.

老将军合上眼，回忆着一个个曾与自己并肩作战的名字。\
The admiral closes his eyes as he remembers those who fought beside him.

**伊戈尔将军**：很多人都死了，死于战争，没于“暴雨”。\
**Admiral Igor**: So many lives have been lost, in wars, in the "Storm."

现在，他们都成了总部纪功廊里的一个个铭刻。\
They have all been enshrined in the Hall of Merit at headquarters.

**伊戈尔将军**：你觉得洛佩拉会怎么做？\
**Admiral Igor**: What do you think Lopera will do?

**莫莉德尔**：她也是您的孩子，我认为她会跟我们一起……\
**Moldir**: She's your child, just like me. I think she will stand with us.

长女的回答让老将军笑起来。\
He smirks.

**伊戈尔将军**：你“认为”，而不是相信。\
**Admiral Igor**: You "think," do you?

**伊戈尔将军**：她不重要。来，看看这个。\
**Admiral Igor**: Anyway, she's not important. Here, take a look at this.

一封邀请函。\
An invitation.

**伊戈尔将军**：我不会戴上它。\
**Admiral Igor**: I will not wear it.

**伊戈尔将军**：你也不会，我保证，你们都不会戴上这个东西。\
**Admiral Igor**: Nor will you. I promise you, not one of us will wear this thing.

收浮窗

**伊戈尔将军**：还有一封信，来自传达“神谕”的祭司，一份来自传道者的礼物。\
**Admiral Igor**: The Preacher has given us a gift and shared with us an "oracle."

**伊戈尔将军**：而我们也会为她带去回礼。\
**Admiral Igor**: We will bring her something in return.

**伊戈尔将军**：天上降下硫磺与烈火，在废墟之中，我们找回了这一奇迹的残留。\
**Admiral Igor**: Fire and brimstone rained down from heaven, yet among the ruins we recovered the remnants of a miracle.

**伊戈尔将军**：它在生长，在呼吸，它是活着的奇迹。\
**Admiral Igor**: A miracle that is living, breathing, and growing.

**伊戈尔将军**：生命的气息在这捧焦土中积蓄，我听见它的低语。\
**Admiral Igor**: I can sense THEIR life force. I can hear THEIR whispers from within these ashes.

一个清醒的梦境，活着的死亡，坏灭的不朽。\
A lucid dream, a living death, a perished immortality.

**伊戈尔将军**：祂不可战胜，莫莉德尔。\
**Admiral Igor**: Moldir, THEY are invincible.

**伊戈尔将军**：比起向那栋白色石屋无止境地投入孩子们的生命……\
**Admiral Igor**: Rather than endlessly throwing young soldiers' lives to the White Stone House ...

**伊戈尔将军**：我选择我们与真正的未来站在一起。\
**Admiral Igor**: I choose to stand with the true future.

收浮窗

**莫莉德尔**：……\
**Moldir**: ...

**莫莉德尔**：我会和您站在一起，父亲。\
**Moldir**: I will always stand with you, Father.

## 8TH-15 北地骏鹰 / The Northern Falcon

办公室

老将军拿起了一旁的档案，接着翻看起一位年轻飞行员的履历。\
The old admiral picks up the file beside him and flips through the young pilot's records.

**伊戈尔将军**：一个酒鬼。\
**Admiral Igor**: Arcanist. Abuses alcohol ...

**伊戈尔将军**：一个爱打架的小神秘学家。\
**Admiral Igor**: And loves to fight.

**伊戈尔将军**：传令兵！\
**Admiral Igor**: Messenger!

**伊戈尔将军**：叫红弩箭中尉到校场等我。\
**Admiral Igor**: Call Lieutenant Lilya. Tell her to meet me at the training ground.

老将军从椅子上动身，走向校场——在那儿，叛徒的血迹还染红着荒草。\
He rises from his chair and heads to the training ground, where the blood of the traitors still stains the grass.

年轻的飞行员举着酒壶，走向老将军。\
Lilya approaches the admiral, her flask clutched in her hand.

**伊戈尔将军**：和我们家乡的酒比起来，味道怎么样？\
**Admiral Igor**: How does it compare to the drink back home?

**红弩箭**：喝了之后犯困，又困又醉，让人没精神。\
**Lilya**: This stuff saps your energy. Makes you feel sleepy.

**伊戈尔将军**：就像这片土地，一直都沉浸在半生半死的醉意里。\
**Admiral Igor**: Just like this land. This place is always submerged in a half-dead stupor.

**伊戈尔将军**：贫穷，混乱，未来比天上的太阳离他们更远。\
**Admiral Igor**: Poverty. Chaos. To them, the future feels farther away than the sun beating down from above.

抬头是照亮大地的太阳，而生活却像在下水道里跳舞。\
While the sun casts its light from above, many choose to dance in the darkness of the sewers.

**伊戈尔将军**：告诉我，中尉，你眼中的基金会是什么样的？\
**Admiral Igor**: Tell me, Lieutenant. What do you think of the Foundation?

**红弩箭**：这是试探吗？\
**Lilya**: Is this some kind of test?

**伊戈尔将军**：这是一位老人的好奇心，他想知道年轻人是怎么看待那个组织的。\
**Admiral Igor**: No, no. Just the curiosity of an old man. I often wonder how the younger generation views the organization.

**红弩箭**：比起重塑之手的疯子来说，基金会至少还能讲道理。\
**Lilya**: Well, unlike those Manus maniacs, the people at the Foundation are at least open to reason.

**红弩箭**：啊，他们很固执，但总的来说，我觉得基金会都还算是好人。\
**Lilya**: Don't get me wrong, they are stubborn. But overall, I think they're good people.

**红弩箭**：比如说司辰的那个小跟班。\
**Lilya**: The Timekeeper's red-headed sidekick, for example.

十四行诗，被困于文书与行政事务而无法与司辰一同来到圣保罗的那位十四行诗。\
Sonetto is too busy with administrative work to join the Timekeeper in São Paulo.

**红弩箭**：规矩，制度，法条律令……说真的，很没意思，但要是一切都乱了套，那就更坏了。\
**Lilya**: She's a stickler for the rules. But it's so boring to follow all the regulations. That being said, it'd probably be even worse without them. Total chaos, actually.

**红弩箭**：总的来说，基金会里是一群不讨喜的人，但总要有人来干这些不讨人喜欢的活儿。\
**Lilya**: Anyway, at the end of the day, someone has to do the thankless jobs. And the people at the Foundation are the only ones willing to do them.

老将军的眼神中掠过一丝微妙的赞许。\
A subtle hint of approval flickers in the admiral's eyes.

**伊戈尔将军**：芝诺一直以来都是基金会最忠诚的伙伴，我们致力于神秘学家和人类共同的光明的未来。\
**Admiral Igor**: As the Foundation's most loyal partner, Zeno has always been committed to creating a brighter future for both arcanists and humans.

**伊戈尔将军**：对抗重塑之手，也对抗世上的战争和混乱。\
**Admiral Igor**: That includes fighting Manus Vindictae, as well as any other conflicts and chaos in the world.

例如在圣保罗，以芝诺独特的方式维持着这座城市脆弱的和平。\
In São Paulo, for example, Zeno maintains the city's fragile peace in its own unique way.

**红弩箭**：嗯哼，一把枪，指哪儿打哪儿。\
**Lilya**: Uh-huh, it's a mindless gun. The Foundation points, and Zeno shoots.

**伊戈尔将军**：“暴雨”让大多数没能得到保护的士兵成为了“必要的牺牲”。\
**Admiral Igor**: Precisely. Countless soldiers have perished in the "Storm," and they've all been deemed "necessary sacrifices."

**红弩箭**：我不喜欢芝诺干的这些事。\
**Lilya**: I have to tell you, I don't like Zeno's role in all this.

**伊戈尔将军**：没错，但这也是命令。\
**Admiral Igor**: Neither do I. But an order's an order.

**伊戈尔将军**：无异于命令士兵们徒劳地送死，对抗一个不可战胜的敌人。\
**Admiral Igor**: Even if it sends your soldiers to die meaningless deaths against an enemy they couldn't possibly defeat.

**伊戈尔将军**：但我们还是义无反顾地走了过来，一路走到今天，撑着这台摇摇欲坠的战车，在雨幕中行进。\
**Admiral Igor**: Still, we march on without hesitation, pushing our weary bodies deeper into the "Storm."

**伊戈尔将军**：但芝诺还能前进多久？它的履带还能坚持多久呢，中尉？\
**Admiral Igor**: But how much longer can Zeno keep going, Lieutenant? How long until our knees buckle and we fall to the ground?

**红弩箭**：我不知道，也没兴趣知道。\
**Lilya**: I don't know, and I don't care.

年轻的飞行员又灌下一口甜甜的烈酒。\
She takes another swig of sweet liquor.

酣甜如梦，沉沦至死。\
Sweet as the oblivion of a dream.

**伊戈尔将军**：阿尔卡纳没有死。\
**Admiral Igor**: Arcana isn't dead.

**伊戈尔将军**：真空弹轰击过后，我们监听到了爆炸中的生命信号。\
**Admiral Igor**: We detected life signs after the explosion of the vacuum bomb.

**红弩箭**：不可能。\
**Lilya**: That's impossible.

**伊戈尔将军**：是啊，不可能，除非这是神迹。但你相信“神迹”吗？\
**Admiral Igor**: Yes, it is impossible. It would take a miracle for her to survive. Do you believe in miracles, Lieutenant?

**红弩箭**：还不如相信酒鬼的胡话。\
**Lilya**: I'd sooner believe the ramblings of a drunkard.

**伊戈尔将军**：可总有人愿意相信奇迹，追随为他们展现奇迹的人，像羊群走向牧人。\
**Admiral Igor**: That may be the case, but when a miracle worker appears, there will always be people who follow them, like sheep follow a shepherd.

**伊戈尔将军**：前些日子的逃兵事件我并不意外，真正让我感到震怒的是他们枪杀了自己的长官。\
**Admiral Igor**: So, when the desertion incident occurred, I wasn't surprised. I was infuriated, however. Not because they abandoned Zeno, but because they murdered their own officer.

**红弩箭**：该死的叛徒。\
**Lilya**: Damn traitors.

**伊戈尔将军**：在第一场“暴雨”到来前，中尉，我们的军队中人类和神秘学家相处融洽。\
**Admiral Igor**: Back before the first "Storm," human and arcanist troops got along well.

**伊戈尔将军**：重要的不是血管里流淌着哪个种族的血，而是团结在部队番号下。\
**Admiral Igor**: We set aside our origins and united under a common banner.

**伊戈尔将军**：我们不是同胞，而是同志。\
**Admiral Igor**: Our bloodlines meant nothing next to our bond as comrades in arms.

**伊戈尔将军**：但“暴雨”改变了一切。\
**Admiral Igor**: But the "Storm" changed everything.

时代倒流，神秘学的辉光在一次次倒退的时代中越发灿烂。\
Time rolled back, and with each regression, the brilliance of arcanum shone ever brighter.

也让往日的同袍间渐渐生出了隔阂。\
Eventually, it formed a rift between them.

**伊戈尔将军**：作为军人，我必须遵照命令向上级送去我的士兵。\
**Admiral Igor**: As a soldier, I must obey my superiors. I sent my men as ordered, no question asked.

**伊戈尔将军**：但……\
**Admiral Igor**: But ...

老将军欲言又止。\
Igor looks hesitant.

**伊戈尔将军**：但他们会把士兵牺牲在什么地方？就像战争，总有些事情没法用简单的“善恶”来论断。\
**Admiral Igor**: Does it really make no difference if the place they die a martyr's death isn't a battlefield? Like war, these things are never simply a matter of "black and white."

**伊戈尔将军**：中尉，司辰在你眼中是什么样的人？\
**Admiral Igor**: Lieutenant, what do you think of the Timekeeper?

**红弩箭**：她很可靠。\
**Lilya**: I trust her completely.

她用一个简短却强而有力的词做出论断。\
Her statement is short and powerful.

**伊戈尔将军**：嗯，我也完全相信你会为那位年轻的司辰牺牲自己。\
**Admiral Igor**: Sounds like you'd gladly sacrifice yourself for her.

**伊戈尔将军**：我们缺少的正是像她这样的领导者。\
**Admiral Igor**: We need more leaders like the Timekeeper.

**伊戈尔将军**：唉。\
**Admiral Igor**: *sigh*

**伊戈尔将军**：重塑之手和他们，何尝不是一枚硬币的不同面呢？\
**Admiral Igor**: Manus Vindictae, the Foundation. They're just two sides of the same coin, aren't they?

老将军叹了口气，随即向红弩箭发出邀请。\
He sighs again. Then he extends Lilya an invitation.
