**伊戈尔将军**：基金会，和平安全理事会，重塑之手……\
**Admiral Igor**: The Foundation, the Pax Security Council, Manus Vindictae ...

**伊戈尔将军**：你认为你们的那位司辰——她最终会选择一条什么样的道路，中尉？\
**Admiral Igor**: Which path do you think the Timekeeper will eventually take, Lieutenant?

**红弩箭**：我相信维尔汀。\
**Lilya**: I trust in Vertin's decision.

**伊戈尔将军**：嗯……我明白了，这就是你的答案。\
**Admiral Igor**: Hm. I see.

**红弩箭**：这是芝诺对我的试探吗？\
**Lilya**: Are you sure this isn't a test from Zeno?

**伊戈尔将军**：不，这和芝诺无关，只是我个人的一点兴趣。和伊戈尔有关，但和伊戈尔将军无关。\
**Admiral Igor**: No, this has nothing to do with Zeno. Right now, I speak to you as simply Igor, not the admiral.

老将军挥挥手，转身离去，留下年轻的飞行员独自留在原地。\
With a wave of his hand, he takes his leave.

老将军的身影消失在阴影中，士兵们却匆匆赶来，将飞行员包围。\
As he vanishes under the shadow of the colonnade, soldiers rush into the training ground. They surround Lilya, their guns pointed firmly at her.

**红弩箭**：什么意思？\
**Lilya**: What's going on?

**莫莉德尔**：为你试图袭击伊戈尔将军的罪行，红弩箭中尉。\
**Moldir**: Lieutenant Lilya, you are under arrest for the assault on Admiral Igor.

一个谎言，令不善说谎的副官女士耳根升红。\
A lie that makes Moldir's ears turn red with shame.

**红弩箭**：袭击？\
**Lilya**: Assault?

一个罪名，但无需对应的罪行与之匹配。\
A crime for which no evidence need be provided.

**红弩箭**：……我懂了。\
**Lilya**: Oh, I get it.

飞行员握紧她心爱的坐骑，可靠的红色38会永远与它骄傲的空中骑士在一起。\
She grips her trusty Red 38. After what happened in Texas, it hasn't left her side.

**莫莉德尔**：解除武装，中尉。\
**Moldir**: Stand down and surrender, Lieutenant.

面对芝诺卫队的枪口，飞行员拿起酒壶，干得一滴不剩。\
Lilya downs the contents of her flask.

**红弩箭**：这儿的酒都跟个孬种一样。\
**Lilya**: Tsk, even the booze here tastes lame.

**红弩箭**：想拿下我，你们总该先把我揍趴下吧？\
**Lilya**: Come on, then. You're not taking me down without a fight.

**莫莉德尔**：开枪。\
**Moldir**: Soldiers! Fire!

升空\
跌落

混战没有给飞行员升上天空的机会，在搏斗中，她渐渐寡不敌众。\
It's useless. There are far too many of them for Lilya to escape.

**莫莉德尔**：你的反抗没有意义，中尉。\
**Moldir**: There is no use resisting, Lieutenant.

抓住

飞行员还是被缴械了武装，由两名士兵押跪在地，双手反绑背后。\
Disarmed, Lilya is forced to her knees, and her hands are bound behind her back.

**红弩箭**：伊戈尔打算做什么！\
**Lilya**: Tell me, what's Igor planning?!

**莫莉德尔**：父亲会带领我们走向一个不再有毫无意义的牺牲的未来。\
**Moldir**: Father will lead us to a future where meaningless sacrifices are no more.

**莫莉德尔**：他已经掷出了骰子。\
**Moldir**: The die has been cast.

**莫莉德尔**：请原谅，我和你没有私人恩怨。这只是命令。\
**Moldir**: I hope you know that this is nothing personal. I'm just following orders.

冰冷的命运，像吹过玛丽·伯德地的寒风。\
A fate as cold as the wind that sweeps across Marie Byrd Land.

**莫莉德尔**：把红弩箭中尉带到监禁室，在得到将军或我的命令前，任何人不能伤害她。\
**Moldir**: Take Lieutenant Lilya to the holding cell. No one is to harm her without orders from the admiral or me.

**红弩箭**：什么？\
**Lilya**: What?

禁闭室\
锁链挣扎

**莫莉德尔**：我们是叛徒，中尉。\
**Moldir**: We are traitors to Zeno now, Lieutenant.

她为这个词感到不齿，但依然坦诚。\
Though these words disgust her, she forces them out.

**莫莉德尔**：但我忠于父亲。\
**Moldir**: I am loyal only to my father.

**莫莉德尔**：很遗憾不能在接下来的日子里与你共事。\
**Moldir**: It's a pity, really. I would've liked to work with you in the future.

监禁室里，被锁住脚踝的飞行员正愤怒地看向光亮下的探视者。\
The shackled pilot stares furiously at Moldir's dark silhouette.

**红弩箭**：他早就在谋划这事了吗？\
**Lilya**: How long has he been planning this?!

**莫莉德尔**：传道者给了父亲礼物，也给了我们一条回到未来的道路。\
**Moldir**: Ever since the Preacher gave Father a gift and a path to a brighter future.

**莫莉德尔**：无论是生是死，红弩箭中尉，我绝不会背叛自己的家人。\
**Moldir**: Live or die, Lieutenant, I will never betray my family.

**莫莉德尔**：……\
**Moldir**: ...

铁门慢慢关上，黑暗复又笼罩监禁室的无光之地。交代下安排后，副官女士将钥匙交给守卫，嘱托几句后离开。\
The door closes, leaving Lilya alone in the darkness of the cell. Moldir issues a few instructions to the guard before handing him the key.

她还要迎接即将到来的其他姐妹兄弟们。\
It will soon be time to welcome her brothers and sisters.

为了父亲选择的道路，义无反顾。\
For there is no turning back from the path her father has chosen.

一辆辆卡车驶入基地，来自各地的芝诺精锐由忠于伊戈尔将军的年轻军官们率领着，赶往基地。\
Trucks led by young officers loyal to Admiral Igor roll into the base, carrying elite Zeno troops from across the country.

为了彻底剿灭重塑之手，为了摧毁天使兄弟会，为了……一位将军所选择的未来。

谎言之中，背叛者的屠刀已然举起。\
To annihilate Manus Vindictae, to destroy the Apostles Brotherhood, and for the future chosen by the admiral.

脚步声\
In a world of lies, the traitor's blade has been raised.

**监狱守卫**：嘘，小同志，别担心，请你稍微忍耐一会儿……\
**Prison Guard**: Don't worry, young comrade. Just hang in a little longer.

**红弩箭**：……？！\
**Lilya**: ...?!

## 8TH-16 “重逢日” / "Family Reunion"

办公室\
After a long wait, father and daughter reconvene.

漫长的等待。

**莫莉德尔**：父亲，托勒密他们到了。\
**Moldir**: Father, Ptolemy and the unit have arrived.

**伊戈尔将军**：啊，负责剿灭重塑之手和“叛徒”的部队到了。\
**Admiral Igor**: Huh. So here they are. The "army of justice" ready to eradicate the Manus and the deserters in one fell swoop.

老将军听着这个“好消息”，取出基金会赠与他的一份礼物。\
He picks up a gift he received from the Foundation.

**伊戈尔将军**：上一次“暴雨”中，基金会做出了这个东西。\
**Admiral Igor**: During the last "Storm," the Foundation created this thing.

**伊戈尔将军**：在拉普拉斯和阿派朗学派的合作下，他们成为了盗火的普罗米修斯。\
**Admiral Igor**: And with the help of Laplace and the Apeiron arcanists, they stole the fire of the gods, just like Prometheus.

切浮窗

**伊戈尔将军**：你会怎么选？\
**Admiral Igor**: Which side would you choose?

**莫莉德尔**：我会跟随，而非选择。\
**Moldir**: I wouldn't. I would follow.

**莫莉德尔**：跟随您，无论到哪儿。\
**Moldir**: Follow you wherever you lead.

她用忠诚来回避内心的动摇与不认可。\
Her loyalty is like a shield to protect herself from her inner doubt.

**伊戈尔将军**：派人把史蒂文的遗物带过来。\
**Admiral Igor**: Send someone to bring Stefen's belongings here.

**伊戈尔将军**：这个叛徒的确在蓝手帕旅馆找回了一件重要的东西。\
**Admiral Igor**: That traitor found something important at Tuesday's Motel.

**伊戈尔将军**：托勒密会用得上的。\
**Admiral Igor**: Ptolemy will find it useful.

**伊戈尔将军**：就这样，你先去吧。\
**Admiral Igor**: That's all for now.

**莫莉德尔**：是。\
**Moldir**: Understood.

芝诺基地

**托勒密**：好久不见，姐姐！\
**Ptolemy**: Moldir! Long time no see!

独眼军官迎上前，拥抱自己的长姐，亲吻她的左右脸颊。\
The one-eyed officer steps forward to embrace his older sister, kissing her on both cheeks.

短暂的问候过后，他直接切入话题。\
The conversation gets straight to the point.

**托勒密**：要给那些人类伙计投降的机会吗？\
**Ptolemy**: What do you say? Do we give those humans a chance to surrender?

**莫莉德尔**：重塑之手不会接受人类。\
**Moldir**: *sigh* Manus Vindictae don't accept humans.

**莫莉德尔**：但如果你的手下放他们逃出基地，父亲也不会怪罪你。\
**Moldir**: But I doubt Father would blame you if your men allowed them to escape the base.

一个小小的暗示。\
A hint.

**托勒密**：放过？哈哈，你还想有退路吗，姐姐？\
**Ptolemy**: Escape the base? Haha, Moldir, are you having second thoughts?

独眼军官对姐姐的“善意”发出嗤笑。\
He sneers at his sister's "kindness."

**托勒密**：要么把这条路走到底，要么你我都要跟父亲一起走上刑场。\
**Ptolemy**: Either follow this path to the very end, or show mercy and get Father and the two of us executed.

独眼军官将预先准备好的命令进一步下发给麾下的士官，让他们带着将军的命令回到各自的联队宣读。\
He shouts a few orders to his officers, instructing them to return to their respective units and await the admiral's command.

**莫莉德尔**：你打算像洛佩拉那样，也搞一场处刑吗？用什么罪名？不愿追随叛乱？还是拒绝服从军令？\
**Moldir**: So what, then? You want to have a mass execution like Lopera did? On what charges? For refusing to join the rebellion? Disobeying orders?

**托勒密**：不，不会有审判。\
**Ptolemy**: Oh, no, there'll be no trials.

他凑近姐姐耳边，轻声呢喃了几个词。\
He leans in close and whispers a few words in his sister's ear.

副官女士露出惊讶的神色。\
Moldir's eyes widen.

**托勒密**：我麾下的军官们早就知道了这件事，只等父亲拿定主意。\
**Ptolemy**: All my men know about this plan. We're just waiting for Father's orders.

**莫莉德尔**：所有人都知道？\
**Moldir**: They all know?

**托勒密**：应该说，直到今天仍活着的军官们都知道。\
**Ptolemy**: Well, those who're still alive.

唯有鲜血与坟土能掩埋秘密。\
Only blood and dirt can bury secrets.

**托勒密**：既然重塑之手送来了能让我们穿越雨幕的奇迹，那为什么要拒绝这份神圣的礼物呢？\
**Ptolemy**: The Manus have provided us with a miracle that allows us to survive the "Storm." How could anyone refuse such a sacred gift?

**托勒密**：在真空弹降下的毁灭里，我们可是清清楚楚侦测到了阿尔卡纳女士留下的生命信号。\
**Ptolemy**: Even after the total destruction caused by the vacuum bomb, we still detected life signs.

**托勒密**：没有人能如此——自我们所得知的资料里，没有人。她不可战胜。\
**Ptolemy**: No one in history has ever been able to do that. Lady Arcana is invincible.

**莫莉德尔**：我不关心阿尔卡纳。但是不愿追随我们的士兵可不会束手就擒。\
**Moldir**: I don't care about Arcana. What worries me is that the soldiers who are unwilling to follow us won't just surrender.

**托勒密**：那就开枪。\
**Ptolemy**: Then we shoot them.

独眼军官轻描淡写般说着“开枪”。\
His delivery is disturbingly casual.

要么追随，要么就去死。\
There are only two options: follow or die.

**莫莉德尔**：我不认为这样——\
**Moldir**: I don't think that's—

老将军沿着长廊朝两人走来。\
The admiral strides toward them.

**托勒密**：啊！父亲——！\
**Ptolemy**: Oh, Father!

**伊戈尔将军**：其他人呢？\
**Admiral Igor**: Where are the others?

**托勒密**：去动员属下士兵了。我们等这天很久了！\
**Ptolemy**: They went to rally the soldiers. We've been waiting for this day for ages!

他似乎早就知晓老将军的计划。\
He seems to have known about the admiral's plan for quite some time.

**莫莉德尔**：你很早就知道了？\
**Moldir**: For ages? How long have you known about this?

她不解地看向独眼军官，表情惊愕。\
She looks at Ptolemy, confusion and astonishment in her eyes.

**伊戈尔将军**：孩子们都知道。\
**Admiral Igor**: I told your siblings some time ago.

**莫莉德尔**：那洛佩拉……\
**Moldir**: Then Lopera ...

**伊戈尔将军**：她没必要，她只负责带回德洛丝。\
**Admiral Igor**: She's not part of the plan. Her only responsibility is to bring back Dores.

**托勒密**：德洛丝？那又是谁？\
**Ptolemy**: Dores? Who's that?

**伊戈尔将军**：那不重要。\
**Admiral Igor**: None of your concern.

**伊戈尔将军**：把命令下达给你的士兵，让他们知道该做的事，你还有别的任务。\
**Admiral Igor**: You have other things to worry about. Go issue your orders to your soldiers.

**伊戈尔将军**：莫莉德尔，准备好飞机，我们去火地岛。\
**Admiral Igor**: Moldir, prepare the aircraft. We're going to Tierra del Fuego.

南方，遥远的南方，从大陆尽头远望冰冷的大陆——那儿好像他的故乡。\
All the way to the southernmost tip of the continent. To a place where he can gaze upon that snow-capped land to the south and feel the icy breeze on his face once again.

**伊戈尔将军**：对我们的士兵，你有几成把握？\
**Admiral Igor**: How many of our soldiers do you think will remain loyal?

**托勒密**：八成，神秘学家都会跟着我们走，这没得说，但里面还有很多人类士兵……别担心，我有办法。\
**Ptolemy**: I'd say about eighty percent. The arcanists will follow us, there's no doubt about that, but we still have a lot of human soldiers. Don't worry. I'll be sure to deal with them.

必要的遗憾，必要的牺牲。\
A necessary sacrifice.

**托勒密**：沾上血，能让所有人都更团结。\
**Ptolemy**: The spilling of blood will only unite us further.

同袍的鲜血，沾满罪恶的血之联结。鲜血将淹没退路。\
A betrayal of their brotherhood. But there will be no escape once blood is spilled, for those who shed blood and for those who draw it.

**伊戈尔将军**：拿上这个，明天去圣保罗。\
**Admiral Igor**: Take this and go to São Paulo tomorrow.

消人\
He gestures to the wind-up toy that once belonged to the traitorous officer who stayed at Tuesday's Motel. It's placed beside a G33 syringe and a Flying Arrow M1903 pistol.

一个丑陋的发条玩具，曾属于蓝手帕旅馆的叛逃军官，与G33针管和一把飞矢M1903式手枪放在一块儿。

**托勒密**：是吗？我也去圣保罗？如果她哄不回来洛佩拉，我就用这个小玩具逗她回来？\
**Ptolemy**: Oh, me too? So, if Moldir fails, you want me to use this little toy to get Lopera back?

**伊戈尔将军**：你去荣军院，用这个带回金伯利。\
**Admiral Igor**: No. You will bring Kimberly back from the Veterans' Residence.

**伊戈尔将军**：这是金伯利的封印物，拿着这个，她不能违抗你。\
**Admiral Igor**: This is Kimberly's seal. As long as it's in your possession, she cannot disobey you.

魅魔难以抗拒契约物所有者的意志。\
A succubus cannot resist the will of whoever holds her contract item.

**伊戈尔将军**：我不希望发生冲突，尽可能和平地带她回来。\
**Admiral Igor**: Bring her back peacefully, if possible.

**托勒密**：如果父亲您需要的话，当然。\
**Ptolemy**: Of course, Father.

**托勒密**：如您所愿。\
**Ptolemy**: I will do as you wish.

老将军留下指令，转身离去。\
Instructions given, the admiral leaves.

**托勒密**：那就开始吧，姐姐。\
**Ptolemy**: Right then, Moldir. Let's get started.

独眼军官吹响口哨，召来卫队，发出屠杀的号令。\
He whistles, signaling the guards to begin their massacre.

校场的枪声传入地下室。\
The sound of gunshots echos through the holding cell.

**红弩箭**：外面怎么了？\
**Lilya**: What's going on out there?

无人应答。\
No one answers.

守卫已经离开，飞行员被独自关在禁闭室，听到远方的枪声，感到困惑。\
The guard has already left. Lilya frowns.

**红弩箭**：打起来了……？\
**Lilya**: Is the base under attack?

**红弩箭**：但谁和谁？重塑的人不可能来攻击基地。\
**Lilya**: By whom? The Manus has no reason to launch a frontal assault.

**红弩箭**：天使兄弟会？\
**Lilya**: The Apostles Brotherhood? No, that's even less likely.

她立刻否认了心中这个更不切实际的念头。\
She immediately dismisses the idea.

匆忙的脚步声

强光，开灯

禁闭室

**监狱守卫**：小同志，快走！\
**Prison Guard**: Get out! Quick, comrade!

砸碎铁链

**红弩箭**：打起来了？\
**Lilya**: Are we under attack?

**监狱守卫**：拿着你的东西快走！\
**Prison Guard**: Just take your stuff and go!

守卫将飞行员的武装还给她，叛军也紧跟着赶来。\
The guard hands Lilya her weapons just as the rebels catch up.

**芝诺叛军**：这儿还有！\
**Zeno Rebel**: More enemies over here!

长黑屏

**红弩箭**：同志——！\
**Lilya**: Comrade!

混战之中，将她救出监禁室的同志腿脚中弹，但追来的叛军越来越多。\
Amidst the chaos, the guard has been shot in the leg. Lilya goes to help, but the rebels are closing in fast.

来不及了。\
There's no time.

**红弩箭**：该死……\
**Lilya**: Damn!

又是一道该死的选择题，但这一次她没时间犹豫。\
Another damnable choice, but this time there's no time to hesitate.

**监狱守卫**：是中尉让我来帮您的，祝您顺……利……\
**Prison Guard**: Lieutenant Moldir asked me to help you. Take care—

枪声

**监狱守卫**：啊——！\
**Prison Guard**: Aaah!

她乘上红色38腾空而起，飞行扫出的尾焰冲过叛军的阻拦，将她带出监牢——\
With a running start, Lilya leaps onto her Red 38 and takes off into the air, bursting through the rebels and leaving them choking on her exhaust.

首先是光，然后是风，弥漫着硝烟与死亡气息的烈风。\
First, the bright light of the outdoors hits her; second, the stench of gunpowder and death.

白屏\
Traitors and loyalists.

天空\
Under the sun, their blood glimmers just the same.

叛徒之后，又是不愿追随叛徒的“叛徒”。\
It's plain to see now that their blood paints the courtyard.

只有太阳平等地对待每一滴血。

鲜血舔舐着“阿尔罕布拉宫”的荒芜庭院。

**托勒密**：一个不留！\
**Ptolemy**: Kill them all!

准备射击

**伊戈尔将军**：不，收拢部队。\
**Admiral Igor**: No. Recall your troops and assemble.

望着溃逃的士兵，老将军约束住麾下的叛军，不再追击。\
The remaining loyalists are fleeing. There's no need to pursue them any further.

在父亲的要求下，托勒密不情不愿地传下指令。\
Ptolemy reluctantly passes on the order.

**托勒密**：全体集合。\
**Ptolemy**: All hands, assemble!

集合

**伊戈尔将军**：战斗到此为止。\
**Admiral Igor**: The bloodshed stops here.

没有悬念的战斗结束了。叛军向曾经的战友开枪，用同志的血锻造了一条将所有人牢牢捆绑的锁链。\
An unceremonious end to the battle. The rebels have formed a new kind of blood brotherhood now.

**伊戈尔将军**：莫莉德尔，去圣保罗接人。\
**Admiral Igor**: Moldir, time to head to São Paulo.

**莫莉德尔**：容我冒犯，父亲，如果洛佩拉真的不愿意回来，该怎么办？\
**Moldir**: Forgive me for asking, Father, but what if Lopera refuses to come back?

**伊戈尔将军**：……\
**Admiral Igor**: ...

**托勒密**：要是你不忍心，姐姐，我很乐意替你去见见我们亲爱的妹妹。\
**Ptolemy**: Oh, Moldir, if it's too much for you to bear, I'd be happy to go and see our dear little sister for you.

**莫莉德尔**：不必了，这是我的任务，我会带人找到她。\
**Moldir**: No need. This is my mission. I will get her to come back.

那颗小小的军用定位纽扣仍旧连接着相距遥远的两人。\
The two of them are still linked via the tracker button.

**伊戈尔将军**：我不打算改变安排。托勒密，你负责带回金伯利。\
**Admiral Igor**: There will be no alteration of the mission. Ptolemy, retrieve Kimberly.

命令不容置疑。独眼军官和副官女人乘上两艘快艇，奔赴各自的目的地。\
The order is non-negotiable. Ptolemy and Moldir board their boats and head to their respective destinations.

快艇离开

## 8TH-17 离群的黑羊 / The Black Lamb

荣军院\
The pieces are falling into place. Lopera has gone to the colonel's manor, as Admiral Igor planned.

伊戈尔将军布置好了一切。洛佩拉按照计划去了上校庄园。\
If Mr. Duncan moves quickly, he might make it to the manor in time to meet her.

如果贫民区的邓肯先生够快，也许他来得及去庄园接应洛佩拉。\
The early morning sun scorches the courtyard.

圣保罗的太阳来得很早。阳光烧灼着庭院。\
White Rum is still tucked away in her bottle, fast asleep.

白朗姆陷入了沉睡。盖住瓶塞，回到了她湿润的梦中。

**天使娜娜**：你在等什么？\
**Anjo Nala**: What are you waiting for?

**维尔汀**：伊戈尔将军会派来援军，我们接到要求，在荣军院等待。\
**Vertin**: Admiral Igor has sent reinforcements. We were instructed to await their arrival at this location.

时间在流逝。太阳越来越高，但预想中的援助迟迟没有来。\
Some time has passed. The sun has now risen well into the sky, but the reinforcements are yet to arrive.

**天使娜娜**：伊戈尔？\
**Anjo Nala**: Igor?

听到伊戈尔的名字，她似乎很紧张。\
She tenses up at the name.

**维尔汀**：你认识将军吗？\
**Vertin**: Do you know him?

**天使娜娜**：不、不认识……也不想认识，芝诺人全是疯子。\
**Anjo Nala**: N-No, I don't. And I don't want to know him, either. I want nothing to do with those Zeno madmen!

她认识。她在隐瞒。\
She knows him. She's hiding something.

**天使娜娜**：离他们远点，相信我，维尔汀，他们……\
**Anjo Nala**: Stay away from them, Vertin. Trust me, they—

他们来了。\
They're here.

一个独眼男人，带着一支全副武装的卫队走入荣军院。\
A young man with an eye patch strides into the Veterans' Residence, followed by a squad of soldiers, all armed to the teeth.

**托勒密**：近卫团军官托勒密，向您致意。您好，圣洛夫基金会的司辰小姐。\
**Ptolemy**: Greetings, Timekeeper of the St. Pavlov Foundation. I'm Ptolemy, the Commander of Igor's Sentinel Unit.

托勒密？没人说起过基地里还有这么一位先生。\
Ptolemy? No one at the base has mentioned such a name before.

**维尔汀**：现在出发吗，军官先生？\
**Vertin**: Are we setting off now, Commander Ptolemy?

**托勒密**：出发？不，不急。洛佩拉会摆平的。\
**Ptolemy**: Setting off? No, no. It's Lopera's mission to take care of the doctor.

**托勒密**：我的任务……是您身后那位小姐。\
**Ptolemy**: My mission, well ... It concerns the young lady behind you.

**天使娜娜**：……？！\
**Anjo Nala**: ...?!

**维尔汀**：我没有得到过相关信息。她和芝诺有什么关系？\
**Vertin**: I wasn't informed of this. What does she have to do with Zeno?

是蓝手帕旅馆的事故吗？\
Is it because of what happened at Tuesday's Motel?

**维尔汀**：据我所知，蓝手帕旅馆的案件和她没有关系。那位先生是自杀的。\
**Vertin**: As far as I'm aware, the Zeno officer at Tuesday's Motel committed suicide. Kimberly had nothing to do with it.

**托勒密**：史蒂文？那家伙死了就死了。\
**Ptolemy**: Oh, Stefen? I couldn't care less about him.

不是为了蓝手帕旅馆的事。那是为什么？\
If that's the case, then why is he here?

**天使娜娜**：门……门是自己塌掉的……\
**Anjo Nala**: The door opened all by itself.

门？\
What door?

**托勒密**：金伯利小姐，我是否可以做出这样的判断：被捕的你从基地逃走，现在却和基金会的司辰在一起。\
**Ptolemy**: Hmph. I'm not stupid, you know. Ms. Kimberly somehow escapes the base.

**托勒密**：司辰，我还听说你在离开之前，特地绕路去看了看咱们那座棕色高塔。\
**Ptolemy**: And suddenly I find her with the Timekeeper, who I hear took a detour to a certain tower before she left.

**托勒密**：请给我们一个解释，为什么你要协助来自重塑之手的金伯利小姐逃亡？\
**Ptolemy**: So, Timekeeper, care to explain why you helped Ms. Kimberly, a member of Manus Vindictae, escape?

**维尔汀**：所以关在那座棕色高塔里的人，是金伯利小姐。\
**Vertin**: Oh, so the captive in that tower was Ms. Kimberly?

她没有回应，既不点头，也不摇头。\
She gives him no answer.

**托勒密**：我希望和平解决问题，将军要求我带回金伯利小姐。\
**Ptolemy**: Per the admiral's orders, I will now escort you back to the base, Ms. Kimberly. And please, don't make me resort to violence.

**天使娜娜**：不，我不能和他们回去……\
**Anjo Nala**: No. I'm not going back there.

她在颤抖。脚步慢慢地、慢慢地往后退，但却不敢直接逃跑。\
She takes a step back, her body trembling all over. She's too frightened to run.

**天使娜娜**：你们会杀了我……像杀那些芝诺人……\
**Anjo Nala**: You'll kill me, just like those Zeno soldiers.

士兵们抬起枪口，对准她，就像在校场对准将被处刑的逃兵。\
Ptolemy's soldiers raise their guns, just as the others did when they executed the deserters.

**托勒密**：我们可以合作，金伯利小姐。\
**Ptolemy**: Now, now. Let's just get along, shall we?

**托勒密**：这不是逮捕，而是……邀请。\
**Ptolemy**: This isn't an arrest, Ms. Kimberly. It's an invitation.

他拿出芝诺的“诚意”。\
He reaches into his pocket and reveals Zeno's "sincerity."

**天使娜娜**：……！\
**Anjo Nala**: ...?!

**托勒密**：每一只魅魔都应该顺从她的本能。\
**Ptolemy**: A succubus should follow her instincts.

**托勒密**：服从主人。\
**Ptolemy**: Come on. Obey your master.

一个玩具。不起眼，甚至有些滑稽的发条玩具。而她却被这个东西吓着了。\
A toy. Unremarkable, even ridiculous, yet utterly terrifying to her.

**托勒密**：你曾经离它很近，金伯利。\
**Ptolemy**: You know, you were close, Kimberly. You almost found it.

**托勒密**：的确，它就在蓝手帕旅馆。史蒂文是个蠢货，他不知道这东西是什么。\
**Ptolemy**: It was hidden at Tuesday's Motel, just like you thought. Stefen thought it was just a wind-up toy. Hmph. What a fool.

**天使娜娜**：——还给我！\
**Anjo Nala**: Give it back!

**托勒密**：是的，就是这样。跟我走吧，金伯利，然后……\
**Ptolemy**: Yes, that's the spirit. Come with me, and I'll—

**维尔汀**：不，他不会把那东西还给你。\
**Vertin**: Don't. He's not going to give it back to you.

**天使娜娜**：……！\
**Anjo Nala**: ...?!

**托勒密**：看来你更愿意和司辰待在一起。\
**Ptolemy**: Oh, so you'd rather stay with the Timekeeper.

**托勒密**：金伯利，你应该清楚谁才是真正的主人。\
**Ptolemy**: I guess you need a little reminder of who your real master is.

**托勒密**：士兵们，预备——\
**Ptolemy**: Soldiers, prepare to fire!

开枪\
Kimberly barely moves as she struggles against the command of the seal. Meanwhile, Ptolemy and his troops have taken control of the courtyard.

消停

金伯利挣扎着反抗封印物的号令，而独眼军官和他的部下压制着整个庭院。

切屏

丢枪

**托勒密**：捡起来。\
**Ptolemy**: Pick it up, Timekeeper.

他丢来一支手枪。\
He's tossed a pistol near her.

**托勒密**：我跟你没有恩怨，也不会对倒地的平民动手。\
**Ptolemy**: I hold no grudge against you, and I'm not going to shoot an unarmed civilian.

**托勒密**：选吧，是拿起武器继续战斗，还是向我投降。\
**Ptolemy**: Make your choice. Take the weapon and continue to fight, or surrender.

**托勒密**：投降，我会保证你的自由和安全，但金伯利必须跟我们走。\
**Ptolemy**: If you do surrender, I'll guarantee your freedom, but Kimberly has to come with us.

握起枪。\
She picks up the pistol.

**托勒密**：很好，你做出了选择。拿起枪，然后站起来。现在你有武器了，司辰。\
**Ptolemy**: I see. So you've chosen to fight. On your feet.

切屏

**托勒密**：然后，金伯利，你——\
**Ptolemy**: Now then, Kimberly.

军官露出恶毒的笑容。\
The officer gives a malicious grin.

**托勒密**：去杀了她。\
**Ptolemy**: Kill her.

**天使娜娜**：杀死……维尔……汀？\
**Anjo Nala**: You want me to kill Vertin?

出立绘\
A command as malicious as the look on his face.

被控制\
She doesn't know what to do.

一个和独眼军官的笑容同样恶毒的命令。\
But her bloodline allows her no choice. The seal takes effect, slowly compelling her to obey it.

她陷入了困惑。

魅魔种族的血脉束缚与对封印物的服从本能渐渐开始发挥作用。

拿起机器人

**托勒密**：……我耐心有限。\
**Ptolemy**: Come on, my patience has its limits.

托勒密举起发条玩具，像暴风雨中托起灯塔。\
Ptolemy raises the wind-up toy, like a lighthouse beacon in a storm.

**托勒密**：服从我，士兵。\
**Ptolemy**: You will obey me!

现场\
Compulsion. An attack so swift that there is no time to react.

打斗\
The succubus looms over, her eyes hollow, her beastly claw poised to strike.

倒下\
Ptolemy will say anything to ensure she enacts his will.

紧接着是让人来不及反应的……袭击。

单身摁住，起爪

被迫接受号令的“士兵”双眼空洞，抬起左臂，亮出兽的利爪。

独眼军官在一旁煽动、怂恿，给出他不会兑现的承诺。

**托勒密**：动手吧，恶魔，只需要一个陌生人的血，就能为自己赎买自由。\
**Ptolemy**: Do it, demon. Your freedom for the life of a stranger.

单身摁住，攻击\
...

震屏

……

闭眼

**托勒密**：杀死她，证明你的忠诚，我保证这个玩具立刻会回到你手中。\
**Ptolemy**: Yes, kill her. Prove your loyalty. Then I'll give you back your toy, I promise.

远看\
The succubus wraps her claws around her neck.

疼痛与窒息的恐惧随即而来。

**天使娜娜**：维尔汀……不……我不想……\
**Anjo Nala**: Vertin ... I ... I can't ...

控制强化\
The command has taken hold of her, but still, she's wavering.

命令仍在生效，但她在……动摇，痛苦地动摇。\
Meanwhile, Ptolemy, like a sadistic spectator in a coliseum, wills their struggle to go on.

而托勒密则像斗兽场上喝彩的暴徒，继续着这一恶趣味的“战斗”。

**托勒密**：司辰，举起枪。\
**Ptolemy**: Raise your gun, Timekeeper.

抓住维尔汀\
Gun ... yes ... I have a gun ...

枪……对……还有枪……\
But breathing ... strength ... it's all ...

可呼吸……力气……全都……

**托勒密**：对准她，然后扣动扳机。\
**Ptolemy**: Aim at her and pull the trigger.

抓住维尔汀2\
...

……

**托勒密**：如果你想活着，你就得对着这怪物开枪，因为她要杀了你。\
**Ptolemy**: This monster's going to kill you. You'll have to shoot her if you want to live.

独眼军官挑动着仇恨与冲突。\
Ptolemy presses further, eager to get a show.

抓住维尔汀3

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

娜娜意志中的反抗无法对抗身体本能的行动。\
No matter how hard she resists, the succubus within her must obey.

那股强大而无法挣脱的力量继续勒紧脖子，几乎无法呼吸。\
Her claws tighten around her neck. She can hardly breathe.

娜娜流泪

**天使娜娜**：不，我不要……\
**Anjo Nala**: No, I don't ...

她的挣扎就像她的泪水般徒劳。\
Her struggle is as futile as her tears.

**托勒密**：这是命令。\
**Ptolemy**: Obey your master.

露出爪子\
Her claws start to sink into her neck.

她的爪子形同一种危险命运的隐喻。

**托勒密**：对，就是这样。\
**Ptolemy**: Yes. Give in. Just like that.

**托勒密**：看，金伯利，她不会被你杀掉。她拿起了枪，她想杀你，为了自救。\
**Ptolemy**: Look, Kimberly. She picked up the gun. Shouldn't you kill her before she kills you?

**托勒密**：她爱惜自己胜过爱你。她会打穿你的心脏，因为她恐惧你、厌恨你、唾弃你。\
**Ptolemy**: She obviously values her own life over yours, and she won't hesitate to fire a bullet through your heart. To her, you're just a horrifying beast.

**托勒密**：因为你是魅魔，是要被契约要求服从的魔鬼。\
**Ptolemy**: I mean, look at you. You're a succubus, a demon born to be bound to a master! Born to be controlled!

独眼军官的轻蔑和傲慢一览无余。\
His contempt is palpable.

娜娜流泪2

**天使娜娜**：不！我、不想……！！\
**Anjo Nala**: No! I-I don't want to!!

她在拒绝。\
She's pleading.

她痛苦的眼泪如雨点般落下。\
Tears pour down her cheeks.

**天使娜娜**：不想逃跑……不想再服从……不想……我……\
**Anjo Nala**: Please. No more orders. No more running. No more.

**天使娜娜**：不想像姐姐……那样……\
**Anjo Nala**: I don't want to be like my sister.

那样被抓捕，然后被处刑，然后流亡，然后躲藏。然后落入没有尽头的躲藏。\
Hiding away for all those years, living no kind of life at all, only to be captured and executed.

**托勒密**：那就杀了她，折断她的脖子。\
**Ptolemy**: If that's what you want, then kill her. Break her neck.

**托勒密**：我以我的名义发出号令：杀死维尔汀！\
**Ptolemy**: Now, heed my order and kill Vertin!

娜娜伸手\
She does everything she can to resist the command, yet her body is compelled to follow.

她抗拒着命令，身体却不由自主地一点点靠近过来。\
She raises a claw. It hangs in the air, like a butcher's knife ready to slice its meat.

她举起爪子，像握起屠刀。

**托勒密**：用她的死结束你的痛苦，魅魔。\
**Ptolemy**: End your suffering with her death.

**托勒密**：服从，无需思考。\
**Ptolemy**: Don't think. Just obey.

握紧脖子的力量越来越强。\
Her grip tightens.

但还能握紧手枪，还有力气，还有机会……\
The pistol ... Get it. There's still a chance.

**天使娜娜**：松开……松开她……\
**Anjo Nala**: L-Let go. Let go of her.

她在哭。\
She's sobbing.

**维尔汀**：娜娜……\
**Vertin**: Nala ...

维尔汀举起枪\
Aim ... at him ...

瞄准……他……

枪声

## 8TH-18 台风眼 / Eye of the Hurricane

枪声

**天使娜娜**：维尔汀……？\
**Anjo Nala**: Vertin?

子弹射出枪口，朝着空中长长的白色尾迹飞去。\
The bullet flies from the barrel, trailing a long, white streak through the air.

独眼军官手中的发条玩具被贯穿了。这个干扰着娜娜心智的、她苦苦寻找的造物开始碎裂。\
It pierces the wind-up toy in Ptolemy's hand—the tool of Nala's subjugation, that thing that she had so desperately sought, so desperately run away from, is destroyed.

它似乎失去了力量。统御的权能在枪火中覆灭。\
Its power is lost. Its controlling force vanquished by the bullet.

**托勒密**：你……怎么敢！\
**Ptolemy**: H-How dare you!

**维尔汀**：啊……啊……哈啊……\
**Vertin**: *pant*

挤压着喉咙的压力消失了。\
Nala releases her throat.

托勒密那只独眼愤怒地看着发条玩具，又转而看向这边。\
Ptolemy glares furiously at the broken wind-up toy, then shifts his gaze toward them.

荣军院

**托勒密**：我想我们没有谈判空间了，司辰。\
**Ptolemy**: Looks like negotiation's off the table, Timekeeper.

**托勒密**：看来暴力是唯一能说服你的手段。\
**Ptolemy**: I suppose I'll have to turn to violence.

**托勒密**：除了金伯利，其他的不用留情。\
**Ptolemy**: Soldiers, kill them all. Spare no one but Kimberly.

**托勒密**：将军只需要她。\
**Ptolemy**: She's the only one the admiral needs.

而她——娜娜流着血的爪子正紧紧攥成一团。\
Nala looks over her shoulder at Ptolemy, her face twisted in rage, her bloodied claw poised to strike.

她渴望鲜血，就像她在船上那时候也如此渴望食物。\
Blood. His blood. She craves it.

**天使娜娜**：我要把你们全杀了！\
**Anjo Nala**: I'll kill every last one of you!

前进\
The battle quickly becomes a massacre.

前进

前进

蓄力

战斗出乎所有人的预料，变成了一边倒的屠戮。

**芝诺士兵**：该死！！她到底是什么怪物！！！\
**Zeno Soldier**: Damn it! What kind of monster is she?!

**芝诺士兵**：长官——！\
**Zeno Soldier**: Sir!

**托勒密**：保持阵型！后退，开火！\
**Ptolemy**: Maintain formation and fall back. Keep firing!

独眼军官的部队只携带了便捷的通用兵装。\
Ptolemy's troops are only equipped with standard military gear.

没有针对神秘学家的捕获装置，也没有火力强大的重武器。\
No devices to capture arcanists, no heavy firepower.

**天使娜娜**：滚出去！！\
**Anjo Nala**: Go to hell!

愤怒意即痛苦，不是刺向自己，就是向外宣泄。她需要宣泄。\
Anger is pain, and she needs to release it.

要用血来偿还她的眼泪。\
They'll pay for her tears in blood.

**芝诺士兵**：疯子……疯子！！\
**Zeno Soldier**: She's ... She's totally insane!

金伯利抓住步枪，握住枪托砸向倒地士兵的脸。\
Kimberly grabs a rifle and smashes the stock into a fallen soldier's face.

**天使娜娜**：为什么……\
**Anjo Nala**: Why?!

先是爪子，之后是牙。\
First claws, then teeth.

撕扯，然后是撕咬。\
Tearing, biting.

掠过墙壁，划过喉咙。\
Slashing stomachs, ripping out throats.

如野猫扑捕雀鸟。\
Like a wildcat pouncing on a sparrow.

芝诺的士兵很勇敢，如果不是敌人，他们或许会是最可靠的同伴。\
The Zeno soldiers fought bravely. Had they not been enemies, they might have made excellent allies.

对同伴的忠诚胜过了对敌人的恐惧。\
Their loyalty to each other outweighed their fear of the enemy.

**托勒密**：撤退——！\
**Ptolemy**: Retreat!

一道割痕同样划伤了她。\
A small trickle of blood runs down her cheek.

她无情地走过荣军院的小小院落，为刚才遭受的痛苦与泪水复仇。\
She walks mercilessly through the courtyard of the Veterans' Residence, avenging all she has suffered.

敌人开始撤退了，又或是……开始逃离，有序地逃离，保持了军人的“风度”。\
The enemy starts to retreat, or rather, flee with the "dignity" of a soldier.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

空气中弥漫着苦涩的气息。\
The air is filled with a bitter scent.

**天使娜娜**：……我不是，不是任你们宰割的羔羊……！\
**Anjo Nala**: I-I am not a lamb for the slaughter!

骤雨来得很突然，雨水冲洗着庭院里的血迹。\
The rain comes suddenly, washing away the blood spilled in the courtyard.

结束了。芝诺军人都撤走了。她失去力气，瘫坐在庭院中。\
It's over. They're gone. She collapses.

**天使娜娜**：呜……呜……好痛……\
**Anjo Nala**: *whimper* It hurts.

痛苦。\
Pain.

像是一只长满钩刺的手握紧了她的心脏。\
Like thorns in her heart.

**维尔汀**：事情会好起来的，金伯利。\
**Vertin**: Everything will be fine, Kimberly.

她在哭。破碎的发条玩具就像她破碎的心灵。\
She's crying. The wind-up toy lies nearby, shattered like her spirit.

**天使娜娜**：维……维尔汀……\
**Anjo Nala**: Vertin ...

她摊开手，茫然地望向天空。\
She spreads her hands and gazes blankly at the sky.

**维尔汀**：我在这里，没事的，我在，我们都在。\
**Vertin**: I'm here. It's okay. You're going to be alright.

庭院中，鲜血染红了万寿菊花瓣。\
The marigolds in the courtyard are stained with blood.

满地狼藉。墙边的猫窝在战斗中被炸成碎屑。\
The place is a mess. Mamãe Mariana's cat's den has been blown to pieces.

老人们或许会做几个新的。\
Perhaps she'll make a new one.

**维尔汀**：你不再需要被任何人约束。\
**Vertin**: You're no longer bound by anyone.

**维尔汀**：没有契约，也没有封印。\
**Vertin**: No contract, no seal.

**维尔汀**：发条玩具已经被打坏了。\
**Vertin**: The wind-up toy's been destroyed.

**维尔汀**：它碎掉了，碎成了一地零件。金伯利以后不需要听从任何人的命令。\
**Vertin**: It's been shattered into pieces. You're free, Kimberly. You don't have to take orders from anyone anymore.

**天使娜娜**：金伯利……以后不需要听从任何人的命令……？\
**Anjo Nala**: Kimberly doesn't have to take orders?

**天使娜娜**：娜娜……不再需要听从任何人的命令。\
**Anjo Nala**: Nala doesn't have to take orders.

她重复着这句话，像是泅水的旅人抓住身边唯一的浮木。\
She repeats her words as if she's drowning, and they're the only pieces of driftwood to cling to.

**维尔汀**：来——\
**Vertin**: Come.

雨停了。\
The rain subsides.

圣保罗的阳光重新洒向染血的彩墙。\
And the sun shines again.

**维尔汀**：如果无处可去，或许，你愿意跟我回基金会吗？\
**Vertin**: If you've got nowhere else to go, you can come to the Foundation with me if you like.

**维尔汀**：你为我们对抗芝诺的叛徒，你保护了我。\
**Vertin**: I'll let them know you risked your life to protect me from the Zeno rebels. Anyway, the choice is yours.

她张开嘴，大口呼吸着粘腻的空气。\
Nala breathes heavily.

**天使娜娜**：我……可以……\
**Anjo Nala**: I ... I can choose?

她的迷茫就像她的痛苦。\
Her confusion matches her pain.

**维尔汀**：只要你愿意。\
**Vertin**: Yes, whatever you want.

**维尔汀**：没有人能支配你，不需要服从任何人的命令。你重新属于你自己了。\
**Vertin**: No one can control you anymore. You belong to no master; only yourself.

**天使娜娜**：我……自己……\
**Anjo Nala**: Belong to myself.

她看着自己的手，浓稠的血，像孩子降生时包裹着的血衣。\
She looks down. She's covered in blood, like a newborn baby.

**天使娜娜**：就像姐姐去世时……我第一次……离开那座房子……的时候吗？\
**Anjo Nala**: Like when my sister died, the first time I left home?

**天使娜娜**：就像我在战乱中……来到圣保罗……\
**Anjo Nala**: Like when I fled to São Paulo during the war.

**天使娜娜**：就像……我在热情之家……\
**Anjo Nala**: Like the old days at Heartfelt Home.

**天使娜娜**：……\
**Anjo Nala**: ...

真实，而又遥远的回忆。\
Real, yet distant memories.

它们曾在坚硬的砂砾上磨砺，也曾在幸福的糖浆里打滚儿，它们都是她一个人面对世界时的生活。\
To her, it's as if those times have been rolled in the sweet nectar of happiness.

她差点忘了自己是为了什么才一直选择逃亡。\
For a moment, she almost forgets why she's been running all this time.

**维尔汀**：是的，不依赖也不受控于任何人，你只需要坦然地接受你的生命。\
**Vertin**: Yes, no longer reliant on or under the control of anyone.

**维尔汀**：存在本身如此。\
**Vertin**: Just think about who you are, what you want.

**维尔汀**：从今天起，祝你的新生活一切顺利……娜娜。\
**Vertin**: And enjoy your new life, Nala, starting today.

红弩箭飞行的音效\
A familiar silhouette streaks across the sky.

天空中闪现出一个熟悉的人影。

**红弩箭**：头儿——！\
**Lilya**: Captain!

骑着红色38的飞行员从天而降，带回了更坏的消息。\
Lilya descends, bearing bad news.

## 8TH-19 赌局 / The Gamble

悲伤圣母教堂\
庄园之主叹息着。\
The master of the manor sighs.

**桑托斯**：我等着和芝诺握手言欢，消除今天这个小小的误会。\
**Santos**: All this time waiting for Zeno. I really want nothing more than to clear up this little misunderstanding of ours.

**桑托斯**：伤害您对我没有任何益处，就像圣保罗这座城市，像这个终将被“暴雨”冲刷而去的虚假的时代。\
**Santos**: There's no benefit to me hurting you. I hope only to peacefully return you to your friends and, in return, receive mine.

**桑托斯**：我希望能够和平地把您交还给您的朋友，正如他们也会和平地把我的朋友还给我。\
**Santos**: After all, this city and its false era will be washed away by the "Storm" before long.

**桑托斯**：对不信者，我们有耐心，他们只是没意识到自己是被天光照耀的孩子。\
**Santos**: *sigh* Those poor unbelievers. We were all once like them, yet to realize that we are children bathed in the light of the divine.

**桑托斯**：终有一天，他们会弃暗投明，如同不久前加入我们的芝诺朋友。\
**Santos**: One day, they will turn from darkness to light, just like our Zeno friends did not long ago.

**桑托斯**：而背信者……啊，背信者必须死。\
**Santos**: The apostates, however, they who have abandoned our faith, they must die.

异端与弃誓之人最为可恨。\
Heretics and oath breakers, the most detestable of all.

**桑托斯**：但我很好奇，是什么人攻击了庄园？\
**Santos**: I'm still curious, you know, about who attacked the manor.

**桑托斯**：是谁打扰了天使兄弟会与伟大重塑之手的使者会面？\
**Santos**: Who disturbed the meeting between the Apostles Brotherhood and the messenger of the great Manus Vindictae?

**桑托斯**：还在这儿……\
**Santos**: Who came here?

他踢开脚下的碎石。\
He kicks a small stone at his feet.

**桑托斯**：抓走了我的朋友。\
**Santos**: And took away my people?

**德洛丝医生**：……\
**Doctor Dores**: ...

魔药将盲眼女士的喉咙锁住，让她出不了声。\
The potion has locked the blind doctor's throat. She cannot speak.

**桑托斯**：马坎多或许会把贫民区的事情搞砸，我毫不怀疑，但无妨。\
**Santos**: I wouldn't be surprised if Marcando's already messed things up in the favela, but ...

后退\
他转过身去，留给医生一个背影。\
He turns his back to the doctor.

**桑托斯**：只要他能招来源源不断的年轻人，只要神秘学家同胞们依然愿意走向我们。\
**Santos**: As long as he continues to recruit young arcanists, it doesn't matter.

**桑托斯**：马坎多这样的人就有用处。\
**Santos**: People like him are useful.

**桑托斯**：在他被“暴雨”吞没前，物尽其用。\
**Santos**: Tools to be used to our benefit until they're lost to the "Storm."

**桑托斯**：芝诺不也是这样使用他们的“货币”——可怜的士兵们的吗，医生？\
**Santos**: Isn't that also how Zeno uses their soldiers, Doctor? As currency to be spent and lost?

不愿被白白消耗的硬币逃离了赌桌，却又滚向另一张桌子。\
A chip may roll away from the gambling table, but it will only find itself at another.

这世界不过是一座巨大的赌场，除了上桌，筹码别无选择。\
All the world's a casino, and all the men and women merely chips. We have no choice but to take our place at the table.

**德洛丝医生**：……\
**Doctor Dores**: ...

他望向医生。\
He looks at the doctor.

**桑托斯**：至少，重塑之手会许诺给他们未来，真正的未来。\
**Santos**: At least Manus Vindictae promises these soldiers a future, a future worth looking forward to.

**桑托斯**：“受苦者”必将重生。\
**Santos**: The Sufferer will be reborn.

**桑托斯**：天使兄弟会将随我驶向南方，成为祂的信众，接受祂的试炼，承蒙祂的恩典。\
**Santos**: And the Apostles Brotherhood will sail south with me. We will become followers of the Sufferer, undertake THEIR trials, and THEIR grace will be bestowed upon us.

靠近\
他贴近盲眼女士，在其耳旁低语。\
He leans close, whispering in her ear.

**桑托斯**：无论这张牌桌被清洗多少次，我们都会在祂的庇护下屹立。\
**Santos**: And with THEIR blessing, no matter how many times the world is reversed, we will stand firm.

**桑托斯**：我们是不朽的。\
**Santos**: For we will be immortal.

**桑托斯**：此即昨日，女士。\
**Santos**: Yesterday is within our reach, dear lady.

上校庄园\
孤身潜入庄园的洛佩拉观察着庄园守卫的动向，发现人比预想中更少。\
Lopera crouches in the bushes by the manor, observing the guards' movements. The place is surprisingly light on security.

**洛佩拉**：七八个人，没法闯过去，可恶……\
**Lopera**: Seven, maybe eight, guards? No way to get through. Damn!

身后传来脚步声，像穿过草丛的蛇蟒，小心翼翼向她靠近。\
Cautious footsteps approach from behind.

**洛佩拉**：什么人——？！\
**Lopera**: Who's there?!

**邓肯先生**：圣母在上，可算找到了，哈哈，没想到是我吧！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Oh, sweet Mary, I finally found you! Haha! I bet you didn't expect to see me here, did you?

一个意料之外的伙伴。\
An unexpected ally.

**洛佩拉**：邓肯？但你怎么知道我在这儿……\
**Lopera**: Duncan? How did you know I was here?!

**邓肯先生**：嘘，别出声。荣军院的朋友都跟我说了。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Shh, keep it down now. Our friends at the Veterans' Residence told me everything.

**邓肯先生**：你的司辰朋友送来联络，说你一个人被安排来了庄园。\
**Mr. Duncan**: The Timekeeper said you were going to the manor alone.

**邓肯先生**：啊，看看这儿，多美的绿色啊。你的目标是那座教堂吗？\
**Mr. Duncan**: My, would you look at the beautiful greenery. Are you heading to that chapel?

绿影之外，教堂矗立在荒凉的日光之下。\
Amidst the distant greenery, just past the building before them, peeks the chapel's bell tower.

**洛佩拉**：如果医生就在那儿的话，我得闯进去看看。\
**Lopera**: Yeah. If the doctor's in there, I have to find a way to break in.

**邓肯先生**：怎么打算？在这儿等援军吗？\
**Mr. Duncan**: Do you have any plans? Reinforcements?

**洛佩拉**：援军？不，当然是给老爹和司辰一个惊喜。\
**Lopera**: Reinforcements? No time for that. Just watch. I can handle this myself.

巡逻的守卫看护着通往教堂的路。\
The path to the chapel is well within the sights of the patrolling guards.

**洛佩拉**：老伙计，你敢跟我一起上吗？\
**Lopera**: Unless you dare to join me, old-timer?

老伙计用行动做出了答复。\
The old veteran answers with action.

他转下墨镜，举起吹管——\
He lowers his sunglasses and lifts his blowpipe.

**邓肯先生**：给我两根吹箭。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Give me a few darts.

**洛佩拉**：好，你弄开守卫，我去教堂看看。\
**Lopera**: Okay. Here's the plan: you lure the guards away, and I'll check inside the chapel.

炼金师颠颠坩埚，神秘术驱动的炉火开始燃烧，倒出几根细针般的毒箭，递给老伙计。\
She tilts her crucible and, in the flame of an arcane skill, produces a few poison darts. She hands them to the old man.

**邓肯先生**：我去那边，你盯紧机会过去，对面的林子能藏住你。\
**Mr. Duncan**: Alright. When I take my shot, I'll head that way. You stay hidden in the woods and make your way to the other side.

老人蹲下身子，对准一个倒霉守卫的脖子——\
He crouches, aiming at an unfortunate guard's neck.

咻——\
*thwip*

中箭的小子立刻倒下。\
The guard drops instantly.

**兄弟会守卫**：林子里有人！\
**Brotherhood Guard**: Intruder! Over there!

警报声随之响起。\
Alarm sirens blare.

**洛佩拉**：把他们往河边带。\
**Lopera**: Lead them toward the river.

老邓肯接过同伴递来的烟雾爆弹。\
Duncan catches the smoke bomb tossed by Lopera.

**邓肯先生**：小伙子们，来点刺激的！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Let's make this a little more exciting, shall we, boys?

爆弹在空中划出一道弧线，老邓肯的吹箭刺破了这颗灰色小球儿。\
烟雾弹\
He lobs the bomb, aims his blowpipe, and pierces the bomb in midair.

**洛佩拉**：干得漂亮！\
**Lopera**: Nice shot!

守卫被引开后，她举着枪，走近庄园中央的废弃教堂……\
横切转场1\
横切转场2\
With the guards distracted, Lopera raises her guns and makes her way to the chapel.

**桑托斯**：啊，有人来救您了，女士。\
**Santos**: Ah. It appears someone has come to your rescue, dear lady.

**桑托斯**：这并不让我意外。\
**Santos**: I'm not surprised.

庄园之主注视着被吊起的盲眼女士。在他手中，捏着一个小小的、不起眼的控制按钮。\
Santos gazes at the doctor. He holds a small control button in his hand.

他不介意将这儿化成一片真正的瓦砾堆。\
He has no qualms about reducing this place to a pile of rubble.

**洛佩拉**：医生——！\
**Lopera**: Doctor!

营救者的呼喊回荡在教堂高高的屋顶之下。\
Her shout echoes through the halls of the chapel.

**桑托斯**：喔？是你？\
**Santos**: Huh? It's you!

那位在船上有过一局之缘的小赌徒。\
The little gambler from the ship.

**洛佩拉**：在船上的时候我就该一枪把你脑袋开瓢。\
**Lopera**: I should've put a bullet in your skull back on that ship.

**桑托斯**：你走到了一张错误的赌桌上。\
**Santos**: I'm afraid you're playing the wrong game now.

**洛佩拉**：哼，怎么，赢家会得到德洛丝医生吗？\
**Lopera**: Oh, yeah? So what does the winner get this time? Dr. Dores?

她走向布道台上的敌人。\
She steps toward the enemy on the pulpit.

庄园之主张开双臂——\
Santos spreads his arms.

**桑托斯**：不，什么也不会得到。\
**Santos**: No, there are no prizes.

**桑托斯**：我们都是风中的尘土。\
**Santos**: You and I are nothing but specks of dust in the wind.

子弹掉落\
丢枪\
拳打\
洛佩拉打空了子弹，卸掉左轮枪，冲上去徒手追击受伤的对手。\
右移\
打拳\
左移\
打拳\
Guns emptied, Lopera drops her revolver and charges at her opponent with nothing but her fists.

**洛佩拉**：看来赢的还是我。\
**Lopera**: Looks like I win again.

靠近\
跌倒\
勒住\
她踢倒已经无力的桑托斯，扼住脖子，另一只拳头停在空中——\
She kicks the weakened Santos to the ground, pinning him by the throat, her fist poised.

**桑托斯**：是的，你赢了赌局。\
**Santos**: Yes, yes, you won this round.

他倒在瓦砾堆中，嘴角流血，面对洛佩拉即将落下的拳头，却微笑起来。\
He lies among the rubble, blood trickling from his mouth, smiling as Lopera's fist hovers above him.

**桑托斯**：但赌桌呢？\
**Santos**: But I'm afraid there won't be a table left to play the next.

**桑托斯**：别了，小赌徒。\
**Santos**: So long, little gambler.

**洛佩拉**：什么？！\
**Lopera**: What?!

**桑托斯**：如果你觉得，我比你那位盲眼的朋友更重要的话……\
**Santos**: Perhaps it's time you paid a little more attention to your friend.

操作\
He presses the button in his hand. After a loud bang, the chapel starts to crumble.

爆炸\
In Lopera's moment of distraction, Santos kicks her away.

爆炸消除\
He vanishes amid the chaos of the explosion.

桑托斯按响按钮，爆炸声与震落的墙砖一同袭来。\
只是对手的一瞬迟疑，桑托斯奋尽力气，踢开洛佩拉。\
随后便在爆炸的混乱中，自告解室隐匿而去。\
留下圣像倒塌，烛火熄灭。\
Now there is no one but Lopera, the doctor, and a building that's about to crush them both.

**洛佩拉**：该死的！\
**Lopera**: Crap!

她忍住疼痛，咬牙跑向布道台，救下被绑着的盲眼医生。\
She grits her teeth and runs to the pulpit, freeing the bound doctor.

**德洛丝医生**：……\
**Doctor Dores**: ...

医生试图开口，但魔药的效力依然封锁着她的喉咙。\
She tries to speak, but the effects of the potion still hold her throat in a tight grip.

**洛佩拉**：有话回去再说。\
**Lopera**: We can talk after we get out of here.

她背起医生，艰难穿过碎石与爆炸引起的浓烟，撤出正在崩塌的教堂。\
She hoists the doctor onto her back and carries her through the falling debris.

## 8TH-20 亲爱的你 / Farewell, Pera

上校庄园

**莫莉德尔**：肃清敌人。\
**Moldir**: Eliminate all hostiles.

**莫莉德尔**：找到洛佩拉和德洛丝医生！\
**Moldir**: Find Lopera and Dr. Dores!

按照将军的安排，副官女士来到庄园，根据定位纽扣的指引寻找着定位对象。\
Following the admiral's orders, Moldir has followed the tracker button's signal to the manor.

但她来晚一步，残余的敌人没有交火欲望，见到芝诺军人，纷纷逃开，枪声很快平息。\
But she has arrived too late. What remains of the Brotherhood have no desire to fight. They scatter, putting a swift end to the gunfire.

染血的甘蔗林燃起火焰，在浓烟与血地里，副官女士寻找着医生与她的妹妹。\
The blood-splattered sugarcane field burns, and amidst the smoke and blood, Moldir searches for the doctor and her sister.

黑幕转场\
Just as the chapel collapses, Lopera makes it through the front door.

上校庄园

在教堂倒塌前，洛佩拉顺利带着盲眼医生来到教堂外。

**洛佩拉**：天使兄弟会呢？\
**Lopera**: Huh? Where have the Brotherhood guards gone?

找上她的，不是邓肯老头儿，也不是兄弟会的守卫……\
Neither Duncan nor the Brotherhood guards greet her.

**洛佩拉**：——啊，姐姐！\
**Lopera**: Oh, Molly!

**莫莉德尔**：还好定位纽扣没出问题，总算找到你了。里面怎么回事？\
**Moldir**: Pera! Thank goodness this tracker button still works. What happened in the chapel?

**洛佩拉**：跟桑托斯打了一架。他溜了，没办法……但……你不是该去荣军院？\
**Lopera**: I had a fight with Santos, but he got away. Weren't you supposed to go to the Veterans' Residence?

她为自己小小的失败露出苦笑——这仍是胜利，尽管不够完美。\
She flashes a brief, bittersweet smile. This is still a victory, albeit an imperfect one.

**莫莉德尔**：救出医生最要紧。\
**Moldir**: Rescuing the doctor is our top priority now.

盲眼女士护着打字机，正坐在庄园的泥地上。\
Doctor Dores sits on the muddy ground, cradling her typewriter.

**莫莉德尔**：看到您没事真是太好了，医生。\
**Moldir**: I'm so glad to see you safe, Doctor.

**莫莉德尔**：干得不错，洛佩拉，现在跟我回基地。带上这位女士一起。\
**Moldir**: Great job, Pera. Let's head back to the base with Dr. Dores.

**洛佩拉**：司辰呢？\
**Lopera**: What about the Timekeeper?

**莫莉德尔**：她……她有基金会的新任务，那和我们没关系。\
**Moldir**: She's on a new mission assigned by the Foundation. It's got nothing to do with us.

**莫莉德尔**：父亲要我立刻带你和医生回基地去。\
**Moldir**: Father wants me to bring you and the doctor back to the base as soon as possible.

**洛佩拉**：什么意思？为什么变成了……到底怎么回事？\
**Lopera**: What do you mean? Why the sudden change of plan? What's going on here?

这不是计划中的安排。事情很突然。\
No one told her about this.

**莫莉德尔**：一起走吧，我们要撤出圣保罗了。\
**Moldir**: Just come already. We're evacuating São Paulo.

撤离？她没听说过有这个安排。\
Evacuating? Since when was this the plan?

**洛佩拉**：撤去哪里？\
**Lopera**: Evacuating? To where?

**莫莉德尔**：洛佩拉，服从命令。\
**Moldir**: Just follow your orders, Lopera.

**洛佩拉**：……\
**Lopera**: ...

**莫莉德尔**：父亲让我来接你走。\
**Moldir**: The admiral sent me to pick you up.

**洛佩拉**：那为什么他没有亲口告诉我？\
**Lopera**: Then why didn't he tell me any of this?

**莫莉德尔**：父亲有自己的考虑！\
**Moldir**: I-I don't know! I'm sure he has his reasons!

情急之中，她用一个无法反驳的理由驳斥了妹妹的质问。\
In her hurry, she presents a reason her sister cannot argue with.

像是意识到了自己的错误，副官女士泄了气。\
Recognizing her hastiness, Moldir sighs.

**莫莉德尔**：……唉，好吧，我们去南方。\
**Moldir**: *sigh* Fine. We're heading south.

**莫莉德尔**：火地岛，那儿已经做好接应我们的准备了。走吧，洛佩拉，跟我们一起走。\
**Moldir**: To Tierra del Fuego. They've made preparations for us. Come on, Pera, come with us.

**莫莉德尔**：你、我、父亲、托勒密，还有大家……大家都准备好了。\
**Moldir**: You, me, Father, Ptolemy, everyone. We'll all be there.

**洛佩拉**：大家？为什么没人跟我说过这件事？\
**Lopera**: Everyone? Why didn't anyone tell me about this?

**莫莉德尔**：因为……别问了，赶紧行动，我们时间不多。\
**Moldir**: Because ... *sigh* Pera, you can ask questions later. We don't have much time.

洛佩拉甩开了姐姐伸来的手，退后两步。\
Lopera knocks away her sister's extended hand, taking two steps back.

**洛佩拉**：为什么是火地岛？\
**Lopera**: No. Why are we going to Tierra del Fuego?

**洛佩拉**：为什么时间不多？\
**Lopera**: And why are we running out of time?

**洛佩拉**：你们想做什么？\
**Lopera**: What are you planning to do?

**洛佩拉**：谁在火地岛接应你们？\
**Lopera**: Who's waiting for you in Tierra del Fuego?

她握紧枪，枪口对准雨水浇洗过的土地。\
She grips the revolver on her side.

她的动摇、惊恐和疑惧在冰冷的枪管中犹豫着。\
She hesitates, fear and confusion flashing across her face.

枪是安全的。枪是可靠的。握紧枪的自己是不会被伤害的。\
Her gun is safe. Her gun is reliable. As long as she holds it, she won't be hurt.

接下来，枪口会颤栗着对准眼前之人，正如雨水从天而下。\
She pulls it from its holster and slowly raises the barrel to her sister. With a final crash of thunder, rain starts to pour.

**洛佩拉**：谁在怂恿父亲？托勒密那混账吗？\
**Lopera**: Who's behind all this? That jerk, Ptolemy?

**莫莉德尔**：不……这是父亲的命令。\
**Moldir**: No. Father gave these orders.

面对枪口，莫莉德尔解开枪套，将手伸向自己的枪。\
Moldir unbuckles her holster, reaching for her own gun.

**洛佩拉**：别动！\
**Lopera**: Don't move!

**莫莉德尔**：别这样，洛佩拉，把枪放下。\
**Moldir**: Come on, Lopera. Lower your gun.

黑色手枪从枪套中滑落，跌到地上。枪主人摊开手，以示友善。\
The handgun slips from its holster and falls to the ground. Moldir spreads her hands in a show of friendship—of sisterhood.

**莫莉德尔**：父亲需要她，我们需要这位医生。\
**Moldir**: Father needs the doctor. We need her.

**莫莉德尔**：带上她，回到基地，和我们一起去火地岛。\
**Moldir**: Bring her back to the base and come with us to Tierra del Fuego.

**洛佩拉**：火地岛上有什么？\
**Lopera**: Why? What're you going to do in Tierra del Fuego?

**莫莉德尔**：……未来，属于神秘学家的未来。\
**Moldir**: Seize the future, a future for all arcanists.

**莫莉德尔**：父亲接受了传道者的承诺。\
**Moldir**: Father has embraced the Preacher's promise.

**洛佩拉**：……\
**Lopera**: ...

**洛佩拉**：重塑之手。\
**Lopera**: Manus Vindictae.

一个无法想象的背叛。\
A betrayal she had never imagined.

**洛佩拉**：我的家人没有叛徒。\
**Lopera**: No. My family are not traitors.

过去没有，现在没有，未来也不会有。\
Not in the past, not now, not ever.

追猎者绝不甘愿沦为自己曾经追猎的叛徒。\
A hunter never willingly becomes the prey she once pursued.

**莫莉德尔**：洛佩拉，你可以什么都不做，不为他们做任何事。\
**Moldir**: Look, you don't have to do anything for them if you don't want to.

副官女士慌忙解释，但她甚至不敢看着妹妹的眼睛。\
She tries to explain, but she can't even look her sister in the eye.

**莫莉德尔**：回家吧，跟我一起回家，跟我们一起走。\
**Moldir**: Just come with us. Come home.

回家。\
Home.

收氛围图\
That single word makes Lopera waver.

一个让洛佩拉短暂动摇的词——短暂而遗憾的动摇。

**莫莉德尔**：抱歉，洛佩拉……\
**Moldir**: Forgive me, Pera.

靠近\
Taking advantage of Lopera's moment of hesitation, Moldir launches an attack.

副官女士抓住她陷入动摇的间歇，一步上前，发起攻击。\
As they wrestle, Lopera pulls the trigger, the bullet shooting into the sky and startling a flock of birds.

枪响\
Finally, Moldir wrestles the gun from Lopera's hand and knocks her to the ground. She lies there, winded and in pain.

情急之下，洛佩拉扣动扳机。子弹射向天空，惊走结群的飞鸟，左轮手枪落入了它曾对准的副官女士手中。

洛佩拉被打倒在地，疼痛让她无法动弹，抱腿捂住胸腹，发出一阵阵痛苦的呻吟。

**洛佩拉**：老爹……为什么……\
**Lopera**: Pa ... Why is he doing this?

她不理解。她无暇思考疼痛。\
The pain is the least of her problems. She simply can't understand how things have ended up this way.

慢靠近

**莫莉德尔**：为了我们所有人，妹妹。\
**Moldir**: For the good of us all, Pera.

**莫莉德尔**：你圆满完成了任务，德洛丝女士安然无恙，护送就交给我吧。\
**Moldir**: Consider your mission complete, I'll take over from here.

**莫莉德尔**：洛佩拉同志。\
**Moldir**: Thank you for your service, Comrade Lopera.

脚步声\
Several Zeno soldiers, returning from their sweep of the manor, arrive at the lieutenant's side.

几名穿着芝诺军装的士兵解决了庄园别处的战斗，赶来副官女士身旁。

**芝诺士兵**：这是……\
**Zeno Soldier**: What's going on?

**莫莉德尔**：这里我来处理。\
**Moldir**: I'll handle this.

**莫莉德尔**：带那位盲眼女士离开，保证她的安全，撤退。\
**Moldir**: Take the blind lady and retreat. Make sure she's safe.

抓走\
The doctor offers no resistance, weakly surrendering to fate as she's taken once again.

虚弱的医生无力反抗，只能任由命运再一次将她掳走。\
Moldir looks down at her fallen sister, her gaze cold.

副官女士望向倒地的妹妹，眼神冷漠。

**莫莉德尔**：很遗憾以这种方式和你告别。\
**Moldir**: I am sorry it has to end this way.

副官女士举起枪，对准往日的亲人。\
She raises her gun, aiming at her cherished sister.

**莫莉德尔**：永别了，妹妹。\
**Moldir**: Farewell, Pera.

雨滴像艳红的蟹爪兰般，在洛佩拉被浸湿的胸口盛开。\
The rain grows heavier. Lopera's soaked body lies in the mud.

**邓肯先生**：坏了！难道洛佩拉那边出问题了！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Crap! Has something gone wrong?

混乱枪声

蹲下

**邓肯先生**：等等，等等，怎么回事！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Wait a minute. What's going on here?!

听到枪声，老邓肯停下来，观察着庄园里的状况。\
He pauses at the echoing of the gunshot and scans his surroundings.

**邓肯先生**：芝诺？\
**Mr. Duncan**: Zeno soldiers?

**邓肯先生**：他们怎么来庄园了？\
**Mr. Duncan**: What are they doing here?

出于直觉，也出于当年打仗遗留下的习惯，他没有鲁莽行事。\
As an experienced soldier, he knows not to act rashly.

远处，一位年轻的女军官指挥着士兵与德洛丝医生离开，但队伍中没有洛佩拉的身影。\
In the distance, a young female officer leads the soldiers and Doctor Dores away, but there's no sign of Lopera.

**邓肯先生**：医生？\
**Mr. Duncan**: That's the doctor, isn't it?

**邓肯先生**：洛佩拉怎么不在？\
**Mr. Duncan**: Why isn't Lopera with them?

起来\
Duncan cautiously makes his way to the chapel to search for her.

往前跑\
The rain comes and goes.

等到陌生的军人离开后，谨慎的老邓肯才跑向教堂方向，找寻同伴。

下雨

雨水忽来忽往。

**洛佩拉**：麻醉弹。\
**Lopera**: Tranquilizer bullet.

**洛佩拉**：啊……我明白了。\
**Lopera**: Urgh, I see.

麻醉的药效退去，雨水从天上淋向少女的脸庞。\
As the effects of the tranquilizer wear off, Lopera can feel her soaked clothes sticking to her.

她捡起碎掉的定位纽扣，莫莉德尔射出的子弹将这枚小东西打成了碎块。\
She sees the tracker button. It's been destroyed. Moldir's bullet must have smashed it.

**洛佩拉**：碎掉了吗？\
**Lopera**: It's shattered.

姐姐的枪法一向很准——和她一样。\
Moldir's aim is as sharp as hers. They truly are sisters.

她攥紧纽扣碎片，在手心一点点地、徒劳地将碎片拼成一块。\
She grips the fragments in her palm, trying in vain to piece them back together.

但雨水冲散了一切。\
But the rain washes them away.

**洛佩拉**：父亲……\
**Lopera**: Pa ...

无论生父，还是养父。\
First her biological father, now her adoptive one.

无论背叛，或是拒绝。\
Betrayal. Rejection.

**洛佩拉**：那父亲呢，你又是从什么时候开始谋划的这件事？\
**Lopera**: How long have you been planning this?

没有人回答她，除了从天而降的雨水。\
There is no answer save for a crash of thunder.

所有人都离开了，除了她。\
She has no one but herself.

**洛佩拉**：除了我，你们都知道吗？\
**Lopera**: Am I really the only one who knew nothing about it?

老将军收养的其他孩子都知道吗？\
Did her siblings know?

除了她，其他的家人都知道。\
Did everyone else in her family know?

**洛佩拉**：我从来没有被你们接纳过吗？\
**Lopera**: Was I ever actually accepted into this "family"?

一个苦涩的想法，呛得她胸中一阵火烧般的灼痛。\
The bitter thought burns in her chest like fire.

**洛佩拉**：……\
**Lopera**: ...

她翻身起来，靠手肘强撑住失去力气的身体，一阵一阵地干呕着。\
She forces herself up, her arms shaking as she heaves her body upright.

眼泪融入雨水，她的头发湿透了。\
Tears, rain—they both become one.

**洛佩拉**：得联系上司辰……\
**Lopera**: I have to tell the Timekeeper.

**洛佩拉**：该死的！\
**Lopera**: Crap!

她捶向雨后湿软的土地，双手沾满泥浆。\
She pounds the ground, splattering her fist with mud.

……\
...

大雨洗过庄园。树影之下，一个熟悉的身影钻了出来。\
From the shadows of the trees, a familiar figure emerges.

老朋友找到她，急匆匆地朝她跑来。\
It's Duncan. He's running over to her.

**邓肯先生**：洛佩拉！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Lopera!

这是仅有的好消息。\
Finally, some good news.

**洛佩拉**：邓肯！你没事真是太好了，我们得赶紧——\
**Lopera**: Duncan! You're okay! We have to hur—

起来\
She tries to stand, but her legs give way, and she collapses again.

倒下

她撑着身子站起来，但腿脚一闪，又跌下去。

**邓肯先生**：发生了什么？那些芝诺的人怎么把你一个人丢在这儿？\
**Mr. Duncan**: What happened? Why did your men leave you here all alone?

他扶住虚弱的洛佩拉，而洛佩拉却对他露出一个悲哀的苦笑。\
He supports the weakened Lopera. She gives him a sad smile.

**洛佩拉**：回荣军院，伊戈尔……他……\
**Lopera**: Hurry back to the Residence. It's Igor ... He...

她说不出口。\
She can't bring herself to finish the sentence.

大雨过后，湛蓝的天穹上日光热烈——太阳就如人心，不可直视。\
The sky clears, and the heat of the blazing sun washes over them once more.

## 8TH-21 原爆点 / Ground Zero

荣军院

年轻的魅魔不再哭泣。飞行员看到庭院里的惨状，皱起眉。\
Nala's tears have dried up. Lilya looks around and frowns.

**红弩箭**：看来你这儿也不轻松……\
**Lilya**: I guess you haven't had an easy time either.

雨水和鲜血。\
Rain and blood.

**红弩箭**：坏消息，伊戈尔召集军团叛乱了。\
**Lilya**: I have bad news. Igor's just started a rebellion.

**维尔汀**：……！\
**Vertin**: ...?!

年轻的飞行员大步走来。\
Lilya strides forward.

**红弩箭**：他调了一批援军。\
**Lilya**: He's got an army.

**维尔汀**：……现在情况怎么样？\
**Vertin**: What's the situation at their base?

**红弩箭**：他们在火并，但叛军肯定赢了。\
**Lilya**: Not good. There was fighting and bloodshed. Lots of it. The rebels must've won.

飞行员给自己灌下一大口酒，用酒精抚平情绪。\
She takes a long swig of liquor in an attempt to steady her emotions.

**红弩箭**：一帮混帐！\
**Lilya**: Those traitorous bastards!

**红弩箭**：洛佩拉呢？难道她也一起叛逃了？\
**Lilya**: What about Lopera? Did she defect, too?

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：我不清楚，但她被安排去上校庄园了。\
**Vertin**: All I know is that she was sent to the colonel's manor earlier.

**维尔汀**：但是伊戈尔为什么会……\
**Vertin**: But why would Igor ...?

**维尔汀**：如果洛佩拉也和伊戈尔一起背叛了……\
**Vertin**: If Lopera's also joined the rebellion ...

事情不会比这更糟糕了。\
Worse than expected.

**红弩箭**：老东西把我们全算计了！\
**Lilya**: The old fart set us up!

荣军院里出现了另一位老人的身影。\
A burly figure appears in the entrance to the Veterans' Residence.

老邓肯背着洛佩拉回到了荣军院。\
It's Duncan, Lopera slung on his back.

**邓肯先生**：她受伤了！\
**Mr. Duncan**: She's injured!

**维尔汀**：卡森先生……！\
**Vertin**: Mr. Karson!

**邓肯先生**：我是邓肯，孩子。\
**Mr. Duncan**: It's Duncan, kid.

**邓肯先生**：这不重要，先来看看她——洛佩拉受伤了！\
**Mr. Duncan**: But that's not important. Lopera needs medical attention!

**洛佩拉**：我不要紧。该死的！老爹他……\
**Lopera**: I'm fine. Ugh! Damn you, Igor!

白朗姆不知何时从熟睡中醒来，见到一片狼藉的庭院与受伤的洛佩拉。\
Waking up from her deep slumber, White Rum looks around to see the courtyard in disarray and an injured Lopera.

老先生把洛佩拉放到椅子上，但瓶中船比这儿其他人都更着急。\
As Duncan gently places Lopera on a chair, she races up to her.

**白朗姆**：天哪，我的小宝贝，你怎么闹成这样了……\
**White Rum**: Oh, my darling little buccaneer! Who did this to you?

**维尔汀**：发生什么了……你怎么会……\
**Vertin**: Lopera, could you tell us what happened?

灰尘。血。的确，她的伤势不重——只是擦破表皮，留下了点儿伤口。\
Bloody and dirty, yes, but her injuries aren't serious. She only has a few scrapes and bruises.

但她挂着一张疲惫的脸，眼角还涨得通红。她似乎不久前才哭过。\
However, her eyes are swollen as if she's just been crying.

**洛佩拉**：伊戈尔……该死！他劫走了德洛丝！\
**Lopera**: Igor ... He took Dores!

**维尔汀**：……！\
**Vertin**: ...?!

穿着芝诺军装的人想抢走金伯利。伊戈尔将军又劫持了德洛丝医生。\
First, Zeno soldiers try to take Kimberly; then, Igor orders the kidnapping of Doctor Dores.

**天使娜娜**：你们要去找那个老头吗？\
**Anjo Nala**: So, are you going to go after him?

**维尔汀**：伊戈尔想带走你，你不能和我们一起去。\
**Vertin**: Yes. But you should stay here. Igor still wants you.

绝不能让伊戈尔得逞。\
Igor mustn't succeed.

**维尔汀**：我们会回来的。\
**Vertin**: We'll come back for you later.

**天使娜娜**：好……\
**Anjo Nala**: Okay.

**红弩箭**：现在怎么办，头儿？现在联络基金会也来不及了，附近没人能来支援。\
**Lilya**: What now, then, Captain? There are no Foundation branches nearby. If we request reinforcements, they'll be too slow to arrive.

**维尔汀**：……\
**Vertin**: ...

**维尔汀**：那我们自己去。\
**Vertin**: Then we go ourselves.

**洛佩拉**：我要见他。\
**Lopera**: Count me in. I have to talk to Igor.

**洛佩拉**：……老爹必须给我一个答案。\
**Lopera**: He owes me an answer.

洛佩拉咬着牙。\
Lopera grits her teeth.

**维尔汀**：白朗姆，请带我们去芝诺基地。\
**Vertin**: White Rum, could you take us to the Zeno base?

**白朗姆**：为了救医生，当然！伙计们，起航吧！\
**White Rum**: Anything to save the doc! Anchors aweigh, mateys!

基地里，叛军正在组织最后的撤退工作。\
Back at the Zeno base, the rebels are organizing the final stages of their retreat.

**莫莉德尔**：你把事情办砸了。\
**Moldir**: You screwed up.

**托勒密**：那是个小小的失败。\
**Ptolemy**: It's just a minor setback.

**莫莉德尔**：父亲很不满意。\
**Moldir**: Father isn't happy.

**托勒密**：她是我的猎物！下一次我会——\
**Ptolemy**: Look, I'll deal with her, okay?! Next time, I'll—

独眼军官不得不咽下失败苦果，为他自己的大意。\
His defeat is a consequence of his own arrogance. It's a bitter pill to swallow.

**莫莉德尔**：没有下一次了，我们没法从基金会手里抢人。\
**Moldir**: There won't be a next time. We can't just waltz into the Foundation and take her.

**莫莉德尔**：飞机准备得怎么样了？\
**Moldir**: Anyway, are the aircraft ready?

**托勒密**：一切都好，父亲现在和医生在一起。\
**Ptolemy**: Yeah. Father and the doctor will be boarding soon.

**托勒密**：不过，她到底是谁？\
**Ptolemy**: Who is she, anyway?

**莫莉德尔**：我不知道。\
**Moldir**: I don't know.

她诚实回答，回答自己的一无所知，从不过问太多。\
Her answer is honest. She rarely questions her father.

她的职责是服从，然后执行——顺便贯彻心中那点儿小小的正义感。\
Her duty is to obey and execute—while holding onto a sliver of her own sense of justice.

**托勒密**：我相信你。看来父亲也没有把所有事都告诉你。\
**Ptolemy**: Looks like Father hasn't told you everything either.

**莫莉德尔**：不能让一个人拿着所有的拼图碎片。\
**Moldir**: You should never entrust all the pieces of a puzzle to a single hand.

**托勒密**：你跟在他身边，也变得越来越……充满魅力了。\
**Ptolemy**: Huh, all this time with Father's made you quite enigmatic.

**托勒密**：秘密就是魅力。\
**Ptolemy**: There's a charm in mystery, you know.

一旁，士兵们正忙着搬运物资。烧毁文件的大火在各个房间点燃，用以销毁不宜留下的文字记录。\
Around them, soldiers are busy transporting supplies and burning sensitive documents in fires.

**托勒密**：你不跟我们上直升机吗？\
**Ptolemy**: Are you not coming with us on the helicopter?

**莫莉德尔**：总要有人组织撤退，你和父亲先走吧。\
**Moldir**: Someone has to stay behind and organize the retreat. You go ahead with Father. I'll join you later.

**托勒密**：我有时候真搞不懂你，姐姐。\
**Ptolemy**: Sometimes I just don't understand you, Moldir.

**莫莉德尔**：我也常常搞不明白自己。\
**Moldir**: Oftentimes, I don't understand myself either.

**莫莉德尔**：这或许就是父亲一直把我带在身边的理由。\
**Moldir**: Perhaps that's why Father always keeps me close.

**莫莉德尔**：你和父亲先走，殿后的任务交给我。\
**Moldir**: Just get going. I'll take up the rear.

士兵们正在加紧撤离。副官女士听见了来自其他庭院的枪声。\
The sound of gunfire echoes from outside the courtyard.

但那不重要——同志间的内战也好，基金会的反扑也好，那都不重要。\
But she pays it no mind. Whether it's an internal conflict or a counterattack from the Foundation, it doesn't matter.

**芝诺士兵**：长官！我们遭到攻击！\
**Zeno Soldier**: Ma'am, we're under attack!

**莫莉德尔**：别纠缠，抓紧时间撤离。\
**Moldir**: Don't get entangled with the enemy. Focus on the evacuation.

**莫莉德尔**：几个人？\
**Moldir**: How many hostiles are there?

**芝诺士兵**：三、三个人……还有艘帆船。\
**Zeno Soldier**: Th-Three, and a sailboat.

**托勒密**：帆船？咱们是活在哪个年代呀，哈哈！\
**Ptolemy**: A sailboat? What is this, the Age of Exploration or something? Hahahahaha!

**芝诺士兵**：还有个飞天上的家伙，她太快了……有两个小队正在A2庭院跟她打。\
**Zeno Soldier**: One of them is flying some kind of aircraft. Oh! She's fast. Two squads are currently engaged with her in courtyard A2.

赶上

**洛佩拉**：所以，你们是打算就这样把我丢在圣保罗吗？\
**Lopera**: So, you're just going to leave me here in São Paulo, huh?

两位来自地面的袭击者则突破了防线，冲杀过来。\
Two rebels break through the defense line and rush over to her.

**洛佩拉**：父亲呢！\
**Lopera**: Where's Igor?!

她手染鲜血，枪口被神秘术造物烫得通红。\
Her hands are bloody, the muzzle of her gun singed red from the repeated use of her arcane skill.

她没有找到老将军的身影。等在这儿的，是一位不受欢迎的兄长。\
No sign of the admiral, only the unwelcome sight of her older brother.

**托勒密**：你比我们上次见面的时候又长高了，妹妹。\
**Ptolemy**: You've grown taller since we last met, dear little sister.

独眼军官满怀恶意地向妹妹打招呼。\
There's a hint of malice in his voice.

**托勒密**：无论你愿意跟我们回家，还是跟着那个司辰转身走开，我都不会拦你。\
**Ptolemy**: Woah, woah! Don't look at me like that. I don't care what you do. Come home, or stay with the Timekeeper. I won't stop you.

**洛佩拉**：滚开。\
**Lopera**: Get out of my face.

她举起枪，这一幕似曾相识。\
She raises her rifle.

曾经对准叛徒的枪口，又一次指向了叛徒的心脏。\
This scene looks all too familiar. Time to execute another traitor.

然而，另一个人却拦在了她身前。\
But someone steps in front of her.

**洛佩拉**：姐姐……？\
**Lopera**: Molly?

**维尔汀**：莫莉德尔女士。\
**Vertin**: Ms. Moldir.

**维尔汀**：很遗憾以这种方式再见到你。\
**Vertin**: It's unfortunate that we have to meet again under these circumstances.

**莫莉德尔**：年轻的司辰，我们只是选择了不同的道路。\
**Moldir**: We've simply chosen different paths, Timekeeper.

**莫莉德尔**：下一次见面，或许就在南极了。托勒密，这里交给我，你去父亲那边。\
**Moldir**: I suppose the next time I see you, we'll be in Antarctica. Ptolemy, go join Father. I can handle this.

独眼军官应声离开。\
Her brother turns and leaves.

**洛佩拉**：姐姐……为什么……\
**Lopera**: Molly, why?

尚未撤离的卫队士兵向副官女士聚拢，举起武器。\
The remaining soldiers gather around the lieutenant, their weapons raised.

**莫莉德尔**：很遗憾……你们不能通过这里。\
**Moldir**: Forgive me. I can't let you pass.

口哨

副官女士向所剩无多的卫队发出命令。\
Moldir issues a command to her remaining soldiers.

**莫莉德尔**：士兵们！瞄准！\
**Moldir**: Soldiers, take aim!

战斗结束了。追随副官女士守卫通道的士兵无一生还。洛佩拉在混战中干掉了叛徒。\
The battle ends. Not one of Moldir's soldiers has survived.

她倒在墙边，额头和左肩在流血。面对妹妹的枪口，她无法——或许也不想动弹。\
She falls against the wall, blood oozing from her forehead and shoulder. Faced with her sister's gun, she cannot—or perhaps doesn't want to—move.

她没有像被处刑的囚犯那样闭上眼，而是以一种悲哀的目光看向妹妹的眼睛。\
There's sorrow in her eyes as her gaze meets her sister's.

**洛佩拉**：我再也不想见到你。\
**Lopera**: I don't ever want to see you again.

泪水和弹壳一起落下。

静默\
As the bullet casing falls to the ground, so too does a tear.

我们没能阻止伊戈尔的叛逃。\
We couldn't halt Igor's escape.

撤离中的援军听到枪声，从其他庭院聚集过来，我们不得不离开基地。\
More rebels came at us following the gunfire, and we were forced to flee the base.

我们失败了。\
We failed.

## 8TH-22 西风咆哮 / The Roaring Forties

西风海崖\
背景移动

**？？？**：您做出了正确的选择。\
**???**: You made the right choice.

**伊戈尔将军**：我们都为了祂的指引而来，传道者。\
**Admiral Igor**: We simply followed THEIR guidance, Preacher.

**伊戈尔将军**：很遗憾，那个魅魔没能带过来。\
**Admiral Igor**: Unfortunately, we failed to bring the succubus.

**伊戈尔将军**：但我想，你会需要这个，还有兀尔德女士。\
**Admiral Igor**: But I did bring you this, and Ms. Urd, as well.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：……\
**Sophia the Preacher**: ...

**传道者·苏菲亚**：不，将军，不是“你”，而是……\
**Sophia the Preacher**: No, Admiral. Not you ...

**传道者·苏菲亚**：我们。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: Us.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：我们都需要祂降下的奇迹。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: We all need the miracle THEY bestow.

**伊戈尔将军**：我的部下不会戴上那面具。他们也不会接受试炼。\
**Admiral Igor**: My men will not wear the masks. Nor will they take the trials.

**伊戈尔将军**：不需要用试炼来试探我麾下孩子们的忠诚，传道者。\
**Admiral Igor**: We need no trials to test the loyalty of my children, Preacher.

**伊戈尔将军**：兀尔德女士暂时由我保护。\
**Admiral Igor**: And for now, Ms. Urd will stay under my protection.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：如您所愿。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: As you wish.

传道者对老将军提出的要求一一承应。\
The Preacher agrees to all of the admiral's requests.

无妨，都无妨。\
It doesn't matter. None of it matters.

她远眺南方。\
She looks southward across the sea.

**传道者·苏菲亚**：下次见，将军。\
**Sophia the Preacher**: Until next time, Admiral.

传道者接过复苏之母留在世上的痕迹，与将军道别离开。\
The Preacher takes the relic left by the Mother of Resurrection and bids farewell to the admiral.

收氛围图

**莫莉德尔**：父亲……\
**Moldir**: Father.

**莫莉德尔**：我对洛佩拉开枪了。\
**Moldir**: I shot at Lopera.

开枪是一回事，但子弹射向了心脏还是大地，又是另一回事。但对老将军来说，这都不重要。\
Shooting is one thing. Whether the bullet hits the heart or the ground is another. To the admiral, however, it is unimportant.

**莫莉德尔**：坦白说，对您的选择，至少从个人层面讲，父亲，我并不完全认同。\
**Moldir**: I have to be honest, Father. I don't fully agree with your decision, at least not on a personal level.

**伊戈尔将军**：你可以保留意见，也可以不认同，中尉，我需要的不是这些。\
**Admiral Igor**: You're entitled to your opinion, Lieutenant. But I don't need your approval.

**莫莉德尔**：而是服从。我明白，父亲。\
**Moldir**: I understand. You only need my obedience.

**伊戈尔将军**：没错。\
**Admiral Igor**: Precisely.

**莫莉德尔**：您一开始就认为洛佩拉不会跟我们走吗？\
**Moldir**: Had you anticipated that Lopera wouldn't come with us?

**伊戈尔将军**：那孩子无关紧要。她解决了自己惹出的麻烦，从兄弟会的闹剧里带回了兀尔德，这就够了。\
**Admiral Igor**: She is inconsequential. She helped us retrieve Urd from that Brotherhood farce. That's all I needed from her.

**莫莉德尔**：但兄弟会……恕我直言，将军。\
**Moldir**: But the Brotherhood ... With all due respect, admiral ...

**莫莉德尔**：我听说他们也和重塑之手……的“朋友”有联系。\
**Moldir**: I've heard they have connections with our "friends" at Manus Vindictae.

她很难说服自己改变称呼，将昔日与之对抗的敌人称作“朋友”。\
She finds it hard to call those they once fought against "friends."

变节是难以洗刷的耻辱。\
Treason is a stain not easily washed clean.

**伊戈尔将军**：我原本以为你会和她做出同样的选择。\
**Admiral Igor**: I thought you'd make the same choice she did.

**莫莉德尔**：不，我会追随您，父亲。\
**Moldir**: No, I will always follow you, Father.

**伊戈尔将军**：随她去吧。\
**Admiral Igor**: Just let her be.

落单的海鸟滑过晴空，鸣叫着，朝温暖的北方飞去。\
A lone seagull glides across the sky, calling out as it flies to the warm north.

老将军拍拍女儿肩上的军徽。\
Igor pats his daughter on the shoulder.

**伊戈尔将军**：带德洛丝医生过来。\
**Admiral Igor**: Now, bring me Dr. Dores.

黑幕转场

**莫莉德尔**：父亲。\
**Moldir**: Father.

副官女士带来盲眼医生，随后沉默地离开海崖。\
She dutifully leads the doctor to her father and leaves the two alone.

**德洛丝医生**：我不认识您。您认错人了，将军。\
**Doctor Dores**: I don't know you, sir. You must have mistaken me for someone else.

**伊戈尔将军**：不，我不可能会认错你。\
**Admiral Igor**: No, I couldn't possibly mistake you.

**伊戈尔将军**：老朋友。\
**Admiral Igor**: Old friend.

**伊戈尔将军**：在千禧年到来前的最后那几天，我们曾并肩作战。\
**Admiral Igor**: In the last days before the millennium, we fought side by side.

往事从老人锈迹斑斑的记忆殿堂里涌出。\
Memories flood the weathered halls of the old admiral's mind.

**伊戈尔将军**：长远来看，那或许是一次错误的行动。\
**Admiral Igor**: In hindsight, that battle may have been a mistake.

**伊戈尔将军**：“暴雨”到来，留下混乱的时代与失去父亲的孤儿们。\
**Admiral Igor**: The "Storm" swept across the world, leaving behind an era of chaos.

**伊戈尔将军**：我们失去了未来。\
**Admiral Igor**: And we lost our future.

将军从不为牺牲动容，因为一切乃是为了胜利与更宏大的目标所必不可少的。\
The admiral has never been fearful of sacrifice, especially when it has served the grander goal.

**伊戈尔将军**：但现在，或许可以走上另一条路，一条我们曾经拼尽一切反对的道路。\
**Admiral Igor**: But now, another path lies before us, one that we once fought desperately against.

**伊戈尔将军**：阿尔卡纳指引的道路——\
**Admiral Igor**: A path paved by Arcana.

**伊戈尔将军**：一条，让世界不再有纷争的道路。\
**Admiral Igor**: A path leading to a world free of conflict.

**伊戈尔将军**：我的老朋友。\
**Admiral Igor**: My old friend.

很遗憾，这些话语中的哪怕是支离破碎的半点信息她都无法理解。\
Sadly, she cannot comprehend even a fragment of these words.

她只是无国界医生德洛丝。\
She's simply Doctor Dores. Nothing more.

**伊戈尔将军**：基金会送给你的那张白色大理石凳上有什么秘密？\
**Admiral Igor**: That marble chair the Foundation gave you ... What's the secret behind it?

**伊戈尔将军**：那个按钮按下后，你又感受到了什么？\
**Admiral Igor**: What happened to you after you pressed that button?

**德洛丝医生**：什么也没有。\
**Doctor Dores**: Nothing.

**伊戈尔将军**：你还记得，曾经走进一间白色房子后发生的事情吗？\
**Admiral Igor**: Do you remember what happened after you walked into that white house?

**德洛丝医生**：抱歉，将军，我对此一无所知。\
**Doctor Dores**: I'm sorry. I don't know anything about that.

她有些倔强，但却愿意以诚实回应老将军的诚实。\
She's stubborn but answers honestly.

老将军叹了口气，随即抽出大衣里的一叠杂志——尽管他本人并非《UTTU》的读者，也对此毫无兴趣。\
The old admiral sighs and pulls a stack of UTTU magazines from his coat. They were not for his own reading.

**伊戈尔将军**：敬爱的兀尔德女士。\
**Admiral Igor**: My dear Ms. Urd.

**伊戈尔将军**：你的名字穿过了一场又一场雨幕。\
**Admiral Igor**: Your name continues to show up between the occurrences of the "Storm."

**伊戈尔将军**：但我始终不知道你究竟遇到了什么，又经历过什么。\
**Admiral Igor**: I don't know what you've encountered, what you've experienced, in all this time.

**伊戈尔将军**：——但你的存在，即将改变我们所有人的命运。\
**Admiral Igor**: But your very existence is about to change the fate of us all.

## 8TH-23 谢幕演出 / The Final Curtain

基金会客房

**苏芙比**：居然有这——么多的人生活在河上！\
**Sotheby**: Hehe! I never knew that so many people lived on the river!

**苏芙比**：他们捡起塑料瓶，像绑着气球鱼一样，绑上木板，居然就可以过河啦！\
**Sotheby**: I saw them tie plastic bottles to planks to make a bridge, and then they crossed the river as if they were walking on a row of puffpuff fish!

涉世未深的大小姐很少有这样的机会，亲身接触挣扎在饥饿边缘的生活。\
Sotheby's sheltered life has given her few chances to witness the struggles of those on the verge of hunger.

但自她从水中苏醒，心中的那个疑惑就久久没能散去。\
But ever since she came to consciousness on the water's edge, that same question has lingered in her heart.

**苏芙比**：……\
**Sotheby**: ...

只是这次她没再提出那个被嚼烂了的疑问。\
She restrains herself from voicing it.

贫民区的很多人都认识邓肯，所有人都在告诉她：是呀，那老家伙就是荣军院的邓肯！仿佛只有自己，还在做着昨日世界的旧梦。\
Duncan's well known in the favela, and everyone keeps telling her, "Yes, that old man is Duncan from the Veterans' Residence!" It's like she's trapped in some kind of dream.

**邓肯先生**：小淑女，我知道你在想些什么……\
**Mr. Duncan**: I know what you're thinking, little lady.

**邓肯先生**：邓肯就是邓肯，我的证件，我的从军履历和军功章，都能证明我是邓肯。\
**Mr. Duncan**: But I am Duncan. My ID card, my military record, my medals—they all prove it.

**邓肯先生**：而您那位叫卡森先生的朋友……孩子，我知道这很难过，但我们总要从回忆中走出来。\
**Mr. Duncan**: As for your friend, Mr. Karson, listen, I know it's hard, but at some point, we have to move on.

**苏芙比**：……谢谢你，只是……\
**Sotheby**: Thank you for the advice; it's just ...

敲门声

**基金会职员**：冒昧打扰——\
**Foundation Staff Member**: Pardon me.

开门声

基金会的职员小姐轻轻推开房门。\
The Foundation staff member gently pushes open the door.

**苏芙比**：咦？\
**Sotheby**: Hm?

**基金会职员**：苏芙比小姐，很抱歉打扰您和邓肯先生的会面。\
**Foundation Staff Member**: My apologies for interrupting.

**基金会职员**：我听说了您在贫民区的冒险，真是非常了不起。多亏了您的坚持，芝诺才得以获得一批充满热情的年轻人。\
**Foundation Staff Member**: Ms. Sotheby, I heard about what happened in the favela. Thanks to your efforts, Zeno has been able to recruit a new group of spirited youths.

职员小姐转向邓肯先生。\
The staff member then turns to Mr. Duncan.

小淑女得意地点点头——她不是可爱的小衣架，在大伙儿都忙于任务时，她也尽力帮助着贫民区的朋友。\
Sotheby gives a proud nod. She's more than just a pretty dress. She did her very best to help her friends in the favela while the others were busy with their missions.

**基金会职员**：您的相关信息我们会登记在案，以比对牺牲于1929年“暴雨”的卡森先生。\
**Foundation Staff Member**: Mr. Duncan, we need to record your information and cross-reference it with that of Mr. Karson, who was lost during the "Storm" of 1929.

**苏芙比**：这真是不可思议……为什么会出现另一个卡森先生呢？\
**Sotheby**: It's bewildering, isn't it? How could there be another Mr. Karson?

**邓肯先生**：1929年？\
**Mr. Duncan**: 1929?

一个充斥着梦想、疯狂与野心的黄金年代。\
A fervent era filled with ambition, dreams, and madness.

**基金会职员**：请吧，邓肯先生，这不会花您太多时间，之后您还有芝诺军备学院的再入伍手续要办理。\
**Foundation Staff Member**: Please come with me, Mr. Duncan. It won't take long. After that, you'll need to initiate the procedures for your re-enlistment in the Zeno Arms Academy.

**基金会职员**：欢迎您回归我们的事业。在这之前，康复中心会负责处理您在圣保罗战斗中受的伤。\
**Foundation Staff Member**: While the said procedures are underway, the rehab center will take care of the injuries you sustained in São Paulo. Welcome back to our cause.

消人\
基金会走廊

**基金会职员**：还有很多类似案例。\
**Foundation Staff Member**: There have been many cases like yours.

**基金会职员**：政要、歌手……基金会比对了九十年代的照片，发现很多人都变成了不同的模样。\
**Foundation Staff Member**: Politicians, singers, the list goes on. The Foundation compared them to photos from the '90s. While their appearances had changed, they were undoubtedly the same person.

职员小姐的话都让老邓肯感到莫名其妙。\
These words leave Duncan feeling puzzled.

陌生的土地、陌生的语言和陌生的新朋友。\
This place is strange, and their language is even stranger.

**邓肯先生**：嗨！中尉！\
**Mr. Duncan**: Heh, hey! Isn't that Lieutenant Lilya?

走到中途，恰好遇见迎面而来的两位朋友。\
Lilya is sauntering down the hallway, swigging on her flask.

**基金会职员**：红弩箭中尉，按照相关章程，我认为这里……应该是禁酒区域。\
**Foundation Staff Member**: This is an alcohol-free zone, Lieutenant Lilya. Please try to follow the regulations.

**红弩箭**：噢，禁酒区域，我都快忘了……\
**Lilya**: Oh, did I just wander into another dry zone? Great.

**红弩箭**：我们总是有那么多的规矩。\
**Lilya**: So many rules and regulations. Ugh, how boring!

**邓肯先生**：洛佩拉也回来了吗？\
**Mr. Duncan**: Has Lopera arrived?

**红弩箭**：回房间了，她状况不太好……接受审讯前，维尔汀给她争取了一些休息时间。\
**Lilya**: She's in her room right now. Vertin managed to secure her some rest time before her interrogation. Poor girl.

**红弩箭**：说真的，这种事情谁遇到都会难受。\
**Lilya**: Honestly, no one deserves to go through what she has.

**红弩箭**：至少比关在屋子里签字写报告难受多了。\
**Lilya**: It's even worse than being cooped up and buried in paperwork.

**基金会职员**：红弩箭中尉，那也是……必要的记录。\
**Foundation Staff Member**: Ahem, clerical work is essential, too.

职员小姐苦笑着，对方当面讽刺着她的工作，令她有些尴尬。\
She gives an awkward smile at this mockery of her work.

红弩箭爽朗地拍了拍她的肩膀，又回过身来望向邓肯。\
Lilya cheerfully pats her on the shoulder and turns back to Duncan.

**红弩箭**：祝你好运，邓肯同志，祝你不会签字签到手酸。\
**Lilya**: Well, good luck, Comrade Duncan. Don't forget to stretch your hand between signing papers.

她宁愿骑红色38骑到双腿发麻，也不愿意在办公室里坐牢。\
She'd rather ride her Red 38 until her legs went numb than be stuck in an office all day.

**基金会职员**：按照流程，接下来您应该也需要提供调查报告。\
**Foundation Staff Member**: You also need to write a report, Lieutenant Lilya.

**基金会职员**：高层很好奇你是怎么从叛军的关押中逃出来了。\
**Foundation Staff Member**: Our executives are quite curious to know how you managed to escape the rebels' custody.

**红弩箭**：莫莉德尔让人来放了我，就基地里那个管事的女人。\
**Lilya**: Moldir, the woman in charge of the base, had one of her guards release me.

副官女士留下的嘱托救了飞行员一命。\
Moldir's orders saved Lilya's life.

**基金会职员**：是叛军里的莫莉德尔中尉放了您吗？\
**Foundation Staff Member**: You mean to say that Moldir, the lieutenant who's joined the rebellion, set you free?

**红弩箭**：我认为是这么回事，至少放我的人是这么跟我说的。\
**Lilya**: I think so. At least, that's what the guard told me.

“是中尉让我来帮您的，祝您……顺利……”\
"Lieutenant Moldir asked me to help you. Take care—"

消回忆

**基金会职员**：……我们会记录在案，当然，希望您在正式报告中也提及这件事。\
**Foundation Staff Member**: I'll be sure to make note of that. And of course, please specify this in your written report as well.

**基金会职员**：这件事非常重要，中尉。\
**Foundation Staff Member**: This is very important, Lieutenant.

**基金会职员**：也许我们还能把伊戈尔的叛军争取回来。\
**Foundation Staff Member**: If she's having doubts, then we may still have a chance to win back Igor's rebels.

**基金会职员**：至少……争取叛军的一部分。\
**Foundation Staff Member**: Or at least some of them.

基金会高层办公室

副会长久违地向鸽子屋发起联络。\
Vice President Constantine makes a long-overdue call with the Pax House.

**康斯坦丁**：……\
**Constantine**: ...

**康斯坦丁**：伊戈尔把所有人都骗进了他的谋乱中。\
**Constantine**: Igor fooled us all with his rebellion.

**康斯坦丁**：可以确认他劫走的“德洛丝医生”就是兀尔德女士。\
**Constantine**: It's been confirmed that the Dr. Dores he took is none other than Ms. Urd.

**康斯坦丁**：目前尚不清楚伊戈尔这一行为的动机。\
**Constantine**: The motives behind his actions, however, are still unclear.

**康斯坦丁**：随他叛乱的只是极小部分芝诺军人，但我判断，有必要督促芝诺军备学院加强内部整顿。\
**Constantine**: While only a small number of the Zeno soldiers chose to join his rebellion, I believe it is necessary to urge the Zeno Arms Academy to strengthen the discipline of their members.

副会长拿掉棋盘上的一枚白色棋子。\
She removes a white chess piece from the board in front of her.

**会长**：别担心，芝诺会自行处理。\
**President**: No need to worry about that. Zeno will handle it themselves.

**康斯坦丁**：……如果您是这么认为的话，我没有疑义。\
**Constantine**: If that's your judgment, then I have no objections.

**康斯坦丁**：对了，我们留在重塑之手的飞蛾传回了新情报。\
**Constantine**: On a separate note, Moth, our mole planted within Manus Vindictae, has sent us some new information.

**康斯坦丁**：大量物资、人员和军事力量都在向南方靠拢，间谍情报也佐证了此前基金会部分人员的猜想：重塑之手正在筹备下一次“暴雨”仪式——一次新的仪式。\
**Constantine**: The Manus are sending supplies, personnel, and weapons in huge numbers to the south. It appears our suspicions were correct. Manus Vindictae is preparing a ritual to draw forth another "Storm."

**会长**：……\
**President**: ...

**康斯坦丁**：而基于露西女士提供的杰瑞·威尔逊的位置信息，可以佐证重塑之手正在往南极移动的消息。\
**Constantine**: The location of Jerry Wilson provided by Ms. Lucy confirms that the Manus are moving toward Antarctica.

**康斯坦丁**：此外，包括天使兄弟会在内的一部分神秘学家组织，正通过走私和人口贩卖等犯罪活动，为重塑之手提供外围协助。\
**Constantine**: Additionally, it's now clear that some of the arcanist organizations, including the Apostles Brotherhood, have been assisting the Manus through criminal activities such as smuggling and human trafficking.

棋盘上，黑色士兵向前进军。\
She advances the black pawn on the chessboard.

**会长**：都是很有价值的消息。司辰情况还好吗？\
**President**: All very valuable information. How's the Timekeeper doing?

**康斯坦丁**：情绪稳定，但她从重塑之手方面带回了一名魅魔。\
**Constantine**: She's stable. It's worth noting, however, that she brought back a succubus from the Manus.

**康斯坦丁**：司辰要求撤销对这名魅魔的通缉，并依据《暴雨改革：秩序与增员》法案，赋予她其他隶属于司辰小队的神秘学家享有的一切权益。\
**Constantine**: She requested that we revoke the arrest warrant for the succubus and grant her all the rights enjoyed by Team Timekeeper in accordance with The Storm Reformation: Manpower and Discipline Act.

**康斯坦丁**：我答应了司辰的请求。\
**Constantine**: I've consented to her request.

**会长**：嗯，这样很好，她是合适的负责人。\
**President**: Excellent. She's the ideal person to keep watch over the succubus.

**康斯坦丁**：明白。\
**Constantine**: Very good, sir.

**会长**：另外，关于伊戈尔……\
**President**: About Igor ...

**会长**：“已故芝诺军备学院上将伊戈尔”会在芝诺总部的纪功廊得到他应得的荣誉。\
**President**: The "late Admiral Igor of the Zeno Arms Academy" will be duly honored in the headquarters' Hall of Merit.

**会长**：他在服役期间的功勋值得被历史铭记。\
**President**: His great achievements and remarkable service deserve to be remembered.

**会长**：就到这里吧。\
**President**: That's all for now.

挂断电话\
插图

老将军的叛离为乐观的九十年代蒙上了一层难以抹除的不祥的阴影。\
The admiral's betrayal has already cast a lasting shadow over the optimistic '90s.

而昔日敌人在失去首脑后竟然没有作鸟兽散，反而向南方聚集力量，试图重振旗鼓的消息则更令她忧心。\
But the news that, even after losing their leader, the Manus are gathering once again is even more worrying.

**康斯坦丁**：维尔汀……\
**Constantine**: Vertin ...

客房

**维尔汀**：伦敦、利马、乌斯怀亚……\
**Vertin**: London, Lima, Ushuaia ...

基金会收到的报告中，大量提及与邓肯先生情况相似的事件。\
The Foundation's reports detail many cases like Duncan's.

一张张熟悉的脸变成了另一个人。\
One familiar face after another turned into someone else.

“暴雨”将众人带回熟悉而充满希望的九十年代。时代光明灿烂，如同日头照临高天之中。\
The "Storm" has brought everyone with it to the bright and hopeful '90s.

**维尔汀**：“来自哥伦比亚的报告：巴勃罗·埃米利奥·埃斯科瓦尔·加维里亚的入狱像与收藏于档案室中的相关记录无法匹配，其余知名人士也出现了相关异状。”\
**Vertin**: "A report from Colombia: The mugshots of Pablo Emilio Escobar Gaviria do not match those archived. Similar anomalies have appeared for other notable figures."

类似的案例还有很多。\
There are many such cases.

但眼下最大的麻烦是伊戈尔的行动。\
But the most pressing issue now is Igor's actions.

**维尔汀**：伊戈尔为什么要劫持兀尔德？\
**Vertin**: Why did Igor abduct Ms. Urd?

**维尔汀**：他为什么要带走金伯利？\
**Vertin**: And why does he want Kimberly?

一个疑问牵出另一个疑问，答案蛇行在沙土之下，无法捕捉。\
One question leads to another, but the answers remain a mystery.

**维尔汀**：伊戈尔他们要去哪里？为什么叛乱？\
**Vertin**: And where are Igor and his army going? Why did they defect?

问题和线索交织在一起，一片混沌。\
It's a maze of questions and clues.

这里既没有能飞离高墙的蜡制的翅膀，也不存在一个指引出口的线团。\
And there is no waxwing to peer over its walls, and no thread to guide the way out.

**维尔汀**：被1929年的“暴雨”回溯掉的卡森先生，又突然出现在了1990年。\
**Vertin**: Mr. Karson, who was reversed by the "Storm" of 1929, has somehow reappeared in 1990.

如同陷入迷宫的旅人，在命运筑起的高墙中，既没有先知讲道架梯的天才，也没有诸神那般高大的身姿足以俯瞰迷宫之全貌。\
If only there were some way to look beyond the towering walls of this maze and see things for what they truly are.

**维尔汀**：不，也许不是这样……\
**Vertin**: Or maybe there's more to it.

落水之人未必被河流吞没，也许只是被冲往了另一片河滩。\
A person pulled under by the river isn't always swallowed. They often wash up on another shore.

可能性，更多的可能性。乌鸦聚集，驱赶白鸽，枯干朽坏的喷泉旁，群鸦啄食着雨水。\
Possibilities. More possibilities. Crows gather and drive away the doves, and by the dry, decaying fountain, they peck at the rainwater.

**维尔汀**：也许……\
**Vertin**: Could it be that ...

这是一个大胆的猜测。\
She makes a bold guess.

**维尔汀**：——暴雨并不会导致生理意义上的死亡？\
**Vertin**: The "Storm" doesn't kill people? At least, not physically?

## 8TH-24 独角戏 / Monologues

她捡起枪，捡起子弹，一一填入弹巢。\
Lopera picks up her gun and loads the bullets one by one.

**洛佩拉**：一，二，三。\
**Lopera**: One, two, three.

这儿没有敌人，没有目标，也没有对手。\
There are no enemies, no targets, no opponents.

她从没有如此茫然地举起过枪。\
She has never raised her gun so aimlessly before.

如同置身荒原的猎人，她无处可去，也无家可归。\
She's lost. Like a hunter in the wilderness with no place to go and no home to return to.

**洛佩拉**：中靶。\
**Lopera**: Shots on target.

三颗子弹，留下标靶上的一个孔洞。\
Three bullets are shot, but they leave only one hole.

**洛佩拉**：一，二，三。\
**Lopera**: One, two, three.

消人\
Empty shells fall. Bullets are reloaded.

弹壳退下，子弹装填。

**洛佩拉**：一，二，三。\
**Lopera**: One, two, three.

客房

枪声

**洛佩拉**：……\
**Lopera**: ...

一个“千疮百孔”的房间。\
The room is riddled with bullet holes.

一位手指麻木的少女，机械性地扣动扳机。\
Lopera is numb. She mechanically pulls the trigger.

枪管没有反应。\
The gun doesn't respond.

**洛佩拉**：黑屏\
**Lopera**: Lies.

**洛佩拉**：谎言。\
**Lopera**: Deception.

**洛佩拉**：欺瞒。\
**Lopera**: Betrayal.

**洛佩拉**：背叛。

她松开手，左轮枪落到脚边。\
She loosens her grip, and the revolver falls to the floor.

**洛佩拉**：从一开始你们就把我支走，对吗？\
**Lopera**: You planned to kick me out right from the very beginning, didn't you?

一个没有将她纳入谋划的谋划。\
A plan that never included her.

**洛佩拉**：还是说，从一开始你们就没有相信过我。\
**Lopera**: Or did you never even trust me in the first place?

**洛佩拉**：这只是一场过家家吗，姐姐？\
**Lopera**: Was this all some kind of game to you, Molly?

客房\
She's lost, lost and alone. Nothing but herself and the hollow sound of the wind blowing through the window.

“猎人”丢下枪，看着眼前没有边际的旷野。这儿只有风，吹过无花果树的风。

她靠上墙壁，抱紧自己。\
She drops to the floor and curls up against the wall.

**洛佩拉**：为什么……\
**Lopera**: Why?!

**天使娜娜**：同一个岔口。\
**Anjo Nala**: At the same crossroad

**天使娜娜**：暖阳变寒冷。\
**Anjo Nala**: When the warm days grow cold

**天使娜娜**：树叶垂落，一个吻。\
**Anjo Nala**: Leaves are falling down to the ground

**天使娜娜**：烈火无法。\
**Anjo Nala**: Fire can't burn down

**天使娜娜**：将过去化为尘埃。\
**Anjo Nala**: My past into ashes

**天使娜娜**：直到现在。\
**Anjo Nala**: By now

**天使娜娜**：在忧郁的热带，我们道别。\
**Anjo Nala**: In the melancholy tropic we say goodbye

**天使娜娜**：我望着你眼中低语。\
**Anjo Nala**: I see whispers in your eyes

**天使娜娜**：在忧郁的热带，我们吻别。\
**Anjo Nala**: In the melancholy tropic we kiss goodbye

**天使娜娜**：而你将与他人相遇。\
**Anjo Nala**: You will find someone in your life

**天使娜娜**：而你将与一生所爱相遇。\
**Anjo Nala**: You will find the love of your life
